From $P(y|x)$ to $P(y)$: Investigating Reinforcement Learning in Pre-train Space
Authors: Yuqiao Tan, Minzheng Wang, Bo Liu, Zichen Liu, Tian Liang, Shizhu He, Jun Zhao, Kang Liu
First: 2026-04-15T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:59:01+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Our code is available at https://github.com/Trae1ounG/Pretrain_Space_RLVR
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) significantly enhances LLM reasoning by optimizing the conditional distribution P(y|x), its potential is fundamentally bounded by the base model's existing output distribution. Optimizing the marginal distribution P(y) in the Pre-train Space addresses this bottleneck by encoding reasoning ability and preserving broad exploration capacity. Yet, conventional pre-training relies on static corpora for passive learning, leading to a distribution shift that hinders targeted reasoning enhancement. In this paper, we introduce PreRL (Pre-train Space RL), which applies reward-driven online updates directly to P(y). We theoretically and empirically validate the strong gradient alignment between log P(y) and log P(y|x), establishing PreRL as a viable surrogate for standard RL. Furthermore, we uncover a critical mechanism: Negative Sample Reinforcement (NSR) within PreRL serves as an exceptionally effective driver for reasoning. NSR-PreRL rapidly prunes incorrect reasoning spaces while stimulating endogenous reflective behaviors, increasing transition and reflection thoughts by 14.89x and 6.54x, respectively. Leveraging these insights, we propose Dual Space RL (DSRL), a Policy Reincarnation strategy that initializes models with NSR-PreRL to expand the reasoning horizon before transitioning to standard RL for fine-grained optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DSRL consistently outperforms strong baselines, proving that pre-train space pruning effectively steers the policy toward a refined correct reasoning subspace.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从$P(y|x)$到$P(y)$：探索预训练空间中的强化学习
尽管带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通过优化条件分布P(y|x)显著提升了大型语言模型的推理能力，但其潜力从根本上受限于基础模型现有的输出分布。在预训练空间中优化边缘分布P(y)通过编码推理能力并保持广泛探索容量，解决了这一瓶颈。然而，传统预训练依赖静态语料进行被动学习，导致分布偏移，阻碍了针对性推理增强。本文提出预训练空间强化学习（PreRL），将奖励驱动的在线更新直接应用于P(y)。我们从理论和实证上验证了log P(y)与log P(y|x)之间的强梯度对齐，确立PreRL作为标准RL的可行替代方案。进一步，我们揭示了一个关键机制：PreRL中的负样本强化（NSR）是推理能力的极高效驱动力。NSR-PreRL能快速剪除错误推理空间，同时激发内源性反思行为，使转换思维和反思思维分别提升14.89倍和6.54倍。基于这些发现，我们提出双空间强化学习（DSRL）——一种策略重生策略：先用NSR-PreRL初始化模型以拓展推理边界，再转换至标准RL进行细粒度优化。大量实验表明DSRL持续超越强基线，证明预训练空间剪枝能有效引导策略进入精炼的正确推理子空间。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a limitation in standard reinforcement learning for language models, where optimizing the conditional distribution P(y|x) is constrained by the model's existing output distribution. The authors propose PreRL, a method that instead optimizes the marginal distribution P(y) in the pre-train space to enhance reasoning ability while maintaining exploration capacity. They theoretically and empirically show gradient alignment between log P(y) and log P(y|x), and identify Negative Sample Reinforcement (NSR) within PreRL as a key mechanism that prunes incorrect reasoning and boosts reflective thoughts, increasing transition and reflection thoughts by 14.89x and 6.54x, respectively. Building on this, they introduce Dual Space RL, which initializes models with NSR-PreRL for broad reasoning expansion before fine-tuning with standard RL, leading to consistent performance improvements over baselines in experiments.
本文针对语言模型标准强化学习的局限性提出改进，其中优化条件分布P(y|x)受限于模型现有输出分布。作者提出PreRL方法，在预训练空间中优化边际分布P(y)，以增强推理能力同时保持探索容量。他们从理论和实验上验证了log P(y)与log P(y|x)的梯度对齐，并发现PreRL中的负样本强化机制能有效修剪错误推理空间并激发内生反思行为，使转换和反思思维分别提升14.89倍和6.54倍。基于此，他们提出双空间强化学习策略，先用NSR-PreRL初始化模型以扩展推理范围，再转入标准强化学习进行细粒度优化，实验表明该方法持续优于基线模型。
Hierarchical DLO Routing with Reinforcement Learning and In-Context Vision-language Models
Authors: Mingen Li, Houjian Yu, Yixuan Huang, Youngjin Hong, Hantao Ye, Changhyun Choi
First: 2025-10-22T05:57:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:36:28+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Long-horizon routing tasks of deformable linear objects (DLOs), such as cables and ropes, are common in industrial assembly lines and everyday life. These tasks are particularly challenging because they require robots to manipulate DLO with long-horizon planning and reliable skill execution. Successfully completing such tasks demands adapting to their nonlinear dynamics, decomposing abstract routing goals, and generating multi-step plans composed of multiple skills, all of which require accurate high-level reasoning during execution. In this paper, we propose a fully autonomous hierarchical framework for solving challenging DLO routing tasks. Given an implicit or explicit routing goal expressed in language, our framework leverages vision-language models~(VLMs) for in-context high-level reasoning to synthesize feasible plans, which are then executed by low-level skills trained via reinforcement learning. To improve robustness over long horizons, we further introduce a failure recovery mechanism that reorients the DLO into insertion-feasible states. Our approach generalizes to diverse scenes involving object attributes, spatial descriptions, implicit language commands, and \myred{extended 5-clip settings}. It achieves an overall success rate of 92\% across long-horizon routing scenarios. Please refer to our project page: https://icra2026-dloroute.github.io/DLORoute/
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习与上下文视觉语言模型的分层可变形线性物体路径规划
可变形线性物体（如电缆、绳索）的长时程路径规划任务在工业装配线和日常生活中十分常见。这类任务极具挑战性，要求机器人通过长时程规划与可靠技能执行来操控物体，需适应其非线性动力学特性、分解抽象路径目标，并生成由多技能构成的多步计划，执行过程均依赖精确的高层推理。本文提出一种全自主分层框架以解决复杂的DLO路径规划任务。给定语言描述的隐式或显式路径目标，本框架利用上下文视觉语言模型进行高层推理以合成可行计划，再通过强化学习训练的低层技能执行。为提升长时程任务的鲁棒性，我们进一步引入故障恢复机制，将DLO重新调整至可插入状态。该方法可泛化至涉及物体属性、空间描述、隐式语言指令及\myred{扩展五夹爪场景}的多样化场景，在长时程路径规划中总体成功率高达92%。详见项目页面：https://icra2026-dloroute.github.io/DLORoute/
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of long-horizon routing tasks for deformable linear objects (DLOs) like cables, which require complex planning and execution due to nonlinear dynamics. The authors propose a hierarchical framework that uses in-context vision-language models for high-level reasoning to synthesize plans from language goals, and employs reinforcement learning-trained low-level skills for execution, enhanced by a failure recovery mechanism for robustness. Experimental results demonstrate the method's generalization across diverse scenes and attributes, achieving a 92% success rate in long-horizon routing scenarios.
本文针对电缆等可变形线性物体的长时程布线任务挑战，该任务因非线性动力学而需要复杂的规划和执行。作者提出了一种分层框架，利用上下文视觉语言模型进行高层推理，从语言目标合成计划，并采用强化学习训练的低层技能进行执行，同时通过故障恢复机制增强鲁棒性。实验结果表明，该方法在不同场景和属性中具有良好泛化能力，在长时程布线场景中实现了92%的整体成功率。
Deep Neural Network-guided PSO for Tracking a Global Optimal Position in Complex Dynamic Environment
Authors: Stephen Raharja, Toshiharu Sugawara
First: 2026-04-15T16:38:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:38:03+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures, 5 tables. Accepted at ISMSI 2026 (10th International Conference on Intelligent Systems, Metaheuristics & Swarm Intelligence ), Cebu, Philippines, April 24-26, 2026. To appear in the ACM International Conference Proceedings Series
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose novel particle swarm optimization (PSO) variants incorporated with deep neural networks (DNNs) for particles to pursue globally optimal positions in dynamic environments. PSO is a heuristic approach for solving complex optimization problems. However, canonical PSO and its variants struggle to adapt efficiently to dynamic environments, in which the global optimum moves over time, and to track them accurately. Many PSO algorithms improve convergence by increasing the swarm size beyond potential optima, which are global/local optima but are not identified until they are discovered. Additionally, in dynamic environments, several methods use multiple sub-population and re-diversification mechanisms to address outdated memory and local optima entrapment. To track the global optimum in dynamic environments with smaller swarm sizes, the DNNs in our methods determine particle movement by learning environmental characteristics and adapting dynamics to pursue moving optimal positions. This enables particles to adapt to environmental changes and predict the moving optima. We propose two variants: a swarm with a centralized network and distributed networks for all particles. Our experimental results show that both variants can track moving potential optima with lower cumulative tracking error than those of several recent PSO-based algorithms, with fewer particles than potential optima.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度神经网络引导的粒子群优化算法在复杂动态环境中追踪全局最优位置
本文提出融合深度神经网络的新型粒子群优化算法变体，使粒子能在动态环境中追踪全局最优位置。粒子群优化是一种解决复杂优化问题的启发式方法，但经典算法及其变体难以高效适应动态环境（全局最优值随时间移动）并实现精准追踪。现有方法常通过扩大种群规模超越潜在最优值（即未被发现前的全局/局部最优）来提升收敛性，或在动态环境中采用多子群与再多样化机制应对记忆过时和局部最优陷阱。为以较小种群规模追踪动态环境中的全局最优，本方法通过深度神经网络学习环境特征、调整动态策略以追踪移动最优值，使粒子能适应环境变化并预测移动最优值。我们提出两种变体：集中式网络架构与分布式粒子网络架构。实验表明，两种变体均能以少于潜在最优值数量的粒子，实现比近期多种粒子群优化算法更低的累积追踪误差。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of canonical particle swarm optimization (PSO) algorithms in efficiently tracking moving global optima in dynamic environments, this paper proposes novel PSO variants that integrate deep neural networks (DNNs) to guide particle movement. The method involves using DNNs, implemented either as a centralized network for the swarm or distributed networks for individual particles, to learn environmental characteristics and adapt dynamics, enabling particles to predict and pursue shifting optimal positions with smaller swarm sizes. Experimental results demonstrate that both proposed variants achieve lower cumulative tracking error compared to several recent PSO-based algorithms while using fewer particles than the number of potential optima.
针对传统粒子群优化算法在动态环境中难以有效追踪移动全局最优解的问题，本文提出了融合深度神经网络的新型粒子群优化变体。该方法通过使用集中式或分布式深度神经网络来学习环境特征并适应动态变化，从而引导粒子运动，使其能够以较小的种群规模预测和追踪移动的最优位置。实验结果表明，与多种近期基于粒子群优化的算法相比，所提出的两种变体在粒子数少于潜在最优解数量的情况下，实现了更低的累积跟踪误差。
A Comparative Study of Dynamic Programming and Reinforcement Learning in Finite Horizon Dynamic Pricing
Authors: Lev Razumovskiy, Nikolay Karenin
First: 2026-04-15T16:36:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:36:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper provides a systematic comparison between Fitted Dynamic Programming (DP), where demand is estimated from data, and Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods in finite-horizon dynamic pricing problems. We analyze their performance across environments of increasing structural complexity, ranging from a single typology benchmark to multi-typology settings with heterogeneous demand and inter-temporal revenue constraints. Unlike simplified comparisons that restrict DP to low-dimensional settings, we apply dynamic programming in richer, multi-dimensional environments with multiple product types and constraints. We evaluate revenue performance, stability, constraint satisfaction behavior, and computational scaling, highlighting the trade-offs between explicit expectation-based optimization and trajectory-based learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有限时域动态定价中动态规划与强化学习的比较研究
本文系统比较了基于数据估计需求的拟合动态规划与强化学习方法在有限时域动态定价问题中的应用。我们分析了它们在结构复杂度递增环境中的性能，从单一类型基准到具有异质需求和跨期收益约束的多类型场景。与将动态规划局限于低维环境的简化比较不同，我们在包含多产品类型和约束的更丰富多维环境中应用动态规划。我们评估了收益表现、稳定性、约束满足行为及计算扩展性，揭示了基于显式期望的优化与基于轨迹的学习之间的权衡关系。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to systematically compare model-based and model-free approaches in complex pricing environments, this paper conducts a comparative study of Fitted Dynamic Programming (DP) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) for finite-horizon dynamic pricing. The method involves applying both approaches across environments of increasing structural complexity, from a single benchmark to multi-typology settings with heterogeneous demand and inter-temporal constraints, without restricting DP to low-dimensional cases. The main experimental results reveal trade-offs in revenue performance, stability, constraint satisfaction, and computational scaling, highlighting the contrast between DP's explicit expectation-based optimization and RL's trajectory-based learning.
本文旨在系统比较基于模型和无模型方法在复杂定价环境中的表现，对有限时域动态定价中的拟合动态规划（DP）和强化学习（RL）进行了对比研究。研究方法是在结构复杂性递增的环境中应用两种方法，从单一基准到具有异质性需求和跨期收入约束的多类型场景，且未将DP局限于低维设置。主要实验结果表明，两种方法在收益性能、稳定性、约束满足行为和计算扩展性上存在权衡，凸显了DP基于显式期望的优化与RL基于轨迹的学习之间的差异。
Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Runtime Safety Shielding for Power Grid Operation
Authors: Gitesh Malik
First: 2026-04-15T16:11:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:11:10+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has shown promise for automating power-grid operation tasks such as topology control and congestion management. However, its deployment in real-world power systems remains limited by strict safety requirements, brittleness under rare disturbances, and poor generalization to unseen grid topologies. In safety-critical infrastructure, catastrophic failures cannot be tolerated, and learning-based controllers must operate within hard physical constraints. This paper proposes a safety-constrained hierarchical control framework for power-grid operation that explicitly decouples long-horizon decision-making from real-time feasibility enforcement. A high-level reinforcement learning policy proposes abstract control actions, while a deterministic runtime safety shield filters unsafe actions using fast forward simulation. Safety is enforced as a runtime invariant, independent of policy quality or training distribution. The proposed framework is evaluated on the Grid2Op benchmark suite under nominal conditions, forced line-outage stress tests, and zero-shot deployment on the ICAPS 2021 large-scale transmission grid without retraining. Results show that flat reinforcement learning policies are brittle under stress, while safety-only methods are overly conservative. In contrast, the proposed hierarchical and safety-aware approach achieves longer episode survival, lower peak line loading, and robust zero-shot generalization to unseen grids. These results indicate that safety and generalization in power-grid control are best achieved through architectural design rather than increasingly complex reward engineering, providing a practical path toward deployable learning-based controllers for real-world energy systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于运行时安全防护的层次化强化学习在电网运行中的应用
强化学习在电网拓扑控制与阻塞管理等自动化任务中展现出潜力，但其在实际电力系统的部署仍受限于严格的安全要求、罕见扰动下的脆弱性以及对未知电网拓扑的泛化能力不足。在安全关键基础设施中，灾难性故障不可容忍，基于学习的控制器必须在硬性物理约束下运行。 本文提出一种面向电网运行的安全约束分层控制框架，明确将长时域决策与实时可行性执行解耦。高层强化学习策略提出抽象控制动作，而确定性运行时安全防护层通过快速前向模拟过滤不安全动作。安全性作为运行时不变性强制执行，与策略质量或训练分布无关。 该框架在Grid2Op基准测试套件中接受评估，涵盖正常运行条件、强制线路停运压力测试，以及在ICAPS 2021大规模输电网上无需重新训练的零样本部署。结果表明：扁平强化学习策略在压力下表现脆弱，纯安全方法则过于保守；相比之下，所提出的分层安全感知方法实现了更长的运行周期、更低的线路峰值负载，并对未知电网具有稳健的零样本泛化能力。 这些结果表明，电网控制中的安全性与泛化能力通过架构设计而非日益复杂的奖励工程能更有效实现，为现实能源系统中可部署的学习型控制器提供了实用路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe and robust reinforcement learning controllers in real-world power grids, which face strict safety constraints and poor generalization to unseen conditions, this paper proposes a hierarchical control framework that decouples high-level decision-making from real-time safety enforcement. The method employs a high-level RL policy to propose abstract actions, which are then filtered by a deterministic runtime safety shield using fast forward simulation to ensure physical feasibility. Experimental results on the Grid2Op benchmark, including stress tests and zero-shot deployment on a large-scale grid, demonstrate that this approach outperforms flat RL policies and safety-only methods by achieving longer episode survival, lower peak line loading, and robust generalization without retraining.
本文针对强化学习在现实电网控制中面临的安全约束严格和泛化能力不足的问题，提出了一种分层控制框架，将高层决策与实时安全执行解耦。该方法采用高层强化学习策略生成抽象控制动作，并通过基于快速前向仿真的确定性运行时安全屏蔽器过滤不安全动作以确保物理可行性。在Grid2Op基准测试中的实验结果表明，包括压力测试和在大规模电网上的零样本部署，该框架相比扁平强化学习策略和纯安全方法，能实现更长的运行生存期、更低的线路峰值负载，且无需重新训练即可稳健泛化。
BOAT: Navigating the Sea of In Silico Predictors for Antibody Design via Multi-Objective Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Jackie Rao, Ferran Gonzalez Hernandez, Leon Gerard, Alexandra Gessner
First: 2026-04-15T15:25:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:25:52+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 29th International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Antibody lead optimization is inherently a multi-objective challenge in drug discovery. Achieving a balance between different drug-like properties is crucial for the development of viable candidates, and this search becomes exponentially challenging as desired properties grow. The ever-growing zoo of sophisticated in silico tools for predicting antibody properties calls for an efficient joint optimization procedure to overcome resource-intensive sequential filtering pipelines. We present BOAT, a versatile Bayesian optimization framework for multi-property antibody engineering. Our `plug-and-play' framework couples uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling with a genetic algorithm to jointly optimize various predicted antibody traits while enabling efficient exploration of sequence space. Through systematic benchmarking against genetic algorithms and newer generative learning approaches, we demonstrate competitive performance with state-of-the-art methods for multi-objective protein optimization. We identify clear regimes where surrogate-driven optimization outperforms expensive generative approaches and establish practical limits imposed by sequence dimensionality and oracle costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BOAT：通过多目标贝叶斯优化在抗体设计的硅学预测器海洋中导航
抗体先导优化本质上是药物发现中的多目标挑战。在不同类药性质间取得平衡对于开发可行候选药物至关重要，而随着所需性质的增加，这种搜索的难度呈指数级增长。日益复杂的抗体性质硅学预测工具亟需一种高效的联合优化流程，以克服资源密集型的顺序筛选流程。我们提出BOAT——一个用于多性质抗体工程的通用贝叶斯优化框架。该'即插即用'框架将不确定性感知代理模型与遗传算法相结合，在高效探索序列空间的同时联合优化多种预测的抗体特性。通过对遗传算法和新型生成学习方法的系统基准测试，我们证明了其在多目标蛋白质优化任务中与前沿方法具有竞争力的性能。我们明确了代理驱动优化优于昂贵生成方法的适用场景，并确定了序列维度和评估成本带来的实际限制。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces BOAT, a Bayesian optimization framework designed to address the multi-objective challenge of antibody lead optimization, where balancing multiple drug-like properties is critical but computationally demanding due to the proliferation of in silico predictors. The method combines uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling with a genetic algorithm in a plug-and-play manner to jointly optimize predicted antibody traits while efficiently exploring sequence space. Experimental benchmarking against genetic algorithms and generative learning approaches shows competitive performance, with the framework outperforming costly generative methods in certain scenarios and revealing practical limits related to sequence dimensionality and computational costs.
本文提出了BOAT，一个贝叶斯优化框架，旨在解决抗体先导化合物优化中的多目标挑战，即平衡多种类药性至关重要，但由于计算机预测工具的激增而计算复杂。该方法以即插即用的方式，将不确定性感知的代理模型与遗传算法结合，共同优化预测的抗体特性，同时高效探索序列空间。通过系统性地与遗传算法和生成学习方法进行基准测试，结果表明该框架具有竞争力，在某些情况下优于昂贵的生成方法，并揭示了序列维度和计算成本带来的实际限制。
Provably Efficient Offline-to-Online Value Adaptation with General Function Approximation
Authors: Shangzhe Li, Weitong Zhang
First: 2026-04-15T15:17:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:17:40+00:00
Comments: 44 pages, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study value adaptation in offline-to-online reinforcement learning under general function approximation. Starting from an imperfect offline pretrained $Q$-function, the learner aims to adapt it to the target environment using only a limited amount of online interaction. We first characterize the difficulty of this setting by establishing a minimax lower bound, showing that even when the pretrained $Q$-function is close to optimal $Q^\star$, online adaptation can be no more efficient than pure online RL on certain hard instances. On the positive side, under a novel structural condition on the offline-pretrained value functions, we propose O2O-LSVI, an adaptation algorithm with problem-dependent sample complexity that provably improves over pure online RL. Finally, we complement our theory with neural-network experiments that demonstrate the practical effectiveness of the proposed method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于通用函数逼近的可证明高效离线到在线价值适应方法

Restless Bandits with Individual Penalty Constraints: A New Near-Optimal Index Policy and How to Learn It
Authors: Nida Zamir, I-Hong Hou
First: 2026-04-05T12:53:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:05:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates the Restless Multi-Armed Bandit (RMAB) framework under individual penalty constraints to address resource allocation challenges in dynamic wireless networked environments. Unlike conventional RMAB models, our model allows each user (arm) to have distinct and stringent performance constraints, such as energy limits, activation limits, or age of information minimums, enabling the capture of diverse objectives including fairness and efficiency. To find the optimal resource allocation policy, we propose a new Penalty-Optimal Whittle (POW) index policy. The POW index of an user only depends on the user's transition kernel and penalty constraints, and remains invariable to system-wide features such as the number of users present and the amount of resource available. This makes it computationally tractable to calculate the POW indices offline without any need for online adaptation. Moreover, we theoretically prove that the POW index policy is asymptotically optimal while satisfying all individual penalty constraints. We also introduce a deep reinforcement learning algorithm to efficiently learn the POW index on the fly. Simulation results across various applications and system configurations further demonstrate that the POW index policy not only has near-optimal performance but also significantly outperforms other existing policies.

标题：带个体惩罚约束的躁动多臂赌博机：一种新的近优索引策略及其学习方法
本文研究了个体惩罚约束下的躁动多臂赌博机（RMAB）框架，以应对动态无线网络环境中的资源分配挑战。与传统RMAB模型不同，本模型允许每个用户（臂）具有独立且严格的性能约束，如能量限制、激活限制或信息时效性下限，从而能够兼顾公平性与效率等多样化目标。为寻求最优资源分配策略，我们提出了一种新的惩罚最优惠特尔（POW）索引策略。用户的POW索引仅取决于其状态转移核与惩罚约束，且与系统规模（如用户数量、可用资源量）无关。这使得离线计算POW索引具有计算可行性，无需在线调整。理论证明该策略在满足所有个体惩罚约束的同时具有渐近最优性。我们还引入了一种深度强化学习算法以动态高效学习POW索引。多场景仿真结果表明，POW索引策略不仅具备近优性能，且显著优于现有其他策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for resource allocation in dynamic wireless networks with diverse user-specific constraints, this paper introduces a novel Penalty-Optimal Whittle (POW) index policy for Restless Multi-Armed Bandits (RMAB) that incorporates individual penalty constraints like energy limits or fairness requirements. The method involves deriving a user-specific POW index based solely on each user's transition dynamics and constraints, making it computationally efficient and offline-calculable without system-wide adaptation. Experimental simulations across various applications show that the POW policy is asymptotically optimal, satisfies all constraints, and outperforms existing policies in near-optimal performance.

Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization
Authors: Yu Li, Sizhe Tang, Tian Lan
First: 2026-04-08T14:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:01:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：链中推理，树中学习：多轮智能体策略优化的自校正与嫁接方法
大语言模型智能体的强化学习常受多步推理任务中稀疏奖励的制约。现有方法（如组相对策略优化）将采样轨迹视为独立链，对每条链的所有步骤赋予均匀奖励，忽略了可能对推理结果产生不成比例影响的关键步骤。本文提出T-STAR（树状结构自教导智能体校正）框架，该框架能还原看似独立轨迹间的潜在关联奖励结构。具体而言，我们通过识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点，将轨迹整合为统一的认知树。该结构支持内省评估机制，将轨迹级奖励沿树反向传播，从而获得步骤级方差缩减的相对优势新度量。基于认知树，我们还开发了上下文思维嫁接技术，通过对比关键分歧点/步骤的成功与失败分支来合成校正推理。随后，我们提出的精准策略优化利用布拉德利-特里型精准损失函数，聚焦于这些关键点/步骤的丰富策略梯度信息。在具身交互、推理与规划基准上的大量实验表明，T-STAR在强基线模型上实现了持续改进，在需要长推理链的任务中提升尤为显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sparse rewards in reinforcement learning for multi-turn LLM agents, where existing methods often treat trajectories as independent chains and uniformly credit all steps, overlooking critical steps that disproportionately affect outcomes. To overcome this, the authors propose T-STAR, a framework that consolidates sampled trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by merging functionally similar nodes, enabling an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards to obtain variance-reduced step-level advantages, and In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points. Experimental results across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks show that T-STAR consistently outperforms strong baselines, with particularly notable gains on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.

DiPO: Disentangled Perplexity Policy Optimization for Fine-grained Exploration-Exploitation Trade-Off
Authors: Xiaofan Li, Ming Yang, Zhiyuan Ma, Shichao Ma, Jintao Du, Yu Cheng, Weiqiang Wang, Zhizhong Zhang, Xin Tan, Yanyun Qu, Lizhuang Ma, Yuan Xie
First: 2026-04-15T14:12:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T14:12:10+00:00
Comments: LLM Reinforce Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed significant advances in the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, effectively managing the exploration and exploitation trade-off remains a critical challenge. In this paper, we fully analyze the exploration and exploitation dilemma of extremely hard and easy samples during the training and propose a new fine-grained trade-off mechanism. Concretely, we introduce a perplexity space disentangling strategy that divides the sample space into distinct exploration (high perplexity) and exploitation (low perplexity) subspaces, thereby mining fine-grained samples requiring exploration-exploitation trade-off. Subsequently, we propose a bidirectional reward allocation mechanism with a minimum impact on verification rewards to implement perplexity-guided exploration and exploitation, enabling more stable policy optimization. Finally, we have evaluated our method on two mainstream tasks: mathematical reasoning and function calling, and experimental results demonstrate the superiority of the proposed method, confirming its effectiveness in enhancing LLM performance by fine-grained exploration-exploitation trade-off.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DiPO：面向细粒度探索-利用权衡的解耦困惑度策略优化
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著推动了大型语言模型（LLM）推理能力的发展，但如何有效管理探索与利用的权衡仍是关键挑战。本文深入分析了训练过程中极难与极易样本的探索-利用困境，提出一种新的细粒度权衡机制。具体而言，我们引入一种困惑度空间解耦策略，将样本空间划分为独立的探索（高困惑度）与利用（低困惑度）子空间，从而挖掘需要探索-利用权衡的细粒度样本。随后，我们提出一种对验证奖励影响最小的双向奖励分配机制，实现困惑度引导的探索与利用，使策略优化更稳定。最后，我们在数学推理和函数调用两个主流任务上评估了本方法，实验结果证明了所提方法的优越性，证实了其通过细粒度探索-利用权衡提升LLM性能的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of balancing exploration and exploitation in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models (LLMs), where existing methods struggle with fine-grained trade-offs on samples of varying difficulty. To tackle this, the authors propose DiPO, a method that first disentangles the sample space into exploration (high perplexity) and exploitation (low perplexity) subspaces to identify samples needing trade-off, then implements a bidirectional reward allocation mechanism for perplexity-guided policy optimization with minimal impact on verification rewards. Experimental evaluations on mathematical reasoning and function calling tasks show that DiPO outperforms existing approaches, effectively enhancing LLM performance through its fine-grained exploration-exploitation mechanism.

Beyond Conservative Automated Driving in Multi-Agent Scenarios via Coupled Model Predictive Control and Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Saeed Rahmani, Gözde Körpe, Zhenlin, Xu, Bruno Brito, Simeon Craig Calvert, Bart van Arem
First: 2026-04-15T13:58:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T13:58:38+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated driving at unsignalized intersections is challenging due to complex multi-vehicle interactions and the need to balance safety and efficiency. Model Predictive Control (MPC) offers structured constraint handling through optimization but relies on hand-crafted rules that often produce overly conservative behavior. Deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) learns adaptive behaviors from experience but often struggles with safety assurance and generalization to unseen environments. In this study, we present an integrated MPC-RL framework to improve navigation performance in multi-agent scenarios. Experiments show that MPC-RL outperforms standalone MPC and end-to-end RL across three traffic-density levels. Collectively, MPC-RL reduces the collision rate by 21% and improves the success rate by 6.5% compared to pure MPC. We further evaluate zero-shot transfer to a highway merging scenario without retraining. Both MPC-based methods transfer substantially better than end-to-end PPO, which highlights the role of the MPC backbone in cross-scenario robustness. The framework also shows faster loss stabilization than end-to-end RL during training, which indicates a reduced learning burden. These results suggest that the integrated approach can improve the balance between safety performance and efficiency in multi-agent intersection scenarios, while the MPC component provides a strong foundation for generalization across driving environments. The implementation code is available open-source.

标题：基于耦合模型预测控制与深度强化学习的多智能体场景非保守自动驾驶

Drowsiness-Aware Adaptive Autonomous Braking System based on Deep Reinforcement Learning for Enhanced Road Safety
Authors: Hossem Eddine Hafidi, Elisabetta De Giovanni, Teodoro Montanaro, Ilaria Sergi, Massimo De Vittorio, Luigi Patrono
First: 2026-04-15T13:39:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T13:39:56+00:00
Comments: This manuscript is 10 pages long and includes 12 figures and 3 tables. The figures provide detailed visualizations of the proposed system architecture, ECG-based drowsiness detection pipeline, Double-Dueling DQN framework, and experimental evaluation results in the CARLA simulation environment
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Driver drowsiness significantly impairs the ability to accurately judge safe braking distances and is estimated to contribute to 10%-20% of road accidents in Europe. Traditional driver-assistance systems lack adaptability to real-time physiological states such as drowsiness. This paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning-based autonomous braking system that integrates vehicle dynamics with driver physiological data. Drowsiness is detected from ECG signals using a Recurrent Neural Network (RNN), selected through an extensive benchmark analysis of 2-minute windows with varying segmentation and overlap configurations. The inferred drowsiness state is incorporated into the observable state space of a Double-Dueling Deep Q-Network (DQN) agent, where driver impairment is modeled as an action delay. The system is implemented and evaluated in a high-fidelity CARLA simulation environment. Experimental results show that the proposed agent achieves a 99.99% success rate in avoiding collisions under both drowsy and non-drowsy conditions. These findings demonstrate the effectiveness of physiology-aware control strategies for enhancing adaptive and intelligent driving safety systems.

标题：基于深度强化学习的睡意感知自适应自主制动系统以提升道路安全

Three Roles, One Model: Role Orchestration at Inference Time to Close the Performance Gap Between Small and Large Agents
Authors: S. Aaron McClendon, Jorge Gallego-Feliciano, Stavros Zervoudakis, Antonios Saravanos
First: 2026-04-13T13:40:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T13:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents show promise on realistic tool-use tasks, but deploying capable agents on modest hardware remains challenging. We study whether inference-time scaffolding alone, without any additional training compute, can improve the performance of a small model in complex multi-step environments. Operating on a single 24GB GPU, we evaluate Qwen3-8B on the AppWorld benchmark under both full-precision and 4-bit quantized configurations. Without any intervention, the raw model achieves just 5.4% (FP16) and 3.0% (AWQ) task goal completion. Guided by a systematic failure mode analysis, we introduce a three-tier inference scaffolding pipeline that deploys the same frozen model in three distinct roles: (1) a summarization model that preserves critical artifacts (tokens, credentials, API responses) while compressing dialogue history; (2) the main agent model that reasons over the compressed context; and (3) an isolated correction model that reviews and revises the agent's code output without access to conversation history, breaking repetitive failure loops. Applied to the same unmodified model, this scaffolding yields 8.9% (FP16) and 5.9% (AWQ) task goal completion, roughly doubling performance in both settings, with particularly strong gains on difficulty-1 tasks (15.8% to 26.3% FP16; 5.3% to 14.0% AWQ). On full-precision inference, our scaffolded 8B model surpasses DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct (7.1%) from the original AppWorld evaluation, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with systems 4 times their size. We formalize the approach as a scaffolded policy over a frozen base model, three invocations of the same weights with different conditioning, drawing connections to test-time compute scaling and action-space shaping in reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：三重角色，单一模型：通过推理时角色编排缩小大小智能体间的性能差距
大语言模型智能体在现实工具使用任务中展现出潜力，但在有限硬件上部署高性能智能体仍具挑战。本研究探讨仅通过推理时架构支持（无需额外训练计算）能否提升小模型在复杂多步骤环境中的表现。我们在单张24GB GPU上，评估Qwen3-8B模型在AppWorld基准测试中的全精度与4位量化配置表现。未经干预时，原始模型任务目标完成率仅为5.4%（FP16）和3.0%（AWQ）。基于系统性故障模式分析，我们引入三层推理架构流水线，将同一冻结模型部署于三个独立角色：（1）摘要模型：压缩对话历史同时保留关键信息（令牌、凭证、API响应）；（2）主智能体模型：在压缩上下文中进行推理；（3）独立修正模型：脱离对话历史审查并修正智能体的代码输出，打破重复故障循环。应用此架构后，同一未修改模型的任务完成率提升至8.9%（FP16）和5.9%（AWQ），两种设置下性能均实现约两倍提升，在难度1任务上增益尤为显著（FP16从15.8%至26.3%；AWQ从5.3%至14.0%）。全精度推理时，经架构优化的8B模型超越了原始AppWorld评估中DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct的表现（7.1%），证明结构化推理时干预能使小模型达到四倍规模系统的竞争力。我们将该方法形式化为冻结基础模型上的架构策略——通过三种不同条件调用同一权重，建立了与强化学习中测试时计算扩展和动作空间塑形的理论联系。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the challenge of deploying capable large language model agents on modest hardware, investigating whether inference-time scaffolding alone can improve a small model's performance without additional training. The method introduces a three-tier inference pipeline that orchestrates a single frozen model into three distinct roles: a summarizer to compress dialogue history, a main agent for reasoning, and an isolated correction model to review and revise code outputs, thereby breaking repetitive failure loops. Experimental results on the AppWorld benchmark with Qwen3-8B show that this scaffolding roughly doubles task goal completion rates, from 5.4% to 8.9% in full-precision and from 3.0% to 5.9% in 4-bit quantized configurations, even enabling the 8B model to surpass a 33B model in full-precision inference.
本研究旨在解决在有限硬件上部署高性能大语言模型智能体的挑战，探索仅通过推理时架构支持（无需额外训练）来提升小模型性能的可能性。方法上，提出了一种三层推理流程，将同一冻结模型编排为三个不同角色：总结模型压缩对话历史，主智能体模型进行推理，以及独立校正模型审查和修正代码输出以打破重复失败循环。在AppWorld基准测试中，对Qwen3-8B的实验结果表明，该架构使任务目标完成率大致翻倍，全精度下从5.4%提升至8.9%，4位量化下从3.0%提升至5.9%，甚至使8B模型在全精度推理中超越了原有评估中的33B模型。
RPS: Information Elicitation with Reinforcement Prompt Selection
Authors: Tao Wang, Jingyao Lu, Xibo Wang, Haonan Huang, Su Yao, Zhiqiang Hu, Xingyan Chen, Enmao Diao
First: 2026-04-15T12:51:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:51:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have shown remarkable capabilities in dialogue generation and reasoning, yet their effectiveness in eliciting user-known but concealed information in open-ended conversations remains limited. In many interactive AI applications, such as personal assistants, tutoring systems, and legal or clinical support, users often withhold sensitive or uncertain information due to privacy concerns, ambiguity, or social hesitation. This makes it challenging for LLMs to gather complete and contextually relevant inputs. In this work, we define the problem of information elicitation in open-ended dialogue settings and propose Reinforcement Prompt Selection (RPS), a lightweight reinforcement learning framework that formulates prompt selection as a sequential decision-making problem. To analyze this problem in a controlled setting, we design a synthetic experiment, where a reinforcement learning agent outperforms a random query baseline, illustrating the potential of policy-based approaches for adaptive information elicitation. Building on this insight, RPS learns a policy over a pool of prompts to adaptively elicit concealed or incompletely expressed information from users through dialogue. We also introduce IELegal, a new benchmark dataset constructed from real legal case documents, which simulates dialogue-based information elicitation tasks aimed at uncovering case-relevant facts. In this setting, RPS outperforms static prompt baselines, demonstrating the effectiveness of adaptive prompt selection for eliciting critical information in LLM-driven dialogue systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RPS：基于强化提示选择的信息引导方法
大语言模型在对话生成与推理方面展现出卓越能力，但在开放式对话中引导用户已知却隐藏信息的效果仍有限。在个人助手、教学系统、法律或临床支持等交互式AI应用中，用户常因隐私顾虑、表述模糊或社交迟疑而隐瞒敏感或不确定信息，导致大语言模型难以获取完整且上下文相关的输入。本研究定义了开放式对话场景中的信息引导问题，提出强化提示选择框架——一种将提示选择建模为序列决策问题的轻量级强化学习方法。通过设计合成实验进行可控分析，强化学习智能体在随机查询基线对比中表现更优，验证了基于策略的自适应信息引导方法的潜力。基于此，RPS通过对话从提示池中学习策略，自适应引导用户透露隐藏或未完整表达的信息。同时，我们构建了IELegal基准数据集——基于真实法律案例文档构建，模拟旨在挖掘案件相关事实的对话式信息引导任务。在该场景中，RPS显著优于静态提示基线，证明了自适应提示选择在LLM驱动对话系统中引导关键信息的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of eliciting concealed or incompletely expressed information from users in open-ended dialogues with large language models (LLMs), motivated by applications like personal assistants and legal support where users may withhold sensitive details. It proposes Reinforcement Prompt Selection (RPS), a lightweight reinforcement learning framework that treats prompt selection as a sequential decision-making problem to adaptively query users. Experimental results include a synthetic setup where RPS outperforms random baselines, and evaluation on the new IELegal benchmark dataset, derived from real legal cases, shows RPS surpasses static prompt methods in uncovering critical facts.
本文针对大型语言模型在开放对话中难以获取用户已知但隐藏信息的问题展开研究，动机源于个人助理、法律支持等应用中用户可能因隐私或不确定性而隐瞒信息。方法上提出了强化提示选择（RPS），这是一个轻量级强化学习框架，将提示选择建模为序列决策问题以自适应地引导用户。主要实验结果包括：在合成实验中RPS优于随机查询基线，并在基于真实法律案例构建的IELegal基准数据集上，RPS超越了静态提示方法，有效提升了关键信息的获取能力。
AlphaCNOT: Learning CNOT Minimization with Model-Based Planning
Authors: Jacopo Cossio, Daniele Lizzio Bosco, Riccardo Romanello, Giuseppe Serra, Carla Piazza
First: 2026-04-15T12:46:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:46:40+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 11 figures , journal
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum circuit optimization is a central task in Quantum Computing, as current Noisy Intermediate Scale Quantum devices suffer from error propagation that often scales with the number of operations. Among quantum operations, the CNOT gate is of fundamental importance, being the only 2-qubit gate in the universal Clifford+T set. The problem of CNOT gates minimization has been addressed by heuristic algorithms such as the well-known Patel-Markov-Hayes (PMH) for linear reversible synthesis (i.e., CNOT minimization with no topological constraints), and more recently by Reinforcement Learning (RL) based strategies in the more complex case of topology-aware synthesis, where each CNOT can act on a subset of all qubits pairs. In this work we introduce AlphaCNOT, a RL framework based on Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) that address effectively the CNOT minimization problem by modeling it as a planning problem. In contrast to other RL- based solution, our method is model-based, i.e. it can leverage lookahead search to evaluate future trajectories, thus finding more efficient sequences of CNOTs. Our method achieves a reduction of up to 32% in CNOT gate count compared to PMH baseline on linear reversible synthesis, while in the constraint version we report a consistent gate count reduction on a variety of topologies with up to 8 qubits, with respect to state-of-the-art RL-based solutions. Our results suggest the combination of RL with search-based strategies can be applied to different circuit optimization tasks, such as Clifford minimization, thus fostering the transition toward the "quantum utility" era.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AlphaCNOT：基于模型规划学习的CNOT门最小化方法
量子电路优化是量子计算的核心任务，当前噪声中等规模量子设备受误差传播影响，其程度常随操作数量增加而加剧。在量子操作中，CNOT门具有基础重要性，是通用Clifford+T集合中唯一的双量子比特门。CNOT门最小化问题已通过启发式算法得到解决，例如线性可逆综合中著名的Patel-Markov-Hayes算法，以及近期在更复杂的拓扑感知综合中采用基于强化学习的方法。本文提出AlphaCNOT，一种基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的强化学习框架，通过将问题建模为规划任务有效解决CNOT最小化问题。与其他基于强化学习的方案不同，本方法采用模型驱动策略，可利用前瞻搜索评估未来轨迹，从而发现更高效的CNOT序列。在线性可逆综合中，本方法相比PMH基线实现CNOT门数量最高减少32%；在约束版本中，针对最多8量子比特的多种拓扑结构，相较最先进的强化学习方案实现了持续的门数量缩减。结果表明，强化学习与搜索策略的结合可应用于不同电路优化任务，如Clifford最小化，从而推动向'量子效用'时代的演进。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reduce error-prone operations in noisy quantum devices, this paper introduces AlphaCNOT, a model-based reinforcement learning framework using Monte Carlo Tree Search to minimize CNOT gates in quantum circuits. The method treats CNOT minimization as a planning problem, enabling lookahead search to evaluate future gate sequences, which outperforms heuristic and prior RL approaches. Experimental results show up to a 32% reduction in CNOT count compared to the Patel-Markov-Hayes baseline for linear reversible synthesis and consistent improvements over state-of-the-art RL methods in topology-constrained settings with up to 8 qubits, suggesting broader applicability to quantum circuit optimization tasks.
本文针对噪声量子设备中易出错操作需减少的问题，提出了AlphaCNOT，一种基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的模型强化学习框架，用于最小化量子电路中的CNOT门。该方法将CNOT最小化建模为规划问题，通过前瞻搜索评估未来门序列，从而超越了启发式算法和先前的强化学习方法。实验结果表明，在线性可逆合成中，相比Patel-Markov-Hayes基线，CNOT数量减少了高达32%；在拓扑约束条件下，对于最多8个量子比特的各种拓扑结构，相比最先进的强化学习方法也实现了持续的门数减少，表明该方法可推广至其他量子电路优化任务。
Character Beyond Speech: Leveraging Role-Playing Evaluation in Audio Large Language Models via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongjie Fu, Fangming Feng, Xize Cheng, Linjun Li, Zhou Zhao, Tao Jin
First: 2026-04-15T12:39:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:39:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid evolution of multimodal large models has revolutionized the simulation of diverse characters in speech dialogue systems, enabling a novel interactive paradigm. Character attributes are manifested not only in textual responses but also through vocal features, as speech conveys rich paralinguistic information that is challenging to quantify. This poses significant difficulties in evaluating the character alignment of role-playing agents. To address these challenges, we present RoleJudge, an evaluation framework that leverages audio large language models to systematically assess the alignment between speech and character across multiple modalities and dimensions. Furthermore, we introduce RoleChat, the first voice role-playing evaluation dataset enriched with chain-of-thought reasoning annotations, comprising a diverse set of authentic and LLM-generated speech samples. Utilizing this dataset, we implement a multi-stage training paradigm and incorporate Standard Alignment in reinforcement learning to mitigate reward misalignment during optimization. Experimental results in terms of accuracy and subjective assessment demonstrate that RoleJudge outperforms various baseline models, validating the effectiveness of our multidimensional evaluation framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越言语的角色：通过强化学习在音频大语言模型中利用角色扮演评估
多模态大模型的快速发展革新了语音对话系统中多样化角色的模拟，催生了一种新颖的交互范式。角色属性不仅体现在文本回应中，还通过语音特征展现，因为语音传递了丰富的副语言信息，这些信息难以量化。这给评估角色扮演代理的角色一致性带来了显著挑战。为解决这些问题，我们提出了RoleJudge评估框架，该框架利用音频大语言模型，系统性地评估跨多种模态和维度的语音与角色一致性。此外，我们引入了RoleChat，这是首个富含思维链推理注释的语音角色扮演评估数据集，包含多样化的真实和LLM生成的语音样本。利用该数据集，我们实施了一个多阶段训练范式，并在强化学习中融入标准对齐，以缓解优化过程中的奖励错位问题。在准确性和主观评估方面的实验结果表明，RoleJudge优于多种基线模型，验证了我们多维评估框架的有效性。

Motivated by the challenge of evaluating character alignment in speech dialogue systems, where vocal features convey rich paralinguistic information beyond text, this paper introduces RoleJudge, a framework that uses audio large language models to assess speech-character alignment across multiple modalities and dimensions. The method involves creating RoleChat, a voice role-playing dataset with chain-of-thought annotations, and implementing a multi-stage training paradigm with Standard Alignment in reinforcement learning to address reward misalignment. 本文的动机源于评估语音对话系统中角色对齐的挑战，其中语音特征传达了超越文本的丰富副语言信息，难以量化。为此，研究提出了RoleJudge框架，利用音频大语言模型从多模态和多维度系统评估语音与角色的对齐性。方法包括创建首个带有思维链推理注释的语音角色扮演数据集RoleChat，并采用多阶段训练范式，在强化学习中引入标准对齐以优化过程中的奖励偏差。实验结果表明，RoleJudge在准确性和主观评估上均优于多种基线模型，验证了该多维评估框架的有效性。
Soft $Q(λ)$: A multi-step off-policy method for entropy regularised reinforcement learning using eligibility traces
Authors: Pranav Mahajan, Ben Seymour
First: 2026-04-15T12:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:10:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Soft Q-learning has emerged as a versatile model-free method for entropy-regularised reinforcement learning, optimising for returns augmented with a penalty on the divergence from a reference policy. Despite its success, the multi-step extensions of soft Q-learning remain relatively unexplored and limited to on-policy action sampling under the Boltzmann policy. In this brief research note, we first present a formal $n$-step formulation for soft Q-learning and then extend this framework to the fully off-policy case by introducing a novel Soft Tree Backup operator. Finally, we unify these developments into Soft $Q(λ)$, an elegant online, off-policy, eligibility trace framework that allows for efficient credit assignment under arbitrary behaviour policies. Our derivations propose a model-free method for learning entropy-regularised value functions that can be utilised in future empirical experiments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Soft $Q(λ)$：一种基于资格迹的多步离策略熵正则化强化学习方法
Soft Q-learning 已成为一种通用的无模型熵正则化强化学习方法，通过优化回报并惩罚与参考策略的差异来实现。尽管其成功，soft Q-learning 的多步扩展仍相对未被充分探索，且局限于玻尔兹曼策略下的同策略动作采样。在本研究简报中，我们首先提出了 soft Q-learning 的正式 $n$ 步公式，随后通过引入一种新颖的 Soft Tree Backup 算子，将该框架扩展至完全离策略场景。最后，我们将这些进展统一为 Soft $Q(λ)$——一个优雅的在线、离策略、基于资格迹的框架，能够在任意行为策略下实现高效的信用分配。我们的推导提出了一种用于学习熵正则化价值函数的无模型方法，可供未来实证实验使用。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend soft Q-learning, a model-free entropy-regularised reinforcement learning method, to multi-step and fully off-policy settings, as existing multi-step approaches are limited to on-policy sampling. The method introduces a formal n-step formulation and a novel Soft Tree Backup operator to enable off-policy learning, culminating in Soft Q(λ), an online, off-policy eligibility trace framework for efficient credit assignment under arbitrary behaviour policies. The main experimental results are not detailed in the abstract, but the derivations propose a model-free method for learning entropy-regularised value functions intended for future empirical validation.
本文的动机源于需要将软Q学习（一种无模型的熵正则化强化学习方法）扩展到多步和完全离策略设置，因为现有的多步方法仅限于在策略采样。该方法提出了一个正式的n步公式和一个新颖的软树回溯算子，以实现离策略学习，最终形成了Soft Q(λ)，这是一个在线、离策略的资格迹框架，可在任意行为策略下进行高效信用分配。摘要中未详细描述主要实验结果，但推导提出了一种用于学习熵正则化价值函数的无模型方法，旨在供未来的实证实验使用。
RL-PLUS: Countering Capability Boundary Collapse of LLMs in Reinforcement Learning with Hybrid-policy Optimization
Authors: Yihong Dong, Xue Jiang, Yongding Tao, Huanyu Liu, Kechi Zhang, Lili Mou, Rongyu Cao, Yingwei Ma, Jue Chen, Binhua Li, Zhi Jin, Fei Huang, Yongbin Li, Ge Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-07-31T23:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:41:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (main)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) has significantly advanced the complex reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, it struggles to break through the inherent capability boundaries of the base LLM, due to its essentially on-policy strategy coupled with LLM's immense action space and sparse reward. Critically, RLVR can lead to the capability boundary collapse, narrowing the LLM's problem-solving scope. To address this problem, we propose RL-PLUS, a novel hybrid-policy optimization approach for LLMs that synergizes internal exploitation with external data to achieve stronger reasoning capabilities and surpass the boundaries of base models. RL-PLUS integrates two core components, i.e., Multiple Importance Sampling to address distributional mismatch from external data, and Exploration-Based Advantage Function to guide the model towards high-value, unexplored reasoning paths. We provide both theoretical analysis and extensive experiments to demonstrate the superiority and generalizability of our approach. Compared with existing RLVR methods, RL-PLUS achieves 1) state-of-the-art performance on six math reasoning benchmarks; 2) superior performance on six out-of-distribution reasoning tasks; 3) consistent and significant gains across diverse model families, with average relative improvements up to 69.2\%. Moreover, the analysis of Pass@k curves indicates that RL-PLUS effectively resolves the capability boundary collapse problem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-PLUS：通过混合策略优化应对大语言模型在强化学习中的能力边界坍缩
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的复杂推理能力，但由于其本质上的同策略特性，结合LLMs庞大的动作空间与稀疏奖励，难以突破基础LLM固有的能力边界。关键的是，RLVR可能导致能力边界坍缩，缩小LLM的解决问题范围。为解决此问题，我们提出RL-PLUS——一种新颖的混合策略优化方法，通过协同内部开发与外部数据，实现更强的推理能力并超越基础模型边界。RL-PLUS整合了两个核心组件：多重重要性采样以解决外部数据的分布失配问题，以及基于探索的优势函数以引导模型走向高价值、未探索的推理路径。我们通过理论分析和大量实验证明了该方法的优越性与泛化能力。与现有RLVR方法相比，RL-PLUS实现了：1）在六个数学推理基准上达到最先进性能；2）在六个分布外推理任务上表现优异；3）在不同模型家族中取得一致且显著的提升，平均相对改进高达69.2%。此外，Pass@k曲线分析表明RL-PLUS有效解决了能力边界坍缩问题。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of capability boundary collapse in Large Language Models (LLMs) during Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR), where on-policy strategies limit performance due to the LLM's vast action space and sparse rewards. To overcome this, the authors propose RL-PLUS, a hybrid-policy optimization method that combines internal exploitation with external data, utilizing Multiple Importance Sampling to handle distributional mismatches and an Exploration-Based Advantage Function to guide exploration of high-value reasoning paths. Experimental results show that RL-PLUS achieves state-of-the-art performance on six math reasoning benchmarks, superior out-of-distribution generalization on six tasks, and consistent gains across model families with average relative improvements up to 69.2%, effectively mitigating capability boundary collapse as evidenced by Pass@k curve analysis.
本文针对大型语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中出现的“能力边界坍塌”问题，即由于模型固有的策略性限制、庞大的动作空间和稀疏奖励，导致其难以突破基础模型的能力边界。为解决此问题，作者提出了RL-PLUS，一种混合策略优化方法，通过结合内部利用和外部数据，采用多重重要性采样处理分布不匹配，并利用基于探索的优势函数引导模型探索高价值推理路径。实验结果表明，RL-PLUS在六个数学推理基准上取得了最先进的性能，在六个分布外推理任务上表现出色，并在不同模型家族中实现了高达69.2%的平均相对提升，通过Pass@k曲线分析证实了该方法有效解决了能力边界坍塌问题。
Think Outside the Policy: In-Context Steered Policy Optimization
Authors: Hsiu-Yuan Huang, Chenming Tang, Weijie Liu, Clive Bai, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-10-30T14:14:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:36:27+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings. 19 pages, 13 figures, 12 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), have achieved remarkable progress in improving the reasoning capabilities of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs). However, they exhibit limited exploration due to reliance on on-policy rollouts which are confined to the current policy's distribution, resulting in narrow trajectory diversity. Recent approaches attempt to expand policy coverage by incorporating trajectories generated from stronger expert models, yet this reliance increases computational cost and such advanced models are often inaccessible. To address these issues, we propose In-Context Steered Policy Optimization (ICPO), a unified framework that leverages the inherent in-context learning capability of LRMs to provide expert guidance using existing datasets. ICPO introduces mixed-policy GRPO with implicit expert forcing, which expands exploration beyond the current policy distribution without requiring advanced LRM trajectories. To further stabilize optimization, ICPO integrates expert region reject sampling to filter unreliable off-policy trajectories and annealed expert-bonus reward shaping to balance early expert guidance with later autonomous improvement. Results demonstrate that ICPO consistently enhances RLVR performance and training stability on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, revealing a scalable and effective RLVR paradigm for LRMs. Our code is available at https://github.com/Celine-hxy/ICPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破策略局限：上下文引导策略优化
现有可验证奖励强化学习方法（如GRPO）在提升大型推理模型能力方面取得显著进展，但其依赖当前策略分布内的同策略轨迹，导致探索受限与轨迹多样性不足。近期研究尝试引入专家模型轨迹以扩展策略覆盖，但会带来计算成本增加且依赖难以获取的先进模型。为此，我们提出上下文引导策略优化框架，利用大型推理模型固有的上下文学习能力，通过现有数据集提供专家指导。该框架引入隐式专家强化的混合策略GRPO，无需依赖先进模型轨迹即可突破当前策略分布的探索限制。为进一步稳定优化，本方法集成专家区域拒绝采样以过滤不可靠的异策略轨迹，并采用退火专家奖励塑形来平衡早期专家指导与后期自主改进。实验表明，该方法在数学推理基准上持续提升RLVR性能与训练稳定性，为大型推理模型提供了可扩展且有效的RLVR范式。代码已开源。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limited exploration and high computational cost of existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods for Large Reasoning Models (LRMs), which rely on on-policy rollouts or inaccessible expert models. The proposed method, In-Context Steered Policy Optimization (ICPO), leverages the in-context learning capability of LRMs to provide expert guidance using existing datasets, introducing mixed-policy Group Relative Policy Optimization with implicit expert forcing to expand exploration, along with expert region reject sampling and annealed expert-bonus reward shaping for stability. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that ICPO consistently enhances RLVR performance and training stability, offering a scalable and effective paradigm.
本研究的动机是解决现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习方法在大型推理模型中的探索有限和计算成本高的问题，这些方法依赖于当前策略的采样或难以获取的专家模型。提出的方法称为上下文引导策略优化，它利用大型推理模型的上下文学习能力，通过现有数据集提供专家指导，引入了混合策略的组相对策略优化与隐式专家强制来扩展探索，并结合专家区域拒绝采样和退火专家奖励塑形以提升稳定性。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法能持续提升强化学习性能和训练稳定性，提供了一个可扩展且有效的范式。
Jump-Start Reinforcement Learning with Vision-Language-Action Regularization
Authors: Angelo Moroncelli, Roberto Zanetti, Marco Maccarini, Loris Roveda
First: 2026-04-15T11:17:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:17:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) enables high-frequency, closed-loop control for robotic manipulation, but scaling to long-horizon tasks with sparse or imperfect rewards remains difficult due to inefficient exploration and poor credit assignment. Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models leverage large-scale multimodal pretraining to provide generalist, task-level reasoning, but current limitations hinder their direct use in fast and precise manipulation. In this paper, we propose Vision-Language-Action Jump-Starting (VLAJS), a method that bridges sparse VLA guidance with on-policy RL to improve exploration and learning efficiency. VLAJS treats VLAs as transient sources of high-level action suggestions that bias early exploration and improve credit assignment, while preserving the high-frequency, state-based control of RL. Our approach augments Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with a directional action-consistency regularization that softly aligns the RL agent's actions with VLA guidance during early training, without enforcing strict imitation, requiring demonstrations, or relying on continuous teacher queries. VLA guidance is applied sparsely and annealed over time, allowing the agent to adapt online and ultimately surpass the guiding policy. We evaluate VLAJS on six challenging manipulation tasks: lifting, pick-and-place, peg reorientation, peg insertion, poking, and pushing in simulation, and validate a subset on a real Franka Panda robot. VLAJS consistently outperforms PPO and distillation-style baselines in sample efficiency, reducing required environment interactions by over 50% in several tasks. Real-world experiments demonstrate zero-shot sim-to-real transfer and robust execution under clutter, object variation, and external perturbations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于视觉-语言-动作正则化的强化学习快速启动方法
强化学习（RL）能够实现机器人操作的高频闭环控制，但由于探索效率低下和信用分配困难，在稀疏或不完美奖励的长周期任务中仍难以扩展。视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通过大规模多模态预训练提供通用任务级推理能力，但现有局限阻碍了其在快速精确操作中的直接应用。本文提出视觉-语言-动作快速启动（VLAJS）方法，通过稀疏VLA指导与在线策略RL的桥接来提升探索和学习效率。VLAJS将VLA模型视为高层动作建议的瞬态来源，用于引导早期探索并改进信用分配，同时保留RL基于状态的高频控制特性。该方法通过方向性动作一致性正则化增强近端策略优化（PPO），在早期训练中使RL智能体动作与VLA指导保持软对齐，无需强制严格模仿、演示数据或持续教师查询。VLA指导以稀疏方式应用并随时间退火，使智能体能够在线适应并最终超越指导策略。我们在六项挑战性操作任务（模拟环境中的抓举、取放、钉孔重定向、钉孔插入、戳动和推动）上评估VLAJS，并在真实Franka Panda机器人上验证了子集任务。VLAJS在样本效率上持续优于PPO和蒸馏式基线方法，在多项任务中减少超过50%的环境交互需求。真实世界实验展示了零样本仿真到现实的迁移能力，以及在杂乱场景、物体变化和外部干扰下的鲁棒执行性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling reinforcement learning (RL) for long-horizon robotic manipulation tasks, which suffer from inefficient exploration and poor credit assignment under sparse rewards. The proposed method, Vision-Language-Action Jump-Starting (VLAJS), bridges sparse guidance from Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models with on-policy RL to improve exploration; it augments Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with a directional action-consistency regularization that softly aligns the RL agent's actions with VLA suggestions during early training, without requiring strict imitation or demonstrations. 本文针对强化学习在稀疏奖励下长周期机器人操作任务中探索效率低和信用分配难的问题，提出了一种视觉-语言-动作跳跃启动方法。该方法通过稀疏的视觉-语言-动作模型高级动作建议来引导早期探索，并采用方向性动作一致性正则化将强化学习代理的动作与视觉-语言-动作模型的指导进行软对齐，无需严格模仿或演示。在六项模拟操作任务和真实机器人实验中的评估表明，该方法在样本效率上 consistently 优于近端策略优化和蒸馏基线，在多项任务中将环境交互需求减少超过50%，并实现了在杂乱环境和干扰下零模拟到真实迁移的鲁棒执行。
Towards Fine-grained Temporal Perception: Post-Training Large Audio-Language Models with Audio-Side Time Prompt
Authors: Yanfeng Shi, Pengfei Cai, Jun Liu, Qing Gu, Nan Jiang, Lirong Dai, Ian McLoughlin, Yan Song
First: 2026-04-15T10:50:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T10:50:29+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Interspeech 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Audio-Language Models (LALMs) enable general audio understanding and demonstrate remarkable performance across various audio tasks. However, these models still face challenges in temporal perception (e.g., inferring event onset and offset), leading to limited utility in fine-grained scenarios. To address this issue, we propose Audio-Side Time Prompt and leverage Reinforcement Learning (RL) to develop the TimePro-RL framework for fine-grained temporal perception. Specifically, we encode timestamps as embeddings and interleave them within the audio feature sequence as temporal coordinates to prompt the model. Furthermore, we introduce RL following Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) to directly optimize temporal alignment performance. Experiments demonstrate that TimePro-RL achieves significant performance gains across a range of audio temporal tasks, such as audio grounding, sound event detection, and dense audio captioning, validating its robust effectiveness.

Optimal Stability of KL Divergence under Gaussian Perturbations
Authors: Jialu Pan, Yufeng Zhang, Nan Hu, Keqin Li, Zhenbang Chen, Ji Wang
First: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T09:15:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of characterizing the stability of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence under Gaussian perturbations beyond Gaussian families. Existing relaxed triangle inequalities for KL divergence critically rely on the assumption that all involved distributions are Gaussian, which limits their applicability in modern applications such as out-of-distribution (OOD) detection with flow-based generative models. In this paper, we remove this restriction by establishing a sharp stability bound between an arbitrary distribution and Gaussian families under mild moment conditions. Specifically, let $P$ be a distribution with finite second moment, and let $\mathcal{N}_1$ and $\mathcal{N}_2$ be multivariate Gaussian distributions. We show that if $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$ is large and $KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$ is at most $ε$, then $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$. Moreover, we prove that this $\sqrtε$ rate is optimal in general, even within the Gaussian family. This result reveals an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, extending classical Gaussian-only relaxed triangle inequalities to general distributions. The result is non-trivial due to the asymmetry of KL divergence and the absence of a triangle inequality in general probability spaces. As an application, we provide a rigorous foundation for KL-based OOD analysis in flow-based models, removing strong Gaussian assumptions used in prior work. More broadly, our result enables KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings arising in deep learning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高斯扰动下KL散度的最优稳定性
本文研究了在高斯族之外，Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度在高斯扰动下的稳定性刻画问题。现有KL散度的松弛三角不等式严格依赖于所有涉及分布均为高斯的假设，这限制了其在基于流的生成模型进行分布外（OOD）检测等现代应用中的适用性。本文通过建立任意分布与高斯族之间在温和矩条件下的尖锐稳定性界，移除了这一限制。具体而言，设P为具有有限二阶矩的分布，N1和N2为多元高斯分布。我们证明，若KL(P||N1)较大且KL(N1||N2)至多为ε，则KL(P||N2) ≥ KL(P||N1) - O(√ε)。此外，我们证明即使在高斯族内，该√ε速率在一般情况下也是最优的。这一结果揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，将经典仅适用于高斯的松弛三角不等式推广至一般分布。由于KL散度的非对称性及一般概率空间中三角不等式的缺失，该结果具有非平凡性。作为应用，我们为基于流的模型中基于KL的OOD分析提供了严格的理论基础，消除了先前工作中使用的强高斯假设。更广泛地，我们的结果使得在深度学习和强化学习中出现的非高斯场景下进行基于KL的推理成为可能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend the stability analysis of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence beyond Gaussian distributions, as existing relaxed triangle inequalities are limited to Gaussian families, hindering applications like out-of-distribution detection in flow-based models. The method establishes a sharp stability bound under mild moment conditions, showing that for any distribution P with finite second moment and Gaussian distributions N1 and N2, if KL(P||N1) is large and KL(N1||N2) ≤ ε, then KL(P||N2) ≥ KL(P||N1) - O(√ε), with the √ε rate proven optimal even within Gaussian families. The main experimental results reveal an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, providing a rigorous foundation for KL-based out-of-distribution analysis in flow-based models and enabling broader KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian deep learning and reinforcement learning settings.
