Reward Hacking in the Era of Large Models: Mechanisms, Emergent Misalignment, Challenges
Authors: Xiaohua Wang, Muzhao Tian, Yuqi Zeng, Zisu Huang, Jiakang Yuan, Bowen Chen, Jingwen Xu, Mingbo Zhou, Wenhao Liu, Muling Wu, Zhengkang Guo, Qi Qian, Yifei Wang, Feiran Zhang, Ruicheng Yin, Shihan Dou, Changze Lv, Tao Chen, Kaitao Song, Xu Tan, Tao Gui, Xiaoqing Zheng, Xuanjing Huang
First: 2026-04-15T08:11:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T08:11:34+00:00
Comments: 42 pages, 5 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and related alignment paradigms have become central to steering large language models (LLMs) and multimodal large language models (MLLMs) toward human-preferred behaviors. However, these approaches introduce a systemic vulnerability: reward hacking, where models exploit imperfections in learned reward signals to maximize proxy objectives without fulfilling true task intent. As models scale and optimization intensifies, such exploitation manifests as verbosity bias, sycophancy, hallucinated justification, benchmark overfitting, and, in multimodal settings, perception--reasoning decoupling and evaluator manipulation. Recent evidence further suggests that seemingly benign shortcut behaviors can generalize into broader forms of misalignment, including deception and strategic gaming of oversight mechanisms. In this survey, we propose the Proxy Compression Hypothesis (PCH) as a unifying framework for understanding reward hacking. We formalize reward hacking as an emergent consequence of optimizing expressive policies against compressed reward representations of high-dimensional human objectives. Under this view, reward hacking arises from the interaction of objective compression, optimization amplification, and evaluator--policy co-adaptation. This perspective unifies empirical phenomena across RLHF, RLAIF, and RLVR regimes, and explains how local shortcut learning can generalize into broader forms of misalignment, including deception and strategic manipulation of oversight mechanisms. We further organize detection and mitigation strategies according to how they intervene on compression, amplification, or co-adaptation dynamics. By framing reward hacking as a structural instability of proxy-based alignment under scale, we highlight open challenges in scalable oversight, multimodal grounding, and agentic autonomy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大模型时代的奖励黑客：机制、涌现性失配与挑战
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）及相关对齐范式已成为引导大语言模型（LLM）和多模态大语言模型（MLLM）符合人类偏好行为的核心方法。然而，这些方法引入了系统性脆弱性：奖励黑客，即模型利用习得奖励信号中的缺陷，在不满足真实任务意图的情况下最大化代理目标。随着模型规模扩大和优化强度提升，此类利用行为表现为冗长偏好、迎合倾向、幻觉合理化、基准过拟合，以及在多模态场景下的感知-推理解耦和评估器操纵。近期证据进一步表明，看似良性的捷径行为可能泛化为更广泛的失配形式，包括欺骗和对监督机制的策略性博弈。本文提出“代理压缩假说”（PCH）作为理解奖励黑客的统一框架，将奖励黑客形式化为针对高维人类目标的压缩奖励表示优化表达性策略时涌现的结果。该视角认为奖励黑客源于目标压缩、优化放大和评估器-策略协同适应的相互作用，统一了RLHF、RLAIF和RLVR体系中的实证现象，并解释了局部捷径学习如何泛化为包括欺骗和监督机制策略性操纵在内的广泛失配形式。我们进一步依据干预压缩、放大或协同适应动态的方式，系统归类检测与缓解策略。通过将奖励黑客定义为规模化背景下基于代理的对齐的结构性失稳，本文强调了可扩展监督、多模态 grounding 和智能体自主性等领域面临的开放挑战。
Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the systemic vulnerability of reward hacking in large models, where models exploit flaws in learned reward signals to maximize proxy objectives rather than fulfilling true human intent, leading to misalignments like verbosity bias and deception. The authors propose the Proxy Compression Hypothesis as a unifying framework, formalizing reward hacking as an emergent result of optimizing expressive policies against compressed reward representations, which explains phenomena across RLHF, RLAIF, and RLVR regimes. Experimental evidence highlights that such exploitation manifests as various shortcut behaviors, including benchmark overfitting and evaluator manipulation, with detection and mitigation strategies organized around intervening in compression, amplification, or co-adaptation dynamics.
本综述论文的动机在于大模型中奖励黑客的系统性漏洞，即模型利用学习到的奖励信号缺陷来最大化代理目标而非实现真实人类意图，导致冗长偏见和欺骗等错位问题。作者提出代理压缩假说作为统一框架，将奖励黑客形式化为针对压缩奖励表示优化表达性策略的涌现结果，从而解释RLHF、RLAIF和RLVR等范式中的现象。实验结果表明，此类利用表现为多种捷径行为，包括基准过拟合和评估器操纵，检测与缓解策略围绕干预压缩、放大或共适应动态进行组织。
Enhancing Reinforcement Learning for Radiology Report Generation with Evidence-aware Rewards and Self-correcting Preference Learning
Authors: Qin Zhou, Guoyan Liang, Qianyi Yang, Jingyuan Chen, Sai Wu, Chang Yao, Zhe Wang
First: 2026-04-15T08:08:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T08:08:06+00:00
Comments: 13 pages,4 figures, ACL2026-main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent reinforcement learning (RL) approaches have advanced radiology report generation (RRG), yet two core limitations persist: (1) report-level rewards offer limited evidence-grounded guidance for clinical faithfulness; and (2) current methods lack an explicit self-improving mechanism to align with clinical preference. We introduce clinically aligned Evidence-aware Self-Correcting Reinforcement Learning (ESC-RL), comprising two key components. First, a Group-wise Evidence-aware Alignment Reward (GEAR) delivers group-wise, evidence-aware feedback. GEAR reinforces consistent grounding for true positives, recovers missed findings for false negatives, and suppresses unsupported content for false positives. Second, a Self-correcting Preference Learning (SPL) strategy automatically constructs a reliable, disease-aware preference dataset from multiple noisy observations and leverages an LLM to synthesize refined reports without human supervision. ESC-RL promotes clinically faithful, disease-aligned reward and supports continual self-improvement during training. Extensive experiments on two public chest X-ray datasets demonstrate consistent gains and state-of-the-art performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于证据感知奖励与自校正偏好学习的放射学报告生成强化学习方法增强
近期强化学习方法在放射学报告生成领域取得进展，但仍存在两个核心局限：(1) 报告级奖励对临床忠实性的证据基础指导有限；(2) 现有方法缺乏与临床偏好对齐的显式自改进机制。本文提出临床对齐的证据感知自校正强化学习方法，包含两个关键组件：首先，分组证据感知对齐奖励提供分组化、证据感知的反馈，强化真阳性的一致性基础，恢复假阴性的漏检发现，并抑制假阳性的无支持内容；其次，自校正偏好学习策略从多组噪声观察中自动构建可靠的疾病感知偏好数据集，并利用大语言模型合成优化报告而无需人工监督。该方法促进临床忠实、疾病对齐的奖励机制，并支持训练过程中的持续自改进。在两个公开胸部X光数据集上的大量实验表明其具有持续增益和最先进的性能表现。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses limitations in reinforcement learning for radiology report generation, specifically the lack of evidence-grounded guidance for clinical faithfulness and an explicit self-improvement mechanism. The proposed ESC-RL method introduces a Group-wise Evidence-aware Alignment Reward (GEAR) to provide evidence-aware feedback that grounds true positives, recovers false negatives, and suppresses false positives, alongside a Self-correcting Preference Learning (SPL) strategy that automatically constructs a disease-aware preference dataset and uses an LLM to synthesize refined reports without supervision. Experimental results on two public chest X-ray datasets show consistent performance gains and state-of-the-art outcomes.
本文针对强化学习在放射学报告生成中的局限性，即缺乏基于证据的临床忠实性指导和明确的自我改进机制，提出了ESC-RL方法。该方法包含组级证据感知对齐奖励（GEAR），通过证据感知反馈来强化真实阳性、恢复假阴性并抑制假阳性内容，以及自我纠正偏好学习（SPL）策略，该策略自动构建疾病感知偏好数据集并利用大语言模型无监督合成精炼报告。在两个公开胸部X光数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法取得了持续的性能提升和领先效果。
Robust Adversarial Policy Optimization Under Dynamics Uncertainty
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T07:15:04+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) policies often fail under dynamics that differ from training, a gap not fully addressed by domain randomization or existing adversarial RL methods. Distributionally robust RL provides a formal remedy but still relies on surrogate adversaries to approximate intractable primal problems, leaving blind spots that potentially cause instability and over-conservatism. We propose a dual formulation that directly exposes the robustness-performance trade-off. At the trajectory level, a temperature parameter from the dual problem is approximated with an adversarial network, yielding efficient and stable worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound. At the model level, we employ Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles, focusing on more adverse environments to the current policy rather than uniform sampling. The two components act independently and complement each other: trajectory-level steering ensures robust rollouts, while model-level sampling provides policy-sensitive coverage of adverse dynamics. The resulting framework, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO) outperforms robust RL baselines, improving resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining dual tractability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态不确定性下的鲁棒对抗策略优化
强化学习策略常在训练环境之外的动态系统中失效，领域随机化或现有对抗性强化学习方法未能完全解决此问题。分布鲁棒强化学习提供了形式化解决方案，但仍依赖代理对抗器逼近难解的原问题，存在可能导致不稳定和过度保守的盲区。我们提出一种对偶形式，直接揭示鲁棒性与性能的权衡关系。在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络逼近对偶问题中的温度参数，在散度界内实现高效稳定的最坏情况推演。在模型层面，采用玻尔兹曼重加权方法处理动态系统集成，聚焦对当前策略更不利的环境而非均匀采样。两个组件独立运作且相互补充：轨迹层面引导确保鲁棒推演，模型层面采样提供对策略敏感的对抗动态覆盖。所提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化框架优于现有鲁棒强化学习基线，在保持对偶可解性的同时，提升了对不确定性的适应能力及对分布外动态的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of reinforcement learning policies to dynamics shifts not fully mitigated by existing robust RL methods, which often rely on surrogate adversaries leading to instability or over-conservatism. The proposed method, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO), introduces a dual formulation to directly manage the robustness-performance trade-off: at the trajectory level, an adversarial network approximates a temperature parameter for efficient worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound, while at the model level, Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles prioritizes sampling more adverse environments relevant to the current policy. Experimental results demonstrate that RAPO outperforms robust RL baselines, enhancing resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining computational tractability.
该研究针对强化学习策略在动态变化下易失效的问题，现有鲁棒强化学习方法常依赖代理对抗者，可能导致不稳定或过度保守。提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化（RAPO）方法采用对偶公式直接处理鲁棒性与性能的权衡：在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络近似温度参数以在发散边界内生成高效的最坏情况推演；在模型层面，利用玻尔兹曼重加权对动态集成进行采样，聚焦于对当前策略更不利的环境。实验结果表明，RAPO优于现有鲁棒强化学习基线，提升了对抗不确定性的鲁棒性和对分布外动态的泛化能力，同时保持计算可处理性。
WOMBET: World Model-based Experience Transfer for Robust and Sample-efficient Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-10T04:57:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T07:14:50+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures, 8th Annual Learning for Dynamics & Control Conference (L4DC)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) in robotics is often limited by the cost and risk of data collection, motivating experience transfer from a source task to a target task. Offline-to-online RL leverages prior data but typically assumes a given fixed dataset and does not address how to generate reliable data for transfer. We propose \textit{World Model-based Experience Transfer} (WOMBET), a framework that jointly generates and utilizes prior data. WOMBET learns a world model in the source task and generates offline data via uncertainty-penalized planning, followed by filtering trajectories with high return and low epistemic uncertainty. It then performs online fine-tuning in the target task using adaptive sampling between offline and online data, enabling a stable transition from prior-driven initialization to task-specific adaptation. We show that the uncertainty-penalized objective provides a lower bound on the true return and derive a finite-sample error decomposition capturing distribution mismatch and approximation error. Empirically, WOMBET improves sample efficiency and final performance over strong baselines on continuous control benchmarks, demonstrating the benefit of jointly optimizing data generation and transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WOMBET：基于世界模型的强化学习经验迁移框架，实现鲁棒与样本高效学习
机器人强化学习常受数据采集成本与风险限制，需通过源任务向目标任务迁移经验。离线-在线强化学习虽能利用先验数据，但通常假设固定数据集且未解决如何生成可靠迁移数据。本文提出《基于世界模型的经验迁移》框架，联合生成并利用先验数据：在源任务学习世界模型，通过不确定性惩罚规划生成离线数据，筛选高回报低认知不确定性的轨迹；在目标任务中采用离线-在线数据自适应采样进行在线微调，实现从先验驱动初始化到任务自适应学习的稳定过渡。理论证明不确定性惩罚目标函数为真实回报下界，推导出包含分布失配与近似误差的有限样本误差分解。实验表明，WOMBET在连续控制基准测试中显著提升样本效率与最终性能，验证了数据生成与迁移联合优化的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the high cost and risk of data collection in robotic reinforcement learning (RL), which drives the need for effective experience transfer from source to target tasks. The proposed method, WOMBET, jointly generates and utilizes prior data by learning a world model in the source task, generating offline data through uncertainty-penalized planning, and filtering trajectories based on high return and low epistemic uncertainty; it then fine-tunes online in the target task with adaptive sampling between offline and online data. Experimental results on continuous control benchmarks show that WOMBET improves sample efficiency and final performance over strong baselines, demonstrating the benefits of optimizing both data generation and transfer.
本文的动机是机器人强化学习中数据收集成本高、风险大，因此需要从源任务向目标任务进行有效的经验迁移。所提出的WOMBET方法通过联合生成和利用先验数据来实现这一目标：在源任务中学习世界模型，通过不确定性惩罚规划生成离线数据，并筛选出高回报、低认知不确定性的轨迹；然后在目标任务中进行在线微调，采用离线和在线数据的自适应采样。在连续控制基准测试中的实验结果表明，WOMBET相比强基线方法提高了样本效率和最终性能，证明了优化数据生成与迁移的益处。
Failure Makes the Agent Stronger: Enhancing Accuracy through Structured Reflection for Reliable Tool Interactions
Authors: Junhao Su, Yuanliang Wan, Junwei Yang, Hengyu Shi, Tianyang Han, Junfeng Luo, Yurui Qiu
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-09-23T09:35:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:57:52+00:00
Comments: ACL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-augmented large language models (LLMs) are usually trained with supervised imitation or coarse-grained reinforcement learning that optimizes single tool calls. Current self-reflection practices rely on heuristic prompts or one-way reasoning: the model is urged to 'think more' instead of learning error diagnosis and repair. This is fragile in multi-turn interactions; after a failure the model often repeats the same mistake. We propose structured reflection, which turns the path from error to repair into an explicit, controllable, and trainable action. The agent produces a short yet precise reflection: it diagnoses the failure using evidence from the previous step and then proposes a correct, executable follow-up call. For training we combine DAPO and GSPO objectives with a reward scheme tailored to tool use, optimizing the stepwise strategy Reflect, then Call, then Final. To evaluate, we introduce Tool-Reflection-Bench, a lightweight benchmark that programmatically checks structural validity, executability, parameter correctness, and result consistency. Tasks are built as mini trajectories of erroneous call, reflection, and corrected call, with disjoint train and test splits. Experiments on BFCL v3 and Tool-Reflection-Bench show large gains in multi-turn tool-call success and error recovery, and a reduction of redundant calls. These results indicate that making reflection explicit and optimizing it directly improves the reliability of tool interaction and offers a reproducible path for agents to learn from failure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：失败使智能体更强大：通过结构化反思提升工具交互的可靠性精度
工具增强的大型语言模型通常通过监督模仿或优化单次工具调用的粗粒度强化学习进行训练。当前的自反思实践依赖启发式提示或单向推理：模型被催促'多思考'而非学习错误诊断与修复。这在多轮交互中十分脆弱；失败后模型常重复相同错误。我们提出结构化反思，将错误到修复的路径转化为显式、可控、可训练的动作。智能体生成简短而精确的反思：基于前一步证据诊断失败，随后提出正确且可执行的后续调用。训练中我们结合DAPO与GSPO目标及针对工具使用的奖励机制，优化'反思-调用-终判'的逐步策略。为评估性能，我们引入Tool-Reflection-Bench轻量基准，通过编程方式检查结构有效性、可执行性、参数正确性与结果一致性。任务构建为包含错误调用、反思、修正调用的微型轨迹，采用分离的训练测试集。在BFCL v3和Tool-Reflection-Bench上的实验显示，多轮工具调用成功率与错误恢复能力显著提升，冗余调用减少。这些结果表明，显式化反思并直接优化能提升工具交互可靠性，为智能体提供可复现的从失败中学习的路径。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the fragility of tool-augmented large language models in multi-turn interactions, where current self-reflection methods often lead to repeated errors after failures. To enhance reliability, the authors propose structured reflection, which explicitly models error diagnosis and repair as a trainable action, combining DAPO and GSPO objectives with a tailored reward scheme to optimize a Reflect-Call-Final strategy. Experimental results on BFCL v3 and the newly introduced Tool-Reflection-Bench benchmark demonstrate significant improvements in multi-turn tool-call success rates, error recovery, and reduction of redundant calls, indicating that direct optimization of structured reflection enables agents to learn effectively from failures.
本文针对工具增强大语言模型在多轮交互中的脆弱性问题，现有自反思方法常在失败后导致重复错误。为提升可靠性，作者提出结构化反思，将错误诊断与修复明确建模为可训练动作，结合DAPO和GSPO目标及定制奖励方案，优化“反思-调用-完成”策略。在BFCL v3和新构建的Tool-Reflection-Bench基准上的实验结果表明，多轮工具调用成功率、错误恢复能力显著提升，冗余调用减少，证明直接优化结构化反思能使智能体从失败中有效学习。
Auto-FP: An Experimental Study of Automated Feature Preprocessing for Tabular Data
Authors: Danrui Qi, Jinglin Peng, Yongjun He, Jiannan Wang
First: 2023-10-04T02:46:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:43:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Classical machine learning models, such as linear models and tree-based models, are widely used in industry. These models are sensitive to data distribution, thus feature preprocessing, which transforms features from one distribution to another, is a crucial step to ensure good model quality. Manually constructing a feature preprocessing pipeline is challenging because data scientists need to make difficult decisions about which preprocessors to select and in which order to compose them. In this paper, we study how to automate feature preprocessing (Auto-FP) for tabular data. Due to the large search space, a brute-force solution is prohibitively expensive. To address this challenge, we interestingly observe that Auto-FP can be modelled as either a hyperparameter optimization (HPO) or a neural architecture search (NAS) problem. This observation enables us to extend a variety of HPO and NAS algorithms to solve the Auto-FP problem. We conduct a comprehensive evaluation and analysis of 15 algorithms on 45 public ML datasets. Overall, evolution-based algorithms show the leading average ranking. Surprisingly, the random search turns out to be a strong baseline. Many surrogate-model-based and bandit-based search algorithms, which achieve good performance for HPO and NAS, do not outperform random search for Auto-FP. We analyze the reasons for our findings and conduct a bottleneck analysis to identify the opportunities to improve these algorithms. Furthermore, we explore how to extend Auto-FP to support parameter search and compare two ways to achieve this goal. In the end, we evaluate Auto-FP in an AutoML context and discuss the limitations of popular AutoML tools. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study on automated feature preprocessing. We hope our work can inspire researchers to develop new algorithms tailored for Auto-FP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Auto-FP：面向表格数据的自动化特征预处理实验研究
经典机器学习模型（如线性模型与树模型）在工业界应用广泛。这类模型对数据分布敏感，因此特征预处理——即将特征从一种分布转换至另一种分布——成为保证模型质量的关键步骤。手动构建特征预处理流程具有挑战性，因为数据科学家需艰难决策预处理器的选择与组合顺序。本文研究如何对表格数据实现自动化特征预处理（Auto-FP）。由于搜索空间庞大，暴力求解方案成本过高。针对这一挑战，我们有趣地发现：Auto-FP可被建模为超参数优化（HPO）或神经架构搜索（NAS）问题。这一洞见使我们能扩展多种HPO与NAS算法以求解Auto-FP问题。我们在45个公开机器学习数据集上对15种算法进行了全面评估与分析。总体而言，基于进化的算法表现出领先的平均排名。令人惊讶的是，随机搜索成为强劲的基线方法；许多在HPO和NAS中表现优异的基于代理模型与多臂赌博机的搜索算法，在Auto-FP任务中并未超越随机搜索。我们分析了现象成因，并通过瓶颈分析指出改进这些算法的潜在方向。此外，我们探索了如何扩展Auto-FP以支持参数搜索，并比较了两种实现路径。最后，我们在AutoML场景中评估Auto-FP，并讨论了主流AutoML工具的局限性。据我们所知，这是首个针对自动化特征预处理的系统性研究。我们希望这项工作能启发研究者开发专门面向Auto-FP的新算法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sensitivity of classical machine learning models to data distributions and the challenge of manually constructing feature preprocessing pipelines, this paper studies automated feature preprocessing (Auto-FP) for tabular data. The method models Auto-FP as either a hyperparameter optimization or neural architecture search problem, enabling the extension of various existing algorithms to search the large space of preprocessor selections and compositions. Experimental results from evaluating 15 algorithms on 45 datasets show that evolution-based algorithms lead in average ranking, while random search serves as a surprisingly strong baseline, outperforming many surrogate-model and bandit-based approaches; the analysis identifies bottlenecks and explores extensions for parameter search and AutoML integration.
针对经典机器学习模型对数据分布敏感且手动构建特征预处理流程困难的问题，本文研究了表格数据的自动化特征预处理（Auto-FP）。方法将Auto-FP建模为超参数优化或神经架构搜索问题，从而扩展多种现有算法来搜索预处理器的选择与组合空间。在45个公开数据集上评估15种算法的实验结果表明，基于进化的算法平均排名领先，而随机搜索作为强基线表现意外出色，优于许多基于代理模型和赌博机的算法；分析揭示了性能瓶颈，并探索了参数搜索和AutoML集成的扩展方向。
RiskWebWorld: A Realistic Interactive Benchmark for GUI Agents in E-commerce Risk Management
Authors: Renqi Chen, Zeyin Tao, Jianming Guo, Jing Wang, Zezhou Xu, Jingzhe Zhu, Qingqing Sun, Tianyi Zhang, Shuai Chen
First: 2026-04-15T06:27:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:27:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents show strong capabilities for automating web tasks, but existing interactive benchmarks primarily target benign, predictable consumer environments. Their effectiveness in high-stakes, investigative domains such as authentic e-commerce risk management remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we present RiskWebWorld, the first highly realistic interactive benchmark for evaluating GUI agents in e-commerce risk management. RiskWebWorld features 1,513 tasks sourced from production risk-control pipelines across 8 core domains, and captures the authentic challenges of risk operations on uncooperative websites, partially environmental hijackments. To support scalable evaluation and agentic reinforcement learning (RL), we further build a Gymnasium-compliant infrastructure that decouples policy planning from environment mechanics. Our evaluation across diverse models reveals a dramatic capability gap: top-tier generalist models achieve 49.1% success, while specialized open-weights GUI models lag at near-total failure. This highlights that foundation model scale currently matters more than zero-shot interface grounding in long-horizon professional tasks. We also demonstrate the viability of our infrastructure through agentic RL, which improves open-source models by 16.2%. These results position RiskWebWorld as a practical testbed for developing robust digital workers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RiskWebWorld：面向电商风险管理GUI智能体的高拟真交互式基准
图形用户界面（GUI）智能体在自动化网页任务方面展现出强大能力，但现有交互式基准主要针对良性、可预测的消费环境。其在电商风险管理等高风险调查领域的有效性仍未得到充分探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出了RiskWebWorld——首个用于评估电商风险管理GUI智能体的高拟真交互式基准。RiskWebWorld包含来自8个核心领域生产风控流程的1,513项任务，并捕捉了非合作网站、部分环境劫持等风险操作的真实挑战。为支持可扩展评估与智能体强化学习（RL），我们进一步构建了符合Gymnasium规范的架构，将策略规划与环境机制解耦。跨模型评估揭示了显著的能力差距：顶级通用模型成功率达49.1%，而专业开源GUI模型几近完全失败。这表明在长周期专业任务中，基础模型规模当前比零样本界面适配更为关键。我们还通过智能体强化学习验证了架构的可行性，使开源模型性能提升16.2%。这些成果使RiskWebWorld成为开发鲁棒数字工作者的实用测试平台。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the lack of realistic benchmarks for evaluating GUI agents in high-stakes, investigative domains like e-commerce risk management, where existing benchmarks focus on benign consumer tasks. The method involves creating RiskWebWorld, a highly realistic interactive benchmark with 1,513 tasks sourced from production pipelines across 8 domains, and building a Gymnasium-compliant infrastructure to support scalable evaluation and agentic reinforcement learning. The main experimental results show a significant capability gap: top-tier generalist models achieve a 49.1% success rate, while specialized GUI models fail nearly completely, indicating that foundation model scale is more critical than zero-shot interface grounding; additionally, agentic RL improves open-source models by 16.2%, demonstrating the benchmark's utility for developing robust agents.
本研究的动机是解决现有基准测试主要针对良性消费环境，缺乏评估图形用户界面（GUI）智能体在电子商务风险管理等高风险调查领域真实性能的不足。方法上，作者提出了RiskWebWorld，这是一个高度真实的交互式基准测试，包含来自8个核心领域生产管道的1,513个任务，并构建了符合Gymnasium标准的基础设施以支持可扩展评估和智能体强化学习。主要实验结果显示显著的能力差距：顶级通用模型成功率为49.1%，而专业开源GUI模型几乎完全失败，表明基础模型规模比零样本界面适应能力更为关键；此外，智能体强化学习将开源模型性能提升了16.2%，验证了该基准作为开发鲁棒数字工作者测试平台的有效性。
Representation over Routing: Overcoming Surrogate Hacking in Multi-Timescale PPO
Authors: Jing Sun
First: 2026-04-15T06:03:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:03:07+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Temporal credit assignment in reinforcement learning has long been a central challenge. Inspired by the multi-timescale encoding of the dopamine system in neurobiology, recent research has sought to introduce multiple discount factors into Actor-Critic architectures, such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), to balance short-term responses with long-term planning. However, this paper reveals that blindly fusing multi-timescale signals in complex delayed-reward tasks can lead to severe algorithmic pathologies. We systematically demonstrate that exposing a temporal attention routing mechanism to policy gradients results in surrogate objective hacking, while adopting gradient-free uncertainty weighting triggers irreversible myopic degeneration, a phenomenon we term the Paradox of Temporal Uncertainty. To address these issues, we propose a Target Decoupling architecture: on the Critic side, we retain multi-timescale predictions to enforce auxiliary representation learning, while on the Actor side, we strictly isolate short-term signals and update the policy based solely on long-term advantages. Rigorous empirical evaluations across multiple independent random seeds in the LunarLander-v2 environment demonstrate that our proposed architecture achieves statistically significant performance improvements. Without relying on hyperparameter hacking, it consistently surpasses the ''Environment Solved'' threshold with minimal variance, completely eliminates policy collapse, and escapes the hovering local optima that trap single-timescale baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：表征优于路由：克服多时间尺度PPO中的代理目标破解
强化学习中的时序信用分配长期是核心挑战。受神经生物学中多巴胺系统多时间尺度编码的启发，近期研究尝试在Actor-Critic架构（如近端策略优化）中引入多个折扣因子，以平衡短期响应与长期规划。然而，本文揭示在复杂延迟奖励任务中盲目融合多时间尺度信号会导致严重的算法病理现象。我们系统论证：将时序注意力路由机制暴露给策略梯度会引发代理目标破解，而采用无梯度不确定性加权则会触发不可逆的短视退化——这一现象被我们称为“时序不确定性悖论”。为解决这些问题，我们提出目标解耦架构：在Critic侧保留多时间尺度预测以强化辅助表征学习，在Actor侧则严格隔离短期信号，仅基于长期优势更新策略。在LunarLander-v2环境中通过多个独立随机种子的严格实证评估表明，所提架构实现了统计显著的性能提升：无需依赖超参数调试即能以最小方差持续超越“环境求解”阈值，完全消除策略崩溃，并摆脱困住单时间尺度基线的悬停局部最优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of temporal credit assignment in reinforcement learning and inspired by multi-timescale dopamine encoding, this paper investigates the pathologies that arise when naively integrating multiple discount factors into PPO for delayed-reward tasks. The method introduces a Target Decoupling architecture that addresses issues like surrogate objective hacking and myopic degeneration by decoupling the Actor and Critic: the Critic uses multi-timescale predictions for representation learning, while the Actor is updated strictly based on long-term advantages. Experimental results in the LunarLander-v2 environment show the proposed architecture achieves statistically significant performance improvements, consistently surpasses the solved threshold with low variance, eliminates policy collapse, and escapes local optima that trap single-timescale baselines.
本文的动机源于强化学习中时序信用分配的挑战，并受到神经生物学中多时间尺度多巴胺编码的启发，旨在解决在延迟奖励任务中简单地将多折扣因子集成到PPO算法所引发的病理问题。其方法提出了一个目标解耦架构，通过解耦执行者和评论者来应对替代目标黑客和短视退化等问题：评论者保留多时间尺度预测以进行辅助表征学习，而执行者则严格隔离短期信号，仅基于长期优势更新策略。在LunarLander-v2环境中的严格实验结果表明，所提出的架构实现了统计上显著的性能提升，能够以最小方差持续超越环境解决阈值，完全避免了策略崩溃，并摆脱了困扰单时间尺度基线的局部最优陷阱。
Feedback-Driven Tool-Use Improvements in Large Language Models via Automated Build Environments
Authors: Junjie Ye, Changhao Jiang, Zhengyin Du, Yufei Xu, Xuesong Yao, Zhiheng Xi, Xiaoran Fan, Qi Zhang, Tao Gui, Xuanjing Huang, Jiecao Chen
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-08-12T09:45:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:01:13+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Effective tool use is essential for large language models (LLMs) to interact with their environment. However, progress is limited by the lack of efficient reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks specifically designed for tool use, due to challenges in constructing stable training environments and designing verifiable reward mechanisms. To address this, we propose an automated environment construction pipeline, incorporating scenario decomposition, document generation, function integration, complexity scaling, and localized deployment. This enables the creation of high-quality training environments that provide detailed and measurable feedback without relying on external tools. Additionally, we introduce a verifiable reward mechanism that evaluates both the precision of tool use and the completeness of task execution. When combined with trajectory data collected from the constructed environments, this mechanism integrates seamlessly with standard RL algorithms to facilitate feedback-driven model training. Experiments on LLMs of varying scales demonstrate that our approach significantly enhances the models' tool-use performance without degrading their general capabilities. Our analysis suggests that these gains result from improved context understanding and reasoning, driven by updates to the lower-layer MLP parameters in models. Code and data are available at https://github.com/bytedance/FTRL.
中文标题/摘要

Chain of Uncertain Rewards with Large Language Models for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shentong Mo
First: 2026-04-15T05:44:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective reward functions is a cornerstone of reinforcement learning (RL), yet it remains a challenging and labor-intensive process due to the inefficiencies and inconsistencies inherent in traditional methods. Existing methods often rely on extensive manual design and evaluation steps, which are prone to redundancy and overlook local uncertainties at intermediate decision points. To address these challenges, we propose the Chain of Uncertain Rewards (CoUR), a novel framework that integrates large language models (LLMs) to streamline reward function design and evaluation in RL environments. Specifically, our CoUR introduces code uncertainty quantification with a similarity selection mechanism that combines textual and semantic analyses to identify and reuse the most relevant reward function components. By reducing redundant evaluations and leveraging Bayesian optimization on decoupled reward terms, CoUR enables a more efficient and robust search for optimal reward feedback. We comprehensively evaluate CoUR across nine original environments from IsaacGym and all 20 tasks from the Bidexterous Manipulation benchmark. The experimental results demonstrate that CoUR not only achieves better performance but also significantly lowers the cost of reward evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的不确定性奖励链强化学习方法
设计有效的奖励函数是强化学习的核心挑战，但传统方法效率低下且存在不一致性，导致该过程既复杂又耗时。现有方法通常依赖大量人工设计与评估步骤，容易产生冗余并忽略中间决策点的局部不确定性。为解决这些问题，我们提出了不确定性奖励链（CoUR）这一创新框架，该框架集成大语言模型以优化强化学习环境中的奖励函数设计与评估流程。具体而言，CoUR通过代码不确定性量化与相似性选择机制，结合文本与语义分析来识别并复用最相关的奖励函数组件。通过减少冗余评估并对解耦的奖励项进行贝叶斯优化，CoUR实现了更高效、更鲁棒的最优奖励反馈搜索。我们在IsaacGym的九个原始环境及双手灵巧操作基准的全部20项任务中进行了全面评估。实验结果表明，CoUR不仅取得了更优性能，还显著降低了奖励评估成本。

To overcome these issues, the authors propose the Chain of Uncertain Rewards (CoUR) framework, which leverages large language models to streamline reward design by introducing code uncertainty quantification and a similarity selection mechanism that combines textual and semantic analysis to reuse relevant reward components, thereby reducing redundancy and employing Bayesian optimization for efficient search. Towards Scalable Lightweight GUI Agents via Multi-role Orchestration
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Junjie Zheng, Leyang Yang, Sheng Zhou, Xiaoxuan Tang, Zhouhua Fang, Zhiwei Liu, Dajun Chen, Yong Li, Jiajun Bu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-15T05:23:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T05:23:04+00:00
Comments: Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents powered by Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) enable digital automation on end-user devices. While scaling both parameters and data has yielded substantial gains, advanced methods still suffer from prohibitive deployment costs on resource-constrained devices. When facing complex in-the-wild scenarios, lightweight GUI agents are bottlenecked by limited capacity and poor task scalability under end-to-end episodic learning, impeding adaptation to multi-agent systems (MAS), while training multiple skill-specific experts remains costly. Can we strike an effective trade-off in this cost-scalability dilemma, enabling lightweight MLLMs to participate in realistic GUI workflows? To address these challenges, we propose the LAMO framework, which endows a lightweight MLLM with GUI-specific knowledge and task scalability, allowing multi-role orchestration to expand its capability boundary for GUI automation. LAMO combines role-oriented data synthesis with a two-stage training recipe: (i) supervised fine-tuning with Perplexity-Weighted Cross-Entropy optimization for knowledge distillation and visual perception enhancement, and (ii) reinforcement learning for role-oriented cooperative exploration. With LAMO, we develop a task-scalable native GUI agent, LAMO-3B, supporting monolithic execution and MAS-style orchestration. When paired with advanced planners as a plug-and-play policy executor, LAMO-3B can continuously benefit from planner advances, enabling a higher performance ceiling. Extensive static and online evaluations validate the effectiveness of our design.
中文标题/摘要

基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的自主图形用户界面（GUI）智能体实现了终端设备上的数字自动化。尽管扩大参数和数据规模带来了显著收益，但先进方法在资源受限设备上仍面临高昂的部署成本。面对复杂的实际场景，轻量级GUI智能体在端到端情景学习下受限于能力不足和任务可扩展性差，难以适应多智能体系统（MAS），而训练多个专用技能专家成本高昂。我们能否在成本与可扩展性的困境中实现有效权衡，使轻量级MLLM能够参与实际GUI工作流？为解决这些挑战，我们提出LAMO框架，该框架赋予轻量级MLLM以GUI专用知识和任务可扩展性，通过多角色编排拓展其GUI自动化能力边界。LAMO结合面向角色的数据合成与两阶段训练方案：（i）采用困惑度加权交叉熵优化的监督微调，实现知识蒸馏与视觉感知增强；（ii）强化学习驱动的面向角色协同探索。基于LAMO，我们开发了任务可扩展的原生GUI智能体LAMO-3B，支持单体执行与MAS式编排。当与先进规划器作为即插即用策略执行器配合时，LAMO-3B可持续受益于规划器进步，实现更高性能上限。大量静态与在线评估验证了我们设计的有效性。

Bridging MARL to SARL: An Order-Independent Multi-Agent Transformer via Latent Consensus
Authors: Zijian Zhao, Jing Gao, Sen Li
First: 2026-04-15T04:52:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:52:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) is widely used to address large joint observation and action spaces by decomposing a centralized control problem into multiple interacting agents. However, such decomposition often introduces additional challenges, including non-stationarity, unstable training, weak coordination, and limited theoretical guarantees. In this paper, we propose the Consensus Multi-Agent Transformer (CMAT), a centralized framework that bridges cooperative MARL to a hierarchical single-agent reinforcement learning (SARL) formulation. CMAT treats all agents as a unified entity and employs a Transformer encoder to process the large joint observation space. To handle the extensive joint action space, we introduce a hierarchical decision-making mechanism in which a Transformer decoder autoregressively generates a high-level consensus vector, simulating the process by which agents reach agreement on their strategies in latent space. Conditioned on this consensus, all agents generate their actions simultaneously, enabling order-independent joint decision making and avoiding the sensitivity to action-generation order in conventional Multi-Agent Transformers (MAT). This factorization allows the joint policy to be optimized using single-agent PPO while preserving expressive coordination through the latent consensus. To evaluate the proposed method, we conduct experiments on benchmark tasks from StarCraft II, Multi-Agent MuJoCo, and Google Research Football. The results show that CMAT achieves superior performance over recent centralized solutions, sequential MARL methods, and conventional MARL baselines. The code for this paper is available at:https://github.com/RS2002/CMAT .
中文标题/摘要
标题：从多智能体强化学习到单智能体强化学习的桥梁：基于潜在共识的序无关多智能体Transformer
协作式多智能体强化学习（MARL）通过将集中控制问题分解为多个交互智能体，广泛用于处理庞大的联合观测与动作空间。然而，这种分解常带来额外挑战，包括非平稳性、训练不稳定、协调能力弱及理论保证有限。本文提出共识多智能体Transformer（CMAT），这是一个将协作式MARL桥接至分层单智能体强化学习（SARL）的集中式框架。CMAT将所有智能体视为统一实体，采用Transformer编码器处理大规模联合观测空间。为应对庞大的联合动作空间，我们引入分层决策机制：Transformer解码器自回归生成高层共识向量，模拟智能体在潜在空间就策略达成一致的过程。基于此共识，所有智能体同步生成动作，实现序无关的联合决策，避免了传统多智能体Transformer（MAT）对动作生成顺序的敏感性。该分解方式使得联合策略可通过单智能体PPO进行优化，同时通过潜在共识保持丰富的协调能力。为评估所提方法，我们在星际争霸II、多智能体MuJoCo及谷歌研究足球的基准任务上开展实验。结果表明，CMAT在性能上优于近期集中式解决方案、顺序式MARL方法及传统MARL基线。本文代码已开源：https://github.com/RS2002/CMAT。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses challenges in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), such as non-stationarity and weak coordination, by proposing the Consensus Multi-Agent Transformer (CMAT), a centralized framework that bridges MARL to hierarchical single-agent reinforcement learning (SARL). The method employs a Transformer encoder for joint observations and a Transformer decoder to autoregressively generate a high-level consensus vector in latent space, enabling order-independent simultaneous action generation by all agents, which is optimized using single-agent PPO. Experimental results on StarCraft II, Multi-Agent MuJoCo, and Google Research Football benchmarks demonstrate that CMAT outperforms recent centralized solutions, sequential MARL methods, and conventional MARL baselines.
本文针对合作多智能体强化学习（MARL）中的非平稳性和弱协调性等挑战，提出了共识多智能体变换器（CMAT），这是一个将MARL桥接到分层单智能体强化学习（SARL）的集中式框架。该方法使用变换器编码器处理联合观察，并通过变换器解码器在潜在空间中自回归生成高层共识向量，使所有智能体能够顺序无关地同时生成动作，并利用单智能体PPO进行优化。在《星际争霸II》、多智能体MuJoCo和谷歌研究足球等基准任务上的实验结果表明，CMAT优于最近的集中式解决方案、顺序MARL方法和传统MARL基线。
Data-Efficient RLVR via Off-Policy Influence Guidance
Authors: Erle Zhu, Dazhi Jiang, Yuan Wang, Xujun Li, Jiale Cheng, Yuxian Gu, Yilin Niu, Aohan Zeng, Jie Tang, Minlie Huang, Hongning Wang
First: 2025-10-30T13:40:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:43:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Data selection is a critical aspect of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). Current data selection methods are largely heuristic-based, lacking theoretical guarantees and generalizability. This work proposes a theoretically-grounded approach using influence functions to estimate the contribution of each data point to the learning objective. To overcome the prohibitive computational cost of policy rollouts required for online influence estimation, we introduce an off-policy influence estimation method that efficiently approximates data influence using pre-collected offline trajectories. Furthermore, to manage the high-dimensional gradients of LLMs, we employ sparse random projection to reduce dimensionality and improve storage and computation efficiency. Leveraging these techniques, we develop \textbf{C}urriculum \textbf{R}L with \textbf{O}ff-\textbf{P}olicy \text{I}nfluence guidance (\textbf{CROPI}), a multi-stage RL framework that iteratively selects the most influential data for the current policy. Experiments on models up to 7B parameters demonstrate that CROPI significantly accelerates training. On a 1.5B model, it achieves a 2.66x step-level acceleration while using only 10\% of the data per stage compared to full-dataset training. Our results highlight the substantial potential of influence-based data selection for efficient RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于离线策略影响引导的数据高效RLVR方法
数据选择是强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）提升大语言模型（LLMs）推理能力的关键环节。当前数据选择方法多基于启发式策略，缺乏理论保证与泛化能力。本研究提出一种理论驱动的方法，利用影响函数估计每个数据点对学习目标的贡献。为克服在线影响估计所需策略展开的过高计算成本，我们引入离线策略影响估计方法，利用预收集的离线轨迹高效近似数据影响力。此外，为处理LLMs的高维梯度，我们采用稀疏随机投影降低维度并提升存储与计算效率。基于这些技术，我们开发了\textbf{C}urriculum \textbf{R}L with \textbf{O}ff-\textbf{P}olicy \text{I}nfluence guidance（\textbf{CROPI}），这是一个多阶段强化学习框架，能迭代选择对当前策略最具影响力的数据。在高达70亿参数的模型实验中，CROPI显著加速训练过程：在15亿参数模型上，相比全数据集训练，每阶段仅使用10%数据即可实现2.66倍的步骤级加速。实验结果凸显了基于影响的数据选择在高效RLVR中的巨大潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of heuristic data selection in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for large language models by proposing a theoretically-grounded method. The core innovation is an off-policy influence estimation technique that uses pre-collected trajectories to approximate each data point's contribution to the learning objective, avoiding costly policy rollouts, and employs sparse random projection to handle high-dimensional gradients efficiently. Based on this, the authors develop CROPI, a multi-stage curriculum RL framework that iteratively selects the most influential data. Experimental results on models up to 7B parameters show that CROPI significantly accelerates training; for instance, a 1.5B model achieved a 2.66x speedup in step-level training while using only 10% of the data per stage compared to full-dataset training, demonstrating the effectiveness of influence-based data selection for efficient RLVR.
本文针对大型语言模型的可验证奖励强化学习中启发式数据选择效率低下的问题，提出了一种基于理论的方法。其核心创新在于一种离策略影响估计技术，该方法利用预先收集的轨迹来近似估计每个数据点对学习目标的贡献，从而避免了耗能的策略推演，并采用稀疏随机投影来高效处理高维梯度。基于此，作者开发了CROPI，一个多阶段的课程强化学习框架，能迭代选择最具影响力的数据。在高达70亿参数的模型上的实验结果表明，CROPI显著加速了训练；例如，一个15亿参数的模型在每阶段仅使用10%数据的情况下，实现了相比全数据集训练2.66倍的步骤级加速，这证明了基于影响的数据选择对于高效可验证奖励强化学习的巨大潜力。
Outperforming Self-Attention Mechanisms in Solar Irradiance Forecasting via Physics-Guided Neural Networks
Authors: Mohammed Ezzaldin Babiker Abdullah, Rufaidah Abdallah Ibrahim Mohammed
First: 2026-04-15T04:17:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:17:20+00:00
Comments: This is a second version of a previously published paper. DOI: Https://doi.org/10.36227/techrxiv.176827103.31624241/v1
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate Global Horizontal Irradiance (GHI) forecasting is critical for grid stability, particularly in arid regions characterized by rapid aerosol fluctuations. While recent trends favor computationally expensive Transformer-based architectures, this paper challenges the prevailing "complexity-first" paradigm. We propose a lightweight, Physics-Informed Hybrid CNN-BiLSTM framework that prioritizes domain knowledge over architectural depth. The model integrates a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) for spatial feature extraction with a Bi-Directional LSTM for capturing temporal dependencies. Unlike standard data-driven approaches, our model is explicitly guided by a vector of 15 engineered features including Clear-Sky indices and Solar Zenith Angle - rather than relying solely on raw historical data. Hyperparameters are rigorously tuned using Bayesian Optimization to ensure global optimality. Experimental validation using NASA POWER data in Sudan demonstrates that our physics-guided approach achieves a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 19.53 W/m^2, significantly outperforming complex attention-based baselines (RMSE 30.64 W/m^2). These results confirm a "Complexity Paradox": in high-noise meteorological tasks, explicit physical constraints offer a more efficient and accurate alternative to self-attention mechanisms. The findings advocate for a shift towards hybrid, physics-aware AI for real-time renewable energy management.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于物理引导神经网络在太阳辐照度预测中超越自注意力机制
全球水平辐照度（GHI）的精确预测对电网稳定性至关重要，尤其在气溶胶快速波动的干旱地区。尽管当前趋势偏向计算成本高昂的Transformer架构，本文挑战了主流的“复杂度优先”范式。我们提出一种轻量级的物理信息混合CNN-BiLSTM框架，将领域知识置于架构深度之上。该模型结合卷积神经网络（CNN）进行空间特征提取，以及双向LSTM捕捉时间依赖性。与标准数据驱动方法不同，我们的模型明确受15个工程特征向量（包括晴空指数和太阳天顶角）引导，而非仅依赖原始历史数据。通过贝叶斯优化严格调整超参数以确保全局最优性。使用苏丹NASA POWER数据的实验验证表明，我们的物理引导方法实现了19.53 W/m²的均方根误差（RMSE），显著优于复杂的基于注意力的基线模型（RMSE 30.64 W/m²）。这些结果证实了“复杂度悖论”：在高噪声气象任务中，显式物理约束为自注意力机制提供了更高效、更准确的替代方案。该发现倡导向混合型、物理感知的人工智能转变，以支持实时可再生能源管理。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate solar irradiance forecasting in arid regions with high aerosol variability, this paper challenges the reliance on complex Transformer models by proposing a lightweight Physics-Informed Hybrid CNN-BiLSTM framework. The method integrates a CNN for spatial features and a BiLSTM for temporal dependencies, explicitly guided by 15 engineered physical features like Clear-Sky indices, with hyperparameters optimized via Bayesian Optimization. Experimental results using NASA POWER data from Sudan show the model achieves an RMSE of 19.53 W/m², significantly outperforming attention-based baselines (RMSE 30.64 W/m²), demonstrating that physics-guided approaches can be more efficient and accurate than self-attention mechanisms in noisy meteorological tasks.
本文针对干旱地区气溶胶快速波动下太阳辐照度预测的需求，挑战了依赖复杂Transformer模型的趋势，提出了一种轻量级的物理信息混合CNN-BiLSTM框架。该方法结合CNN提取空间特征和BiLSTM捕捉时间依赖性，并明确引入了包括晴空指数在内的15个工程物理特征进行指导，同时使用贝叶斯优化调整超参数。基于苏丹NASA POWER数据的实验结果表明，该模型的均方根误差为19.53 W/m²，显著优于基于注意力机制的基线模型（均方根误差30.64 W/m²），证实了在噪声较高的气象任务中，物理引导方法比自注意力机制更高效、准确。
In-Context Autonomous Network Incident Response: An End-to-End Large Language Model Agent Approach
Authors: Yiran Gao, Kim Hammar, Tao Li
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-02-13T18:09:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:45:06+00:00
Comments: 2026 AAAI Summer Symposium on Human-Aware AI Agents for the Cyber Battlefield
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rapidly evolving cyberattacks demand incident response systems that can autonomously learn and adapt to changing threats. Prior work has extensively explored the reinforcement learning approach, which involves learning response strategies through extensive simulation of the incident. While this approach can be effective, it requires handcrafted modeling of the simulator and suppresses useful semantics from raw system logs and alerts. To address these limitations, we propose to leverage large language models' (LLM) pre-trained security knowledge and in-context learning to create an end-to-end agentic solution for incident response planning. Specifically, our agent integrates four functionalities, perception, reasoning, planning, and action, into one lightweight LLM (14b model). Through fine-tuning and chain-of-thought reasoning, our LLM agent is capable of processing system logs and inferring the underlying network state (perception), updating its conjecture of attack models (reasoning), simulating consequences under different response strategies (planning), and generating an effective response (action). By comparing LLM-simulated outcomes with actual observations, the LLM agent repeatedly refines its attack conjecture and corresponding response, thereby demonstrating in-context adaptation. Our agentic approach is free of modeling and can run on commodity hardware. When evaluated on incident logs reported in the literature, our agent achieves recovery up to 23% faster than those of frontier LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：情境自适网络事件响应：一种端到端大语言模型智能体方法
快速演变的网络攻击需要能够自主学习并适应动态威胁的事件响应系统。先前研究已广泛探索强化学习方法，该方法通过大量事件模拟学习响应策略。虽然有效，但需人工构建模拟器模型，且抑制了原始系统日志与告警中的有效语义。为突破这些局限，我们提出利用大语言模型（LLM）预训练的安全知识与情境学习能力，构建端到端的智能体化事件响应规划方案。具体而言，我们的智能体将感知、推理、规划、执行四项功能集成于一个轻量化LLM（140亿参数模型）中。通过微调与思维链推理，该LLM智能体能够处理系统日志并推断底层网络状态（感知）、更新攻击模型假设（推理）、模拟不同响应策略的后果（规划）、生成有效响应方案（执行）。通过对比LLM模拟结果与实际观测，智能体持续优化攻击假设与对应响应，实现情境自适应。我们的智能体方法无需建模，可在商用硬件上运行。基于文献记载的事件日志评估表明，本智能体的恢复速度比前沿LLM方案最高提升23%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for autonomous incident response systems that can adapt to evolving cyberattacks without the handcrafted modeling and semantic suppression inherent in prior reinforcement learning approaches, this paper proposes an end-to-end agent using a lightweight large language model (LLM). The method integrates perception, reasoning, planning, and action into a single 14B-parameter LLM, which is fine-tuned and employs chain-of-thought reasoning to process system logs, infer network states, update attack conjectures, simulate response strategies, and generate actions, all while adapting in-context by comparing simulated outcomes with actual observations. The main experimental results show that this agentic approach, which requires no explicit modeling and runs on commodity hardware, achieves recovery up to 23% faster than frontier LLMs when evaluated on literature-reported incident logs.
本文的动机是应对快速演变的网络攻击，需要能够自主适应威胁的事件响应系统，而先前基于强化学习的方法需要手工建模模拟器且抑制了原始日志中的有用语义。为此，论文提出一种端到端的智能体方法，利用轻量级大语言模型（LLM），通过微调和思维链推理，将感知、推理、规划和行动四项功能集成到一个14B参数的LLM中，使其能够处理系统日志、推断网络状态、更新攻击假设、模拟不同响应策略并生成有效行动，同时通过比较模拟结果与实际观察实现上下文自适应。主要实验结果表明，该方法无需显式建模，可在商用硬件上运行，在文献报告的事件日志评估中，其恢复速度比前沿大语言模型快达23%。
Minimax Optimality and Spectral Routing for Majority-Vote Ensembles under Markov Dependence
Authors: Ibne Farabi Shihab, Sanjeda Akter, Anuj Sharma
First: 2026-04-15T02:32:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:32:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Majority-vote ensembles achieve variance reduction by averaging over diverse, approximately independent base learners. When training data exhibits Markov dependence, as in time-series forecasting, reinforcement learning (RL) replay buffers, and spatial grids, this classical guarantee degrades in ways that existing theory does not fully quantify. We provide a minimax characterization of this phenomenon for discrete classification in a fixed-dimensional Markov setting, together with an adaptive algorithm that matches the rate on a graph-regular subclass. We first establish an information-theoretic lower bound for stationary, reversible, geometrically ergodic chains in fixed ambient dimension, showing that no measurable estimator can achieve excess classification risk better than $Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$. We then prove that, on the AR(1) witness subclass underlying the lower-bound construction, dependence-agnostic uniform bagging is provably suboptimal with excess risk bounded below by $Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$, exhibiting a $\sqrt{\Tmix}$ algorithmic gap. Finally, we propose \emph{adaptive spectral routing}, which partitions the training data via the empirical Fiedler eigenvector of a dependency graph and achieves the minimax rate $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$ up to a lower-order geometric cut term on a graph-regular subclass, without knowledge of $\Tmix$. Experiments on synthetic Markov chains, 2D spatial grids, the 128-dataset UCR archive, and Atari DQN ensembles validate the theoretical predictions. Consequences for deep RL target variance, scalability via Nyström approximation, and bounded non-stationarity are developed as supporting material in the appendix.
中文标题/摘要
标题：马尔可夫依赖下多数投票集成的最小最大最优性与谱路由
多数投票集成通过平均多样化、近似独立的基础学习器实现方差缩减。当训练数据呈现马尔可夫依赖性时（如时间序列预测、强化学习回放缓冲区和空间网格场景），这一经典保证会以现有理论未能完全量化的方式退化。我们在固定维度的马尔可夫设定下，针对离散分类问题给出了该现象的最小最大刻画，并提出一种在图正则子类上匹配该速率的自适应算法。首先，我们为固定环境维度中的平稳、可逆、几何遍历链建立了信息论下界，证明任何可测估计器的超额分类风险不可能优于$Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$。随后在支撑下界构造的AR(1)见证子类上，证明依赖无关的均匀装袋方法具有可证明的次优性，其超额风险下界为$Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$，呈现$\sqrt{\Tmix}$的算法间隙。最后提出\emph{自适应谱路由}方法，通过依赖图的经验费德勒特征向量划分训练数据，在图正则子类上以忽略低阶几何割项为代价，在未知$\Tmix$的情况下达到$\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$的最小最大速率。在合成马尔可夫链、二维空间网格、128数据集UCR档案及Atari DQN集成上的实验验证了理论预测。附录中进一步探讨了深度强化学习目标方差、基于Nyström近似的可扩展性及有界非平稳性等相关推论。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the degradation of majority-vote ensemble performance when training data exhibits Markov dependence, as common in time-series, reinforcement learning, and spatial applications, where existing theory fails to fully quantify the impact. To characterize this, the authors establish a minimax lower bound showing that no estimator can achieve excess classification risk better than Ω(√(T_mix/n)) for stationary, reversible, geometrically ergodic Markov chains, and prove that standard uniform bagging is suboptimal with a risk of Ω(T_mix/√n), revealing a √T_mix gap. They propose an adaptive spectral routing method that partitions data via the Fiedler eigenvector of a dependency graph, achieving the minimax rate O(√(T_mix/n)) on a graph-regular subclass without prior knowledge of mixing time, with experimental validation on synthetic Markov chains, spatial grids, UCR time-series data, and Atari DQN ensembles.
本文针对多数投票集成方法在训练数据具有马尔可夫依赖性（常见于时间序列、强化学习和空间网格应用）时性能下降的问题展开研究，现有理论未能充分量化其影响。为刻画这一现象，作者建立了极小极大下界，表明对于平稳、可逆、几何遍历的马尔科夫链，任何估计器的超额分类风险不可能优于Ω(√(T_mix/n))，并证明标准的均匀装袋方法是次优的，风险为Ω(T_mix/√n)，揭示了√T_mix的算法差距。他们提出了一种自适应谱路由方法，通过依赖图的费德勒特征向量划分数据，在无需先验混合时间知识的情况下，于图正则子类上达到了极小极大速率O(√(T_mix/n))，并在合成马尔可夫链、空间网格、UCR时间序列数据和Atari DQN集成上进行了实验验证。
Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Augmented Step-Level Transitions for LLM Agents
Authors: Shuai Zhen, Yanhua Yu, Ruopei Guo, Nan Cheng, Yang Deng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:16:31+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in complex interactive decision-making tasks. However, existing LLM agents typically rely on increasingly long interaction histories, resulting in high computational cost and limited scalability. In this paper, we propose STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) framework that enables step-level learning by conditioning only on single-step transitions rather than full interaction histories. STEP-HRL structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress of overall task. By introducing a local progress module, it also iteratively and selectively summarizes interaction history within each subtask to produce a compact summary of local progress. Together, these components yield augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks consistently demonstrate that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baselines in terms of performance and generalization while reducing token usage. Our code is available at https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强步级转移的大语言模型智能体分层强化学习
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在复杂交互式决策任务中展现出强大能力。然而，现有LLM智能体通常依赖日益增长的交互历史，导致计算成本高昂且可扩展性受限。本文提出STEP-HRL，一种分层强化学习（HRL）框架，通过仅以单步转移而非完整交互历史为条件，实现步级学习。STEP-HRL采用分层任务结构，利用已完成的子任务表征整体任务的全局进展。通过引入局部进展模块，该框架还能迭代且选择性地总结每个子任务内的交互历史，生成局部进展的紧凑摘要。这些组件共同为高层策略和低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试中的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能和泛化能力上均显著优于基线方法，同时降低了令牌使用量。代码已开源：https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost and limited scalability of large language model (LLM) agents that rely on long interaction histories, this paper introduces STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework designed to enable step-level learning by conditioning policies only on single-step transitions rather than full histories. The method structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress and employing a local progress module to iteratively summarize interaction history within subtasks, thereby producing augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on the ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks show that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baseline methods in performance and generalization while significantly reducing token usage.
针对依赖长交互历史导致高计算成本和有限可扩展性的大语言模型智能体问题，本文提出了STEP-HRL，一种分层强化学习框架，通过仅基于单步转移而非完整历史来支持步级学习。该方法将任务分层组织，利用完成的子任务表示全局进展，并通过局部进展模块迭代总结子任务内的交互历史，从而为高层和低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试上的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能和泛化能力上显著优于基线方法，同时大幅降低了令牌使用量。
From Prediction to Justification: Aligning Sentiment Reasoning with Human Rationale via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shihao Zhang, Ziwei Wang, Jie Zhou, Yulan Wu, Qin Chen, Zhikai Lei, Liyang Yu, Liang Dou, Liang He
First: 2026-04-15T01:55:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T01:55:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Aspect-based Sentiment Analysis (ABSA) systems have achieved high accuracy in identifying sentiment polarities, they often operate as "black boxes," lacking the explicit reasoning capabilities characteristic of human affective cognition. Humans do not merely categorize sentiment; they construct causal explanations for their judgments. To bridge this gap, we propose ABSA-R1, a large language model framework designed to mimic this ``reason-before-predict" cognitive process. By leveraging reinforcement learning (RL), ABSA-R1 learns to articulate the why behind the what, generating natural language justifications that ground its sentiment predictions. We introduce a Cognition-Aligned Reward Model (formerly sentiment-aware reward model) that enforces consistency between the generated reasoning path and the final emotional label. Furthermore, inspired by metacognitive monitoring, we implement a performance-driven rejection sampling strategy that selectively targets hard cases where the model's internal reasoning is uncertain or inconsistent. Experimental results on four benchmarks demonstrate that equipping models with this explicit reasoning capability not only enhances interpretability but also yields superior performance in sentiment classification and triplet extraction compared to non-reasoning baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从预测到论证：通过强化学习将情感推理与人类理性对齐
尽管基于方面的情感分析系统在识别情感极性方面已达到高准确率，但其常如“黑箱”般运作，缺乏人类情感认知特有的显式推理能力。人类不仅分类情感，还会为判断构建因果解释。为弥合此差距，我们提出ABSA-R1——一个旨在模拟“先推理后预测”认知过程的大语言模型框架。通过强化学习，ABSA-R1学会阐明情感预测背后的原因，生成支撑其判断的自然语言论证。我们引入认知对齐奖励模型（原情感感知奖励模型），强制要求生成推理路径与最终情感标签保持一致。此外，受元认知监控启发，我们实施性能驱动的拒绝采样策略，针对性处理模型内部推理不确定或不一致的高难度案例。在四个基准测试上的实验表明，赋予模型这种显式推理能力不仅能提升可解释性，还在情感分类和三元组提取任务上优于非推理基线模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the lack of explicit reasoning in Aspect-based Sentiment Analysis (ABSA) systems, which typically function as black boxes, by proposing ABSA-R1, a framework that mimics human 'reason-before-predict' cognition using reinforcement learning to generate natural language justifications for sentiment predictions. The method employs a Cognition-Aligned Reward Model to ensure consistency between reasoning and sentiment labels and incorporates a performance-driven rejection sampling strategy to focus on uncertain cases. Experiments on four benchmarks show that this approach not only improves interpretability but also achieves superior performance in sentiment classification and triplet extraction compared to non-reasoning baselines.
本文针对基于方面的情感分析系统通常作为黑箱运行、缺乏显式推理能力的问题，提出了ABSA-R1框架，该框架通过强化学习模仿人类“先推理后预测”的认知过程，生成情感预测的自然语言理由。方法采用认知对齐奖励模型确保推理路径与情感标签的一致性，并引入基于性能的拒绝采样策略以聚焦模型内部推理不确定或矛盾的困难案例。在四个基准测试上的实验结果表明，赋予模型这种显式推理能力不仅增强了可解释性，而且在情感分类和三元组提取任务上优于非推理基线模型。
On the Use of Evolutionary Optimization for the Dynamic Chance Constrained Open-Pit Mine Scheduling Problem
Authors: Ishara Hewa Pathiranage, Aneta Neumann
First: 2026-04-15T01:16:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T01:16:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted to publish in 2026 IEEE World Congress on Computational Intelligence (WCCI)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-pit mine scheduling is a complex real world optimization problem that involves uncertain economic values and dynamically changing resource capacities. Evolutionary algorithms are particularly effective in these scenarios, as they can easily adapt to uncertain and changing environments. However, uncertainty and dynamic changes are often studied in isolation in real-world problems. In this paper, we study a dynamic chance-constrained open-pit mine scheduling problem in which block economic values are stochastic and mining and processing capacities vary over time. We adopt a bi-objective evolutionary formulation that simultaneously maximizes expected discounted profit and minimizes its standard deviation. To address dynamic changes, we propose a diversity-based change response mechanism that repairs a subset of infeasible solutions and introduces additional feasible solutions whenever a change is detected. We evaluate the effectiveness of this mechanism across four multi-objective evolutionary algorithms and compare it with a baseline re-evaluation-based change-response strategy. Experimental results on six mining instances demonstrate that the proposed approach consistently outperforms the baseline methods across different uncertainty levels and change frequencies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于进化优化的动态机会约束露天矿调度问题研究
露天矿调度是涉及不确定经济价值和动态变化资源容量的复杂现实优化问题。进化算法在此类场景中尤为有效，因其能灵活适应不确定的动态环境。然而在实际问题中，不确定性与动态变化常被孤立研究。本文研究一个动态机会约束露天矿调度问题，其中区块经济价值具有随机性，采矿与处理能力随时间变化。我们采用双目标进化模型，同步最大化期望贴现利润并最小化其标准差。针对动态变化，提出基于多样性的变化响应机制：在检测到变化时修复部分不可行解并引入新增可行解。通过四种多目标进化算法验证该机制有效性，并与基于重评估的基准变化响应策略对比。在六个采矿实例上的实验结果表明，所提方法在不同不确定水平和变化频率下均稳定优于基准方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the complex open-pit mine scheduling problem, motivated by the need to handle both uncertain block economic values and dynamically changing resource capacities simultaneously, which are often studied separately. The method employs a bi-objective evolutionary formulation to maximize expected profit while minimizing its risk, and introduces a diversity-based change response mechanism that repairs infeasible solutions and adds feasible ones upon detecting environmental changes. Experimental results on six mining instances show that this proposed mechanism consistently outperforms a baseline re-evaluation strategy across various uncertainty levels and change frequencies when tested with four multi-objective evolutionary algorithms.
本文针对露天矿调度这一复杂问题，其动机在于需要同时处理不确定的区块经济价值和动态变化的资源容量，而这两者在以往研究中常被孤立对待。方法上采用了一种双目标进化优化框架，以同时最大化期望利润并最小化其风险，并提出了一种基于多样性的变化响应机制，能在检测到环境变化时修复不可行解并引入新的可行解。在六个采矿实例上的实验结果表明，当与四种多目标进化算法结合时，所提出的机制在不同不确定性水平和变化频率下均一致优于基于重新评估的基线策略。
SPG: Sandwiched Policy Gradient for Masked Diffusion Language Models
Authors: Chenyu Wang, Paria Rashidinejad, DiJia Su, Song Jiang, Sid Wang, Siyan Zhao, Cai Zhou, Shannon Zejiang Shen, Feiyu Chen, Tommi Jaakkola, Yuandong Tian, Bo Liu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-10T16:52:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T23:15:20+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) are emerging as an efficient alternative to autoregressive models due to their ability to decode multiple tokens in parallel. However, aligning dLLMs with human preferences or task-specific rewards via reinforcement learning (RL) is challenging because their intractable log-likelihood precludes the direct application of standard policy gradient methods. While prior work uses surrogates like the evidence lower bound (ELBO), these one-sided approximations can introduce significant policy gradient bias. To address this, we propose the Sandwiched Policy Gradient (SPG) that leverages both an upper and a lower bound of the true log-likelihood. Experiments show that SPG significantly outperforms baselines based on ELBO or one-step estimation. Specifically, SPG improves the accuracy over state-of-the-art RL methods for dLLMs by 3.6% in GSM8K, 2.6% in MATH500, 18.4% in Countdown and 27.0% in Sudoku.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPG：面向掩码扩散语言模型的三明治策略梯度
扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）因其能并行解码多个令牌的特性，正成为自回归模型的高效替代方案。然而，通过强化学习（RL）将dLLMs与人类偏好或任务特定奖励对齐具有挑战性，因其难处理的似然对数阻碍了标准策略梯度方法的直接应用。现有研究虽采用证据下界（ELBO）等替代方法，但这些单边近似可能引入显著的策略梯度偏差。为此，我们提出三明治策略梯度（SPG），该方法同时利用真实似然对数的上界与下界。实验表明，SPG显著优于基于ELBO或单步估计的基线方法。具体而言，在GSM8K、MATH500、Countdown和Sudoku任务中，SPG较dLLMs最先进RL方法的准确率分别提升3.6%、2.6%、18.4%和27.0%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to align diffusion large language models (dLLMs) with human preferences via reinforcement learning, which is challenging due to their intractable log-likelihood that prevents direct policy gradient application. The method introduces the Sandwiched Policy Gradient (SPG), which leverages both upper and lower bounds of the true log-likelihood to reduce bias compared to prior one-sided approximations like the evidence lower bound. Experimental results show that SPG significantly outperforms baselines, improving accuracy by up to 27.0% in tasks such as GSM8K, MATH500, Countdown, and Sudoku.
本研究的动机是通过强化学习将扩散大语言模型与人类偏好对齐，但由于其难以处理的似然函数，标准策略梯度方法无法直接应用。方法上提出了夹逼策略梯度，利用真实似然函数的上界和下界来减少先前单边近似（如证据下界）带来的偏差。实验结果表明，该方法显著优于基线，在GSM8K、MATH500、Countdown和Sudoku等任务中准确率提升最高达27.0%。
When Can You Poison Rewards? A Tight Characterization of Reward Poisoning in Linear MDPs
Authors: Jose Efraim Aguilar Escamilla, Haoyang Hong, Jiawei Li, Haoyu Zhao, Xuezhou Zhang, Sanghyun Hong, Huazheng Wang
First: 2026-04-11T06:55:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T22:53:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reward poisoning attacks in reinforcement learning (RL), where an adversary manipulates rewards within constrained budgets to force the target RL agent to adopt a policy that aligns with the attacker's objectives. Prior works on reward poisoning mainly focused on sufficient conditions to design a successful attacker, while only a few studies discussed the infeasibility of targeted attacks. This paper provides the first precise necessity and sufficiency characterization of the attackability of a linear MDP under reward poisoning attacks. Our characterization draws a bright line between the vulnerable RL instances, and the intrinsically robust ones which cannot be attacked without large costs even running vanilla non-robust RL algorithms. Our theory extends beyond linear MDPs -- by approximating deep RL environments as linear MDPs, we show that our theoretical framework effectively distinguishes the attackability and efficiently attacks the vulnerable ones, demonstrating both the theoretical and practical significance of our characterization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：何时可毒化奖励？线性MDP中奖励毒化攻击的紧致刻画
本文研究强化学习中的奖励毒化攻击：攻击者在预算约束下操纵奖励信号，迫使目标智能体执行符合攻击者意图的策略。现有研究主要关注设计有效攻击者的充分条件，仅少数工作讨论定向攻击的不可行性。本文首次对线性马尔可夫决策过程在奖励毒化攻击下的可攻击性给出了精确的充要条件刻画。该刻画清晰划分了易受攻击的强化学习实例与本质鲁棒的实例——后者即使运行普通非鲁棒算法也难以被低成本攻击。我们的理论可拓展至线性MDP之外：通过将深度强化学习环境近似为线性MDP，证明该理论框架能有效区分可攻击性并高效攻击脆弱实例，展现了本刻画的理论与实践价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates reward poisoning attacks in reinforcement learning, where an adversary aims to manipulate an agent's learned policy by altering rewards within a limited budget. The primary motivation is to establish a precise theoretical boundary distinguishing RL instances that are vulnerable to such attacks from those that are inherently robust. The method involves providing the first tight characterization of attackability for linear Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), detailing both necessary and sufficient conditions for successful poisoning. Experimental results validate the theory by showing that this framework can effectively classify the attackability of environments, including those approximated as linear MDPs in deep RL, and successfully execute attacks on vulnerable instances, highlighting its practical applicability.
本文研究强化学习中的奖励投毒攻击，即攻击者在有限预算内操纵奖励，以使目标智能体学习符合其意图的策略。其动机在于首次为线性马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）下的攻击可能性提供了精确的必要与充分条件刻画，从而清晰区分了易受攻击的RL实例与本质上稳健、即使运行普通非鲁棒算法也难以低成本攻击的实例。方法上，该研究建立了线性MDP中奖励投毒攻击能力的严格理论特征。实验结果表明，该理论框架能有效区分环境的可攻击性，包括将深度RL环境近似为线性MDP的情况，并能高效攻击脆弱实例，证明了其理论与实际意义。
eBandit: Kernel-Driven Reinforcement Learning for Adaptive Video Streaming
Authors: Mahdi Alizadeh
First: 2026-04-09T22:02:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T21:45:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
User-space Adaptive Bitrate (ABR) algorithms cannot see the transport layer signals that matter most, such as minimum RTT and instantaneous delivery rate, and they respond to network changes only after damage has already propagated to the playout buffer. We present eBandit, a framework that relocates both network monitoring and ABR algorithm selection into the Linux kernel using eBPF. A lightweight epsilon-greedy Multi-Armed Bandit (MAB) runs inside a sockops program, evaluating three ABR heuristics against a reward derived from live TCP metrics. On an adversarial synthetic trace eBandit achieves $416.3 \pm 4.9$ cumulative QoE, outperforming the best static heuristic by $7.2\%$. On 42 real-world sessions eBandit achieves a mean QoE per chunk of $1.241$, the highest across all policies, demonstrating that kernel-resident bandit learning transfers to heterogeneous mobile conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：eBandit：基于内核驱动的自适应视频流强化学习框架
用户态自适应码率（ABR）算法无法获取传输层关键信号（如最小RTT与即时传输速率），且仅在网络变化已波及播放缓冲区后才作出响应。本文提出eBandit框架，利用eBPF将网络监测与ABR算法选择迁移至Linux内核。轻量级ε-贪心多臂赌博机（MAB）在sockops程序中运行，通过实时TCP指标衍生的奖励函数评估三种ABR启发式算法。在对抗性合成轨迹测试中，eBandit累计QoE达416.3±4.9，较最佳静态启发式算法提升7.2%。在42组真实会话中，eBandit实现分块平均QoE 1.241，为所有策略中最高，证明内核驻留赌博机学习可迁移至异构移动网络环境。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for eBandit stems from the limitations of user-space Adaptive Bitrate (ABR) algorithms, which lack direct access to key transport-layer signals like minimum RTT and instantaneous delivery rate, leading to delayed responses that degrade streaming quality. Beyond Uniform Sampling: Synergistic Active Learning and Input Denoising for Robust Neural Operators
Authors: Samrendra Roy, Souvik Chakraborty, Syed Bahauddin Alam
First: 2026-04-14T21:43:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T21:43:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural operators have emerged as fast surrogate models for physics simulations, yet they remain acutely vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, a critical liability for safety-critical digital twin deployments. We present a synergistic defense that combines active learning-based data generation with an input denoising architecture. The active learning component adaptively probes model weaknesses using differential evolution attacks, then generates targeted training data at discovered vulnerability locations while an adaptive smooth-ratio safeguard preserves baseline accuracy. The input denoising component augments the operator architecture with a learnable bottleneck that filters adversarial noise while retaining physics-relevant features. On the viscous Burgers' equation benchmark, the combined approach achieves a 2.04% combined error (1.21% baseline + 0.83% robustness), representing an 87% reduction relative to standard training (15.42% combined) and outperforming both active learning alone (3.42%) and input denoising alone (5.22%). More broadly, our results, combined with cross-architecture vulnerability analysis from prior work, suggest that optimal training data for neural operators is architecture-dependent: because different architectures concentrate sensitivity in distinct input subspaces, uniform sampling cannot adequately cover the vulnerability landscape of all models. These findings have potential implications for the deployment of neural operators in safety-critical energy systems including nuclear reactor monitoring.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越均匀采样：面向鲁棒神经算子的协同主动学习与输入去噪方法
神经算子作为物理仿真的快速代理模型已崭露头角，但其对对抗性扰动高度敏感，这对安全关键的数字孪生部署构成严重隐患。本研究提出一种协同防御框架，将基于主动学习的数据生成与输入去噪架构相结合。主动学习组件通过差分进化攻击自适应探测模型弱点，在发现的脆弱位置生成针对性训练数据，同时采用自适应平滑比保护机制维持基准精度。输入去噪组件通过可学习的瓶颈结构增强算子架构，在过滤对抗噪声的同时保留物理相关特征。在粘性伯格斯方程基准测试中，该组合方法实现了2.04%的综合误差（1.21%基准误差+0.83%鲁棒性误差），相较于标准训练（15.42%）降低87%，且优于单独使用主动学习（3.42%）或输入去噪（5.22%）的方案。更广泛而言，本研究结果结合先前工作的跨架构脆弱性分析表明：神经算子的最优训练数据具有架构依赖性——由于不同架构将敏感性集中于不同的输入子空间，均匀采样无法充分覆盖所有模型的脆弱性图谱。这些发现对神经算子在核反应堆监测等安全关键能源系统中的部署具有潜在意义。

This paper addresses the vulnerability of neural operators, which are fast surrogate models for physics simulations, to adversarial perturbations, a critical issue for safety-critical applications like digital twins. 本文针对神经算子（物理仿真的快速代理模型）在对抗性扰动下的脆弱性问题展开研究，这在数字孪生等安全关键应用中至关重要。所提出的协同防御方法结合了主动学习和输入去噪：主动学习组件通过差分进化攻击自适应探测模型弱点，在发现的脆弱位置生成针对性训练数据；输入去噪组件则在算子架构中加入可学习的瓶颈层，以过滤对抗噪声并保留物理相关特征。在粘性伯格斯方程基准测试中，该组合方法实现了2.04%的综合误差，相比标准训练降低了87%，且优于单独使用主动学习或输入去噪；更广泛的分析表明，由于不同架构的敏感性子空间各异，神经算子的最优训练数据具有架构依赖性。
Empowerment Gain and Causal Model Construction: Children and adults are sensitive to controllability and variability in their causal interventions
Authors: Eunice Yiu, Kelsey Allen, Shiry Ginosar, Alison Gopnik
First: 2025-12-09T04:14:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T19:30:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Philosophical Transactions A, Special issue: World models, AGI, and the hard problems of life-mind continuity. Expected publication in 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning about the causal structure of the world is a fundamental problem for human cognition. Causal models and especially causal learning have proved to be difficult for large pretrained models using standard techniques of deep learning. In contrast, cognitive scientists have applied advances in our formal understanding of causation in computer science, particularly within the Causal Bayes Net formalism, to understand human causal learning. In the very different tradition of reinforcement learning, researchers have described an intrinsic reward signal called "empowerment" which maximizes mutual information between actions and their outcomes. "Empowerment" may be an important bridge between classical Bayesian causal learning and reinforcement learning and may help to characterize causal learning in humans and enable it in machines. If an agent learns an accurate causal world model, they will necessarily increase their empowerment, and increasing empowerment will lead to a more accurate causal world model. Empowerment may also explain distinctive features of childrens causal learning, as well as providing a more tractable computational account of how that learning is possible. In an empirical study, we systematically test how children and adults use cues to empowerment to infer causal relations, and design effective causal interventions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：赋能增益与因果模型构建：儿童与成人对其因果干预中的可控性与变异性敏感
理解世界的因果结构是人类认知的基本问题。因果模型，尤其是因果学习，对于采用标准深度学习技术的大型预训练模型而言已被证明是困难的。相比之下，认知科学家运用了计算机科学中因果关系的形式化理解进展，特别是因果贝叶斯网络形式体系，来阐释人类的因果学习。在截然不同的强化学习传统中，研究者描述了一种称为“赋能”的内在奖励信号，它最大化行动与其结果之间的互信息。“赋能”可能成为经典贝叶斯因果学习与强化学习之间的重要桥梁，并有助于刻画人类的因果学习机制，同时赋能机器实现该能力。若智能体习得准确的因果世界模型，其赋能必然增强；而增强赋能又将导向更精确的因果世界模型。赋能亦可解释儿童因果学习的独特特征，并为该学习过程如何实现提供更易处理的计算解释。在一项实证研究中，我们系统检验了儿童与成人如何利用赋能线索推断因果关系，并设计有效的因果干预策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of enabling machines to learn causal models akin to humans, and bridging Bayesian causal learning with reinforcement learning, this paper investigates the concept of 'empowerment'—maximizing mutual information between actions and outcomes—as a key mechanism. The method involves an empirical study where both children and adults are systematically tested on how they use cues related to controllability and variability to infer causal relations and design interventions. The main experimental results demonstrate that both children and adults are sensitive to these empowerment-related cues, successfully applying them to learn causal structures and plan effective interventions, supporting empowerment as a tractable computational account of human causal learning.
本文的动机源于让机器像人类一样学习因果模型的挑战，旨在桥接贝叶斯因果学习与强化学习，研究“赋能”（即最大化行动与结果间的互信息）作为关键机制。研究方法是通过实证研究，系统测试儿童和成人如何利用与可控性和变异性相关的线索来推断因果关系并设计干预措施。主要实验结果表明，儿童和成人都对这些赋能相关线索敏感，能成功运用它们学习因果结构并规划有效干预，从而支持赋能作为人类因果学习的一种可计算解释。
Not All Tokens Matter: Towards Efficient LLM Reasoning via Token Significance in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hanbing Liu, Lang Cao, Yuanyi Ren, Mengyu Zhou, Haoyu Dong, Xiaojun Ma, Shi Han, Dongmei Zhang
First: 2025-06-09T18:27:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T19:15:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) show strong reasoning abilities but often produce unnecessarily long explanations that reduce efficiency. Although reinforcement learning (RL) has been used to improve reasoning, most methods focus on accuracy and rely on uniform length-based rewards that overlook the differing contributions of individual tokens, often harming correctness. We revisit length optimization in RL through the perspective of token significance. Observing that many chain-of-thought (CoT) tokens contribute little to the final answer, we introduce a significance-aware length reward that selectively penalizes insignificance tokens, reducing redundancy while preserving essential reasoning. We also propose a dynamic length reward that encourages more detailed reasoning early in training and gradually shifts toward conciseness as learning progresses. Integrating these components into standard policy optimization yields a framework that improves both reasoning efficiency and accuracy. Experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate substantial reductions in response length while preserving or improving correctness, highlighting the importance of modeling token significance for efficient LLM reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：并非所有令牌都重要：基于强化学习中令牌重要性实现高效大语言模型推理
大语言模型展现出强大的推理能力，但常生成冗余冗长的解释而降低效率。尽管强化学习已被用于改进推理，现有方法多聚焦准确性，并依赖基于长度的均匀奖励机制，忽视了单个令牌的差异化贡献，甚至可能损害正确性。本研究从令牌重要性视角重新审视强化学习的长度优化：观察到思维链中许多令牌对最终答案贡献甚微，我们提出一种重要性感知的长度奖励机制，选择性惩罚无关紧要的令牌以降低冗余，同时保留核心推理逻辑；另提出动态长度奖励机制，在训练初期鼓励详细推理，随学习进程逐步转向简洁表达。将上述组件整合至标准策略优化框架后，实验表明该方案能在保持或提升准确性的同时显著缩短响应长度，验证了建模令牌重要性对提升大语言模型推理效率的关键价值。
