The motivation for this work stems from the limitations of Large Language Models (LLMs) in knowledge-intensive reasoning and the challenge of performing precise multi-hop reasoning over Knowledge Graphs (KGs) for complex queries, as existing pipeline-based methods often fragment the process and lose intermediate information. The method introduces KG-Reasoner, an end-to-end framework that integrates multi-step reasoning into a unified "thinking" phase of a Reasoning LLM, using Reinforcement Learning (RL) to train the LLM to internalize KG traversal, enabling dynamic path exploration and backtracking. The main experimental results show that KG-Reasoner achieves competitive or superior performance on eight multi-hop and knowledge-intensive reasoning benchmarks compared to state-of-the-art methods.
本工作的动机源于大语言模型在知识密集型推理上的局限性，以及对知识图谱进行精确多跳推理以处理复杂查询的挑战，因为现有的基于流水线的方法常使推理过程碎片化并丢失中间信息。方法上提出了KG-Reasoner，这是一个端到端框架，将多步推理集成到推理大语言模型的统一“思考”阶段，通过强化学习训练大语言模型内化知识图谱遍历过程，从而实现动态路径探索和必要时的回溯。主要实验结果表明，在八个多跳和知识密集型推理基准测试上，KG-Reasoner相比最先进方法取得了有竞争力或更优的性能。
AAPO: Enhancing the Reasoning Capabilities of LLMs with Advantage Margin
Authors: Jian Xiong, Jingbo Zhou, Jingyong Ye, Qiang Huang, Dejing Dou
First: 2025-05-20T12:13:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T09:06:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as an effective approach for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs), especially in scenarios where supervised fine-tuning (SFT) falls short due to limited chain-of-thought (CoT) data. Among RL-based post-training methods, group relative advantage estimation, as exemplified by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has attracted considerable attention for eliminating the dependency on the value model, thereby simplifying training compared to traditional approaches like Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). However, we observe that exsiting group relative advantage estimation method still suffers from training inefficiencies, particularly when the estimated advantage approaches zero. To address this limitation, we propose Advantage-Augmented Policy Optimization (AAPO), a novel RL algorithm that optimizes the cross-entropy (CE) loss using advantages enhanced through a margin-based estimation scheme. This approach effectively mitigates the inefficiencies associated with group relative advantage estimation. Experimental results on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate the superior performance of AAPO. Code is available at https://github.com/JianxXiong/AAPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AAPO：基于优势边际增强大语言模型推理能力
强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的有效方法，尤其在监督微调因思维链数据有限而效果不足的场景中。在基于强化学习的后训练方法中，以分组相对策略优化为代表的群体相对优势估计因无需依赖价值模型而备受关注，相比近端策略优化等传统方法简化了训练流程。然而，现有群体相对优势估计方法仍存在训练效率低下的问题，尤其在估计优势趋近于零时更为明显。为突破此局限，我们提出优势增强策略优化——一种通过边际估计方案增强优势值来优化交叉熵损失的新型强化学习算法。该方法有效缓解了群体相对优势估计的效率瓶颈。在多个数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明AAPO具有优越性能。代码已开源：https://github.com/JianxXiong/AAPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses inefficiencies in reinforcement learning methods for enhancing large language models' reasoning, particularly when group relative advantage estimation yields near-zero advantages, which hampers training. The authors propose Advantage-Augmented Policy Optimization (AAPO), a novel algorithm that improves cross-entropy loss optimization by incorporating a margin-based scheme to augment advantage estimates, thereby mitigating these inefficiencies. Experiments on multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that AAPO achieves superior performance compared to existing methods, validating its effectiveness in boosting LLM reasoning capabilities without relying on value models.
本文针对强化学习在提升大语言模型推理能力时存在的训练低效问题，特别是当群体相对优势估计接近零时，提出了优势增强策略优化（AAPO）算法。该方法通过引入基于边际的估计方案来增强优势，优化交叉熵损失，有效缓解了群体相对优势估计的不足。在多个数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，AAPO相比现有方法具有更优的性能，证实了其在无需依赖价值模型的情况下增强大语言模型推理能力的有效性。
From Kinematics to Dynamics: Learning to Refine Hybrid Plans for Physically Feasible Execution
Authors: Lidor Erez, Shahaf S. Shperberg, Ayal Taitler
First: 2026-04-14T09:00:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T09:00:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In many robotic tasks, agents must traverse a sequence of spatial regions to complete a mission. Such problems are inherently mixed discrete-continuous: a high-level action sequence and a physically feasible continuous trajectory. The resulting trajectory and action sequence must also satisfy problem constraints such as deadlines, time windows, and velocity or acceleration limits. While hybrid temporal planners attempt to address this challenge, they typically model motion using linear (first-order) dynamics, which cannot guarantee that the resulting plan respects the robot's true physical constraints. Consequently, even when the high-level action sequence is fixed, producing a dynamically feasible trajectory becomes a bi-level optimization problem. We address this problem via reinforcement learning in continuous space. We define a Markov Decision Process that explicitly incorporates analytical second-order constraints and use it to refine first-order plans generated by a hybrid planner. Our results show that this approach can reliably recover physical feasibility and effectively bridge the gap between a planner's initial first-order trajectory and the dynamics required for real execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从运动学到动力学：学习优化混合规划以实现物理可行执行
在许多机器人任务中，智能体必须穿越一系列空间区域以完成任务。这类问题本质上是离散-连续混合的：包含高层动作序列与物理可行的连续轨迹。生成的轨迹与动作序列还需满足时间限制、时间窗口、速度或加速度限制等约束条件。虽然混合时序规划器试图解决这一挑战，但其通常采用线性（一阶）动力学建模运动，无法保证生成的规划符合机器人真实的物理约束。因此，即使高层动作序列已确定，生成动力学可行的轨迹仍会形成双层优化问题。我们通过连续空间中的强化学习解决该问题：定义显式包含解析二阶约束的马尔可夫决策过程，并利用其优化混合规划器生成的一阶规划。实验表明，该方法能可靠恢复物理可行性，有效弥合规划器初始一阶轨迹与实际执行所需动力学之间的差距。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that hybrid temporal planners, which generate sequences of discrete actions and continuous trajectories, often rely on simplified first-order dynamics models that fail to guarantee physical feasibility under real robot constraints like acceleration limits. To address this, the authors propose a reinforcement learning method in continuous space, formulating a Markov Decision Process that incorporates analytical second-order constraints to refine the initial first-order plans. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach reliably recovers physical feasibility, effectively bridging the gap between the planner's output and the dynamics needed for real-world execution.
本文的动机在于混合时序规划器通常基于简化的一阶动力学模型生成离散动作序列和连续轨迹，但无法保证在真实机器人加速度等约束下的物理可行性。为此，作者提出一种连续空间中的强化学习方法，通过构建包含解析二阶约束的马尔可夫决策过程来优化初始一阶规划。实验结果表明，该方法能可靠地恢复物理可行性，有效弥合了规划器输出与实际执行所需动力学之间的差距。
WebFactory: Automated Compression of Foundational Language Intelligence into Grounded Web Agents
Authors: Sicheng Fan, Qingyun Shi, Shengze Xu, Shengbo Cai, Tieyong Zeng, Li Ling, Yanyi Shang, Dehan Kong
First: 2026-03-05T10:51:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T08:14:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current paradigms for training GUI agents are fundamentally limited by a reliance on either unsafe, non-reproducible live web interactions or costly, scarce human-crafted data and environments. We argue this focus on data volume overlooks a more critical factor: the efficiency of compressing a large language model's (LLM) latent knowledge into actionable agent behavior. We introduce WebFactory, a novel, fully automated closed-loop reinforcement learning pipeline for GUI agents, systematically compressing LLM-encoded internet intelligence into efficient, grounded actions. Our pipeline features a process of scalable environment synthesis, knowledge-aware task generation, LLM-powered trajectory collection, decomposed reward RL training, and systematic agent evaluation. Remarkably, our agent demonstrates exceptional data efficiency and generalization. Trained on synthetic data from only 10 websites within WebFactory, it achieves performance comparable to GUI agents trained on the same amount of human-annotated data from a much larger set of environments. This superior performance is consistent across our internal offline and online transfer benchmarks, where our agent also significantly outperforms the base foundation model. We further provide critical insights into the "embodiment potential" of different LLM foundations, offering a new axis for model evaluation. This work presents a scalable and cost-effective paradigm for transforming passive internet knowledge into active, grounded intelligence, marking a critical step towards general-purpose interactive agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WebFactory：将基础语言智能自动压缩为具身网络智能体
当前训练GUI智能体的范式存在根本性局限，其依赖于不安全、不可复现的实时网络交互，或成本高昂、稀缺的人工标注数据与环境。我们认为，对数据规模的过度关注忽视了一个更关键的因素：将大语言模型（LLM）的潜在知识高效压缩为可执行的智能体行为。本文提出WebFactory——一种全新的、全自动闭环强化学习流程，用于系统地将LLM编码的网络智能压缩为高效、具身化的GUI智能体行为。该流程包含可扩展环境合成、知识感知任务生成、LLM驱动的轨迹收集、分解奖励强化学习训练及系统化智能体评估。值得注意的是，我们的智能体展现出卓越的数据效率与泛化能力：仅使用WebFactory中10个网站生成的合成数据进行训练，其性能即可媲美在更庞大环境集合中使用等量人工标注数据训练的GUI智能体。这一优势在我们内部的离线与在线迁移基准测试中均得到验证，且智能体表现显著超越基础大模型。我们进一步对不同LLM基座的“具身化潜力”提出关键见解，为模型评估提供了新维度。本工作提出了一种可扩展、高效益的范式，将被动网络知识转化为主动的具身智能，标志着向通用交互智能体迈出关键一步。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of current GUI agent training paradigms that rely on unsafe live web interactions or costly human-crafted data, this paper introduces WebFactory, a fully automated closed-loop reinforcement learning pipeline designed to compress a large language model's latent knowledge into efficient, grounded agent actions. The method involves scalable environment synthesis, knowledge-aware task generation, LLM-powered trajectory collection, and decomposed reward RL training. Experimental results show that an agent trained on synthetic data from only 10 websites within WebFactory achieves performance comparable to agents trained on extensive human-annotated data from larger environments, demonstrating exceptional data efficiency and generalization, and significantly outperforms the base foundation model in offline and online transfer benchmarks.
针对当前GUI智能体训练范式依赖不安全的实时网络交互或昂贵人工标注数据的局限，本文提出了WebFactory，一种全自动闭环强化学习流程，旨在将大语言模型的潜在知识压缩为高效、具身的智能体行为。该方法包括可扩展的环境合成、知识感知任务生成、大语言模型驱动的轨迹收集以及分解奖励强化学习训练。实验结果表明，在WebFactory中仅使用10个网站的合成数据训练的智能体，其性能可与在更大规模环境中使用大量人工标注数据训练的智能体相媲美，展现出卓越的数据效率和泛化能力，并在离线和在线迁移基准测试中显著优于基础大模型。
Prompt Evolution for Generative AI: A Classifier-Guided Approach
Authors: Melvin Wong, Yew-Soon Ong, Abhishek Gupta, Kavitesh K. Bali, Caishun Chen
Venue: IEEE Conference on Artificial Intelligence (CAI) 2023 (Pages 226-229)
First: 2023-05-24T14:48:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T07:08:36+00:00
Comments: This work is published in the Proceedings of the IEEE Conference on Artificial Intelligence (CAI 2023). IEEE copyrights applies
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Synthesis of digital artifacts conditioned on user prompts has become an important paradigm facilitating an explosion of use cases with generative AI. However, such models often fail to connect the generated outputs and desired target concepts/preferences implied by the prompts. Current research addressing this limitation has largely focused on enhancing the prompts before output generation or improving the model's performance up front. In contrast, this paper conceptualizes prompt evolution, imparting evolutionary selection pressure and variation during the generative process to produce multiple outputs that satisfy the target concepts/preferences better. We propose a multi-objective instantiation of this broader idea that uses a multi-label image classifier-guided approach. The predicted labels from the classifiers serve as multiple objectives to optimize, with the aim of producing diversified images that meet user preferences. A novelty of our evolutionary algorithm is that the pre-trained generative model gives us implicit mutation operations, leveraging the model's stochastic generative capability to automate the creation of Pareto-optimized images more faithful to user preferences.
中文标题/摘要
标题：生成式AI的提示进化：一种分类器引导方法
基于用户提示的数字内容合成已成为推动生成式AI应用爆发的重要范式。然而，此类模型常难以将生成输出与提示所隐含的目标概念/偏好有效关联。当前研究主要聚焦于输出生成前的提示增强或模型性能的预先优化。本文则提出“提示进化”概念，通过在生成过程中引入进化选择压力与变异机制，产生更符合目标概念/偏好的多样化输出。我们基于这一框架提出多目标实现方案，采用多标签图像分类器引导方法：分类器的预测标签作为待优化的多目标，旨在生成满足用户偏好的多样化图像。本进化算法的新颖之处在于，利用预训练生成模型的随机生成能力实现隐式变异操作，从而自动化生成更贴合用户偏好的帕累托优化图像。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the frequent disconnect between user prompts and the outputs of generative AI models, which often fail to capture desired concepts or preferences. To address this, the authors propose a method called prompt evolution, which applies evolutionary selection pressure and variation during generation, using a multi-label image classifier to guide the process by treating predicted labels as multiple objectives for optimization. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach successfully produces diversified, Pareto-optimized images that are more faithful to user preferences, leveraging the stochastic capabilities of pre-trained generative models for automated mutation.
本文的动机在于生成式AI模型常无法将输出与用户提示中隐含的目标概念或偏好有效连接。为此，作者提出了一种提示演化的方法，在生成过程中引入进化选择压力和变异，采用多标签图像分类器作为引导，将预测标签作为多个优化目标。实验结果表明，该方法能成功生成多样化、帕累托优化的图像，更贴合用户偏好，并利用预训练生成模型的随机生成能力实现自动化变异。

First: 2026-04-14T07:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T07:02:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We describe the pre-training, post-training, and quantization of Nemotron 3 Super, a 120 billion (active 12 billion) parameter hybrid Mamba-Attention Mixture-of-Experts model. Nemotron 3 Super is the first model in the Nemotron 3 family to 1) be pre-trained in NVFP4, 2) leverage LatentMoE, a new Mixture-of-Experts architecture that optimizes for both accuracy per FLOP and accuracy per parameter, and 3) include MTP layers for inference acceleration through native speculative decoding. We pre-trained Nemotron 3 Super on 25 trillion tokens followed by post-training using supervised fine tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). The final model supports up to 1M context length and achieves comparable accuracy on common benchmarks, while also achieving up to 2.2x and 7.5x higher inference throughput compared to GPT-OSS-120B and Qwen3.5-122B, respectively. Nemotron 3 Super datasets, along with the base, post-trained, and quantized checkpoints, are open-sourced on HuggingFace.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Nemotron 3 Super：面向智能体推理的开放高效混合专家Mamba-Transformer模型
本文介绍了Nemotron 3 Super的预训练、后训练及量化过程，该模型为1200亿参数（激活120亿）的混合Mamba-注意力专家混合模型。作为Nemotron 3系列首个实现以下特性的模型：1) 采用NVFP4格式预训练；2) 集成LatentMoE——一种兼顾每FLOP精度与每参数精度的新型专家混合架构；3) 内置MTP层，通过原生推测解码实现推理加速。模型基于25万亿token进行预训练，并通过监督微调与强化学习进行后训练。最终模型支持高达100万token的上下文长度，在主流基准测试中达到可比精度，同时相比GPT-OSS-120B和Qwen3.5-122B分别实现最高2.2倍与7.5倍的推理吞吐量提升。Nemotron 3 Super的数据集及基础版、后训练版、量化版检查点已在HuggingFace开源。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind Nemotron 3 Super is to create an open, efficient large language model that combines high accuracy with superior inference speed for agentic reasoning tasks. The method involves pre-training a 120B parameter hybrid Mamba-Transformer Mixture-of-Experts model, incorporating novel architectural elements like LatentMoE for efficiency and MTP layers for speculative decoding acceleration, followed by supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. Experimental results show the model achieves competitive accuracy on standard benchmarks while supporting a 1M token context length and delivering up to 2.2x and 7.5x higher inference throughput compared to leading open-source models like GPT-OSS-120B and Qwen3.5-122B.
Nemotron 3 Super 的开发动机是构建一个开源、高效的大型语言模型，旨在为智能体推理任务结合高准确性与卓越的推理速度。其方法包括预训练一个1200亿参数（活跃120亿）的混合Mamba-Transformer专家混合模型，引入了LatentMoE等新颖架构以提高效率，并采用MTP层进行推测解码加速，随后进行了监督微调和强化学习。实验结果表明，该模型在常见基准测试上达到了可比的准确性，同时支持100万令牌的上下文长度，并且相比GPT-OSS-120B和Qwen3.5-122B等领先开源模型，推理吞吐量最高提升了2.2倍和7.5倍。
TempoNet: Slack-Quantized Transformer-Guided Reinforcement Scheduler for Adaptive Deadline-Centric Real-Time Dispatchs
Authors: Rong Fu, Yibo Meng, Guangzhen Yao, Jiaxuan Lu, Zeyu Zhang, Zhaolu Kang, Ziming Guo, Jia Yee Tan, Xiaojing Du, Simon James Fong
First: 2026-02-20T09:56:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T06:55:12+00:00
Comments: 43 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-time schedulers must reason about tight deadlines under strict compute budgets. We present TempoNet, a reinforcement learning scheduler that pairs a permutation-invariant Transformer with a deep Q-approximation. An Urgency Tokenizer discretizes temporal slack into learnable embeddings, stabilizing value learning and capturing deadline proximity. A latency-aware sparse attention stack with blockwise top-k selection and locality-sensitive chunking enables global reasoning over unordered task sets with near-linear scaling and sub-millisecond inference. A multicore mapping layer converts contextualized Q-scores into processor assignments through masked-greedy selection or differentiable matching. Extensive evaluations on industrial mixed-criticality traces and large multiprocessor settings show consistent gains in deadline fulfillment over analytic schedulers and neural baselines, together with improved optimization stability. Diagnostics include sensitivity analyses for slack quantization, attention-driven policy interpretation, hardware-in-the-loop and kernel micro-benchmarks, and robustness under stress with simple runtime mitigations; we also report sample-efficiency benefits from behavioral-cloning pretraining and compatibility with an actor-critic variant without altering the inference pipeline. These results establish a practical framework for Transformer-based decision making in high-throughput real-time scheduling.

标题：TempoNet：面向自适应截止时间中心实时调度的松弛量化Transformer引导强化学习调度器
实时调度器必须在严格的计算预算下处理紧迫的截止时间。本文提出TempoNet强化学习调度器，将置换不变Transformer与深度Q值近似相结合。其紧急令牌化器将时间松弛量离散化为可学习的嵌入表示，稳定价值学习并捕捉截止时间临近度。采用具有分块Top-K选择与局部敏感分块机制的延迟感知稀疏注意力堆叠，可在无序任务集上实现近线性扩展和亚毫秒级推理的全局推理。多核映射层通过掩码贪婪选择或可微分匹配，将上下文化Q值分数转换为处理器分配。在工业混合关键性轨迹和大型多处理器环境中的广泛评估表明，相比解析调度器和神经基线方法，该方案在截止时间满足率方面持续提升，同时优化稳定性得到改善。诊断分析包括松弛量化敏感性分析、注意力驱动的策略解释、硬件在环与内核微基准测试，以及带简易运行时缓解机制的压力鲁棒性验证；同时报告了行为克隆预训练带来的样本效率优势，以及与无需修改推理流程的演员-评论员变体的兼容性。这些结果为基于Transformer的高吞吐量实时调度决策建立了实用框架。

The method employs an Urgency Tokenizer to discretize temporal slack into learnable embeddings for stable value learning, along with a latency-aware sparse attention mechanism for efficient global reasoning over task sets. GeM-EA: A Generative and Meta-learning Enhanced Evolutionary Algorithm for Streaming Data-Driven Optimization
Authors: Yue Wu, Yuan-Ting Zhong, Ze-Yuan Ma, Yue-Jiao Gong
First: 2026-04-14T06:18:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T06:18:54+00:00
Comments: accepted by GECCO 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Streaming Data-Driven Optimization (SDDO) problems arise in many applications where data arrive continuously and the optimization environment evolves over time. Concept drift produces non-stationary landscapes, making optimization methods challenging due to outdated models. Existing approaches often rely on simple surrogate combinations or directly injecting solutions, which may cause negative transfer under sudden environmental changes. We propose GeM-EA, a Generative and Meta-learning Enhanced Evolutionary Algorithm for SDDO that unifies meta-learned surrogate adaptation with generative replay for effective evolutionary search. Upon detecting concept drift, a bi-level meta-learning strategy rapidly initializes the surrogate using environment-relevant priors, while a linear residual component captures global trends. A multi-island evolutionary strategy further leverages historical knowledge via generative replay to accelerate optimization. Experimental results on benchmark SDDO problems demonstrate that GeM-EA achieves faster adaptation and improved robustness compared with state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GeM-EA：面向流数据驱动优化的生成式与元学习增强进化算法

RationalRewards: Reasoning Rewards Scale Visual Generation Both Training and Test Time
Authors: Haozhe Wang, Cong Wei, Weiming Ren, Jiaming Liu, Fangzhen Lin, Wenhu Chen
First: 2026-04-13T15:38:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T06:06:15+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://tiger-ai-lab.github.io/RationalRewards/ ; Code, Dataset, Models are released
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Most reward models for visual generation reduce rich human judgments to a single unexplained score, discarding the reasoning that underlies preference. We show that teaching reward models to produce explicit, multi-dimensional critiques before scoring transforms them from passive evaluators into active optimization tools, improving generators in two complementary ways: at training time, structured rationales provide interpretable, fine-grained rewards for reinforcement learning; at test time, a Generate-Critique-Refine loop turns critiques into targeted prompt revisions that improve outputs without any parameter updates. To train such a reward model without costly rationale annotations, we introduce Preference-Anchored Rationalization (PARROT), a principled framework that recovers high-quality rationales from readily available preference data through anchored generation, consistency filtering, and distillation. The resulting model, RationalRewards (8B), achieves state-of-the-art preference prediction among open-source reward models, competitive with Gemini-2.5-Pro, while using 10-20x less training data than comparable baselines. As an RL reward, it consistently improves text-to-image and image-editing generators beyond scalar alternatives. Most strikingly, its test-time critique-and-refine loop matches or exceeds RL-based fine-tuning on several benchmarks, suggesting that structured reasoning can unlock latent capabilities in existing generators that suboptimal prompts fail to elicit.

标题：RationalRewards：推理奖励机制在训练与测试阶段均提升视觉生成效果
现有视觉生成奖励模型大多将丰富的人类评判简化为单一未解释分数，忽略了偏好背后的推理过程。本研究证明，通过训练奖励模型在评分前生成明确的多维度评析，可将其从被动评估工具转化为主动优化工具，从两个互补维度改进生成器：训练阶段，结构化推理为强化学习提供可解释的细粒度奖励；测试阶段，“生成-评析-优化”循环将评析转化为针对性提示词修订，无需参数更新即可提升输出质量。为免去昂贵的人工标注成本，我们提出偏好锚定推理框架（PARROT），通过锚定生成、一致性过滤与蒸馏技术，从现有偏好数据中提取高质量推理依据。最终模型RationalRewards（80亿参数）在开源奖励模型中实现最优偏好预测性能，媲美Gemini-2.5-Pro，且训练数据量仅为同类基线的5%-10%。作为强化学习奖励，该模型在文本到图像生成及图像编辑任务中持续优于传统标量奖励方案。最显著的是，其测试阶段评析优化循环在多项基准测试中达到或超越基于强化学习的微调效果，表明结构化推理能激发现有生成器未被低效提示词调动的潜在能力。

Black-Box Optimization From Small Offline Datasets via Meta Learning with Synthetic Tasks
Authors: Azza Fadhel, The Hung Tran, Trong Nghia Hoang, Jana Doppa
First: 2026-04-14T06:00:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T06:00:30+00:00
Comments: Accepted for Publication at International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of offline black-box optimization, where the goal is to discover optimal designs (e.g., molecules or materials) from past experimental data. A key challenge in this setting is data scarcity: in many scientific applications, only small or poor-quality datasets are available, which severely limits the effectiveness of existing algorithms. Prior work has theoretically and empirically shown that performance of offline optimization algorithms depends on how well the surrogate model captures the optimization bias (i.e., ability to rank input designs correctly), which is challenging to accomplish with limited experimental data. This paper proposes Surrogate Learning with Optimization Bias via Synthetic Task Generation (OptBias), a meta-learning framework that directly tackles data scarcity. OptBias learns a reusable optimization bias by training on synthetic tasks generated from a Gaussian process, and then fine-tunes the surrogate model on the small data for the target task. Across diverse continuous and discrete offline optimization benchmarks, OptBias consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in small data regimes. These results highlight OptBias as a robust and practical solution for offline optimization in realistic small data settings.

标题：基于元学习与合成任务的小样本离线黑盒优化方法
本文研究离线黑盒优化问题，目标是从历史实验数据中发现最优设计（如分子或材料）。该场景的核心挑战在于数据稀缺性：许多科学应用仅能获取少量或低质量数据集，严重制约现有算法的有效性。已有研究从理论与实证表明，离线优化算法的性能取决于代理模型对优化偏差的捕捉能力（即正确排序输入设计的能力），这在有限实验数据下难以实现。本文提出通过合成任务生成学习优化偏差的元学习框架OptBias，直接应对数据稀缺问题。OptBias通过高斯过程生成的合成任务学习可复用的优化偏差，随后针对目标任务在小样本数据上微调代理模型。在连续与离散离线优化基准测试中，OptBias在小数据场景下始终优于现有先进基线方法。这些结果表明OptBias为现实小数据场景下的离线优化提供了鲁棒且实用的解决方案。

Labeled TrustSet Guided: Batch Active Learning with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Guofeng Cui, Yang Liu, Pichao Wang, Hankai Hsu, Xiaohang Sun, Xiang Hao, Zhu Liu
First: 2026-04-14T05:22:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T05:22:59+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Batch active learning (BAL) is a crucial technique for reducing labeling costs and improving data efficiency in training large-scale deep learning models. Traditional BAL methods often rely on metrics like Mahalanobis Distance to balance uncertainty and diversity when selecting data for annotation. However, these methods predominantly focus on the distribution of unlabeled data and fail to leverage feedback from labeled data or the model's performance. To address these limitations, we introduce TrustSet, a novel approach that selects the most informative data from the labeled dataset, ensuring a balanced class distribution to mitigate the long-tail problem. Unlike CoreSet, which focuses on maintaining the overall data distribution, TrustSet optimizes the model's performance by pruning redundant data and using label information to refine the selection process. To extend the benefits of TrustSet to the unlabeled pool, we propose a reinforcement learning (RL)-based sampling policy that approximates the selection of high-quality TrustSet candidates from the unlabeled data. Combining TrustSet and RL, we introduce the Batch Reinforcement Active Learning with TrustSet (BRAL-T) framework. BRAL-T achieves state-of-the-art results across 10 image classification benchmarks and 2 active fine-tuning tasks, demonstrating its effectiveness and efficiency in various domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于标注信任集引导的批量主动学习与强化学习方法
批量主动学习（BAL）是降低标注成本、提升大规模深度学习模型训练数据效率的关键技术。传统BAL方法在选取待标注数据时，常依赖马氏距离等指标来平衡不确定性与多样性，但这些方法主要关注未标注数据的分布，未能有效利用已标注数据的反馈或模型性能信息。为克服这些局限，本文提出TrustSet方法，从已标注数据集中选择信息量最大的样本，并确保类别分布均衡以缓解长尾问题。与侧重维持整体数据分布的CoreSet不同，TrustSet通过剪枝冗余数据并利用标签信息优化选择过程，从而提升模型性能。为将TrustSet的优势扩展至未标注数据池，我们提出一种基于强化学习（RL）的采样策略，近似从未标注数据中筛选高质量的TrustSet候选样本。结合TrustSet与RL，我们构建了基于信任集的批量强化主动学习框架（BRAL-T）。BRAL-T在10个图像分类基准和2个主动微调任务中均取得最先进的结果，验证了其在多领域的高效性与有效性。

Experimental results show that BRAL-T achieves state-of-the-art performance on 10 image classification benchmarks and 2 active fine-tuning tasks, demonstrating effectiveness across domains.

Characterizing higher-order representations through generative diffusion models explains human decoded neurofeedback performance
Authors: Hojjat Azimi Asrari, Megan A. K. Peters
First: 2025-03-18T15:08:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T05:13:11+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Brains construct not only "first-order" representations of the environment but also "higher-order" representations about those representations -- including higher-order uncertainty estimates that guide learning and adaptive behavior. Higher-order expectations about representational uncertainty -- i.e., learned through experience -- may play a key role in guiding behavior and learning, but their characterization remains empirically and theoretically challenging. Here, we introduce the Noise Estimation through Reinforcement-based Diffusion (NERD) model, a novel computational framework that trains denoising diffusion models via reinforcement learning to infer distributions of noise in functional MRI data from a decoded neurofeedback task, where healthy human participants learn to achieve target neural states. We hypothesize that participants accomplish this task by learning about and then minimizing their own representational uncertainty. We test this hypothesis with NERD, which mirrors brain-like unsupervised learning. Our results show that NERD outperforms backpropagation-trained control models in capturing human performance with explanatory power enhanced by clustering learned noise distributions. Importantly, our results also reveal individual differences in expected-uncertainty representations that predict task success, demonstrating NERD's utility as a powerful tool for probing higher-order neural representations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过生成扩散模型表征高阶表征以解释人类解码神经反馈表现
大脑不仅构建环境的'一阶'表征，还构建关于这些表征的'高阶'表征——包括指导学习和适应性行为的高阶不确定性估计。关于表征不确定性的高阶预期（即通过经验习得）可能在指导行为和学习中起关键作用，但其表征在实证和理论上仍具挑战性。本文提出基于强化扩散的噪声估计模型，这是一种通过强化学习训练去噪扩散模型的新型计算框架，用于从解码神经反馈任务的功能磁共振数据中推断噪声分布。该任务要求健康人类参与者学习达成目标神经状态。我们假设参与者通过学习和最小化自身表征不确定性来完成此任务，并使用模拟类脑无监督学习的NERD模型验证该假设。结果表明，NERD在捕捉人类表现方面优于反向传播训练的对照模型，且通过聚类学习到的噪声分布增强了模型解释力。重要的是，研究还揭示了预期不确定性表征的个体差异可预测任务成功率，证明NERD可作为探究高阶神经表征的有效工具。

本研究旨在解决表征高阶神经表征（特别是关于表征不确定性的学习预期）的挑战，这些预期指导适应性行为。作者提出了基于强化学习的噪声估计扩散（NERD）模型，该计算框架利用强化学习训练去噪扩散模型，处理来自解码神经反馈任务的fMRI数据，在该任务中参与者学习控制目标神经状态。实验结果表明，NERD在捕捉人类任务表现方面优于基于反向传播训练的模型，其解释能力通过聚类学习到的噪声分布得到增强，并且揭示了预期不确定性表征的个体差异可预测任务成功率，从而展示了其作为探究高阶神经表征的有力工具的实用性。
Improved particle swarm optimization algorithm: multi-target trajectory optimization for swarm drones
Authors: Minze Li, Wei Zhao, Ran Chen, Mingqiang Wei
First: 2025-07-18T04:31:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T05:04:10+00:00
Comments: New experiments have revealed systematic errors in the original data
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-time trajectory planning for unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) in dynamic environments remains a key challenge due to high computational demands and the need for fast, adaptive responses. Traditional Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO) methods, while effective for offline planning, often struggle with premature convergence and latency in real-time scenarios. To overcome these limitations, we propose PE-PSO, an enhanced PSO-based online trajectory planner. The method introduces a persistent exploration mechanism to preserve swarm diversity and an entropy-based parameter adjustment strategy to dynamically adapt optimization behavior. UAV trajectories are modeled using B-spline curves, which ensure path smoothness while reducing optimization complexity. To extend this capability to UAV swarms, we develop a multi-agent framework that combines genetic algorithm (GA)-based task allocation with distributed PE-PSO, supporting scalable and coordinated trajectory generation. The distributed architecture allows for parallel computation and decentralized control, enabling effective cooperation among agents while maintaining real-time performance. Comprehensive simulations demonstrate that the proposed framework outperforms conventional PSO and other swarm-based planners across several metrics, including trajectory quality, energy efficiency, obstacle avoidance, and computation time. These results confirm the effectiveness and applicability of PE-PSO in real-time multi-UAV operations under complex environmental conditions.

标题：改进粒子群优化算法：集群无人机多目标轨迹优化
动态环境中无人机实时轨迹规划因高计算需求和快速自适应响应的要求，仍是关键挑战。传统粒子群优化方法虽适用于离线规划，但在实时场景中常面临早熟收敛和延迟问题。为突破这些局限，我们提出PE-PSO——一种增强型基于PSO的在线轨迹规划器。该方法引入持续探索机制以保持群体多样性，并采用基于熵的参数调整策略动态优化行为。通过B样条曲线建模无人机轨迹，在保证路径平滑性的同时降低优化复杂度。为扩展至无人机集群，我们开发了结合遗传算法任务分配与分布式PE-PSO的多智能体框架，支持可扩展的协同轨迹生成。分布式架构支持并行计算与去中心化控制，在保持实时性能的同时实现智能体间有效协作。综合仿真表明，该框架在轨迹质量、能效、避障及计算时间等多项指标上优于传统PSO及其他集群规划器，验证了PE-PSO在复杂环境条件下实时多无人机操作中的有效性与适用性。

Quantile Q-Learning: Revisiting Offline Extreme Q-Learning with Quantile Regression
Authors: Xinming Gao, Shangzhe Li, Yujin Cai, Wenwu Yu
First: 2025-11-15T01:10:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T04:29:16+00:00
Comments: Accepted by TMLR 2026; Code available at: https://github.com/yunqianevergarden/Quantile-Q-Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) enables policy learning from fixed datasets without further environment interaction, making it particularly valuable in high-risk or costly domains. Extreme $Q$-Learning (XQL) is a recent offline RL method that models Bellman errors using the Extreme Value Theorem, yielding strong empirical performance. However, XQL and its stabilized variant MXQL suffer from notable limitations: both require extensive hyperparameter tuning specific to each dataset and domain, and also exhibit instability during training. To address these issues, we proposed a principled method to estimate the temperature coefficient $β$ via quantile regression under mild assumptions. To further improve training stability, we introduce a value regularization technique with mild generalization, inspired by recent advances in constrained value learning. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm achieves competitive or superior performance across a range of benchmark tasks, including D4RL and NeoRL2, while maintaining stable training dynamics and using a consistent set of hyperparameters across all datasets and domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分位数Q学习：基于分位数回归的离线极端Q学习再探
离线强化学习（RL）允许从固定数据集中学习策略而无需与环境进一步交互，这使其在高风险或高成本领域具有重要价值。极端Q学习（XQL）是一种近期提出的离线RL方法，它利用极值定理对贝尔曼误差进行建模，取得了显著的实证性能。然而，XQL及其稳定变体MXQL存在明显局限：两者均需针对每个数据集和领域进行大量超参数调优，且在训练过程中表现出不稳定性。为解决这些问题，我们提出了一种基于温和假设、通过分位数回归估计温度系数β的原则性方法。为进一步提升训练稳定性，受约束值学习最新进展的启发，我们引入了一种具有温和泛化性的值正则化技术。实验结果表明，所提算法在包括D4RL和NeoRL2在内的一系列基准任务中取得了竞争性或更优的性能，同时保持了稳定的训练动态，并在所有数据集和领域中使用了一致的超参数集。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of Extreme Q-Learning (XQL) and its stabilized variant MXQL in offline reinforcement learning, which require extensive, dataset-specific hyperparameter tuning and suffer from training instability. The proposed method, Quantile Q-Learning, introduces a principled approach to estimate the critical temperature coefficient via quantile regression under mild assumptions and incorporates a value regularization technique to enhance stability. Experimental results on benchmark datasets like D4RL and NeoRL2 show that the algorithm achieves competitive or superior performance while maintaining stable training and using a consistent hyperparameter set across all tasks.
本文针对离线强化学习中极端Q学习（XQL）及其稳定变体MXQL的局限性进行了改进，这些方法需要针对每个数据集进行大量超参数调整且训练不稳定。提出的方法——分位数Q学习，通过分位数回归在温和假设下原则性地估计温度系数，并引入值正则化技术以提高稳定性。在D4RL和NeoRL2等基准任务上的实验结果表明，该算法在保持训练稳定的同时，使用一致的超参数集实现了竞争性或更优的性能。
Hard Negative Sample-Augmented DPO Post-Training for Small Language Models
Authors: Haocheng Lu, Minjun Zhu, Henry Yu
First: 2025-12-17T06:15:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T04:23:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) continue to struggle with mathematical reasoning, and common post-training pipelines often reduce each generated solution to a binary outcome: correct or incorrect. This perspective is limiting in practice, as failures in chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning are frequently structured; solutions may appear convincing while containing subtle logical, algebraic, or numerical flaws. Meanwhile, reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) variants that rely on large reward models or LLM-as-a-judge signals are often expensive, difficult to scale, and unstable to iterate. We propose a lightweight and pragmatic post-training pipeline that targets such structured errors under realistic compute budgets. Starting from supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on MetaMathQA-style CoT data, we introduce a compact MathVerifier that decomposes a candidate solution into a six-dimensional error profile and aggregates it into interpretable wrongness and absurdity scores. These verifier signals serve two roles: (i) mining hard negatives that are near-correct yet structurally flawed, and (ii) defining per-sample importance weights that emphasize the most informative preference pairs. We integrate both into an offline Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) objective via a verifier-guided weighted formulation. Experiments on a 1.5B-parameter Qwen2.5 model show that verifier-guided, weighted DPO yields more targeted improvements than vanilla SFT and unweighted DPO, particularly on problems where solutions are numerically close to correct but logically inconsistent, while avoiding the overhead of training large reward models or relying on external judges.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向小语言模型的困难负样本增强DPO后训练
大语言模型在数学推理任务上仍面临挑战，常见的后训练流程常将生成结果简化为二元判断（正确/错误）。这种视角在实践中具有局限性，因为思维链推理的失败往往具有结构性：看似合理的解答可能包含细微的逻辑、代数或数值缺陷。同时，依赖大型奖励模型或LLM评判信号的RLHF变体通常成本高昂、难以扩展且迭代不稳定。我们提出一种轻量级、实用的后训练流程，旨在实际计算预算下针对此类结构性错误。该方法从基于MetaMathQA式思维链数据的监督微调出发，引入一个紧凑的数学验证器，将候选解分解为六维错误画像并聚合为可解释的错误度与荒谬度分数。该验证器信号发挥双重作用：(1)挖掘接近正确但存在结构性缺陷的困难负样本；(2)定义强调最具信息量偏好对的样本级重要性权重。我们通过验证器引导的加权公式将两者整合至离线直接偏好优化目标中。在15亿参数的Qwen2.5模型上的实验表明，验证器引导的加权DPO相比原始SFT和无加权DPO能带来更具针对性的性能提升——尤其在数值接近正确但逻辑不一致的问题上表现显著，同时避免了训练大型奖励模型或依赖外部评判的开销。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of binary correctness judgments and the high cost of traditional RLHF methods for mathematical reasoning, this paper proposes a lightweight post-training pipeline that targets structured errors in chain-of-thought solutions. The method involves supervised fine-tuning on CoT data, then using a compact MathVerifier to decompose solutions into error profiles and compute wrongness/absurdity scores; these scores are used to mine hard negative samples and weight preference pairs for a verifier-guided, weighted Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) objective. Experimental results on a 1.5B-parameter model demonstrate that this approach yields more targeted improvements over vanilla SFT and unweighted DPO, especially on problems with numerically close but logically flawed solutions, without the overhead of large reward models or external judges.
针对数学推理中二元正确性判断的局限性以及传统RLHF方法的高成本，本文提出了一种轻量级后训练流程，旨在解决思维链推理中的结构化错误。该方法首先在CoT数据上进行监督微调，然后使用一个紧凑的MathVerifier将候选解分解为六维错误特征并计算错误与荒谬分数；这些分数用于挖掘困难负样本并为偏好对分配权重，从而构建一个验证器引导的加权直接偏好优化目标。在15亿参数模型上的实验结果表明，该方法相比普通监督微调和未加权的DPO能带来更具针对性的性能提升，特别是在数值接近正确但逻辑不一致的问题上，同时避免了训练大型奖励模型或依赖外部评判的开销。
ARGen: Affect-Reinforced Generative Augmentation towards Vision-based Dynamic Emotion Perception
Authors: Huanzhen Wang, Ziheng Zhou, Jiaqi Song, Li He, Yunshi Lan, Yan Wang, Wenqiang Zhang
First: 2026-04-14T04:05:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T04:05:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dynamic facial expression recognition in the wild remains challenging due to data scarcity and long-tail distributions, which hinder models from effectively learning the temporal dynamics of scarce emotions. To address these limitations, we propose ARGen, an Affect-Reinforced Generative Augmentation Framework that enables data-adaptive dynamic expression generation for robust emotion perception. ARGen operates in two stages: Affective Semantic Injection (ASI) and Adaptive Reinforcement Diffusion (ARD). The ASI stage establishes affective knowledge alignment through facial Action Units and employs a retrieval-augmented prompt generation strategy to synthesize consistent and fine-grained affective descriptions via large-scale visual-language models, thereby injecting interpretable emotional priors into the generation process. The ARD stage integrates text-conditioned image-to-video diffusion with reinforcement learning, introducing inter-frame conditional guidance and a multi-objective reward function to jointly optimize expression naturalness, facial integrity, and generative efficiency. Extensive experiments on both generation and recognition tasks verify that ARGen substantially enhances synthesis fidelity and improves recognition performance, establishing an interpretable and generalizable generative augmentation paradigm for vision-based affective computing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARGen：面向视觉动态情感感知的情感增强生成式数据增强框架
由于数据稀缺和长尾分布，野外动态面部表情识别仍面临挑战，这阻碍了模型有效学习稀缺情感的时间动态特性。为应对这些局限，我们提出ARGen——一种情感增强生成式数据增强框架，能够通过数据自适应的动态表情生成实现鲁棒的情感感知。ARGen包含两个阶段：情感语义注入（ASI）和自适应增强扩散（ARD）。ASI阶段通过面部动作单元建立情感知识对齐，并采用检索增强的提示生成策略，借助大规模视觉-语言模型合成一致且细粒度的情感描述，从而将可解释的情感先验注入生成过程。ARD阶段将文本条件化的图像到视频扩散与强化学习相结合，引入帧间条件引导和多目标奖励函数，共同优化表情自然度、面部完整性和生成效率。在生成与识别任务上的大量实验表明，ARGen显著提升了合成保真度并改善了识别性能，为基于视觉的情感计算建立了可解释、可泛化的生成式增强范式。

Experimental results demonstrate that ARGen significantly improves synthesis fidelity and boosts recognition performance, offering an interpretable and generalizable augmentation paradigm for vision-based affective computing.

The Stackelberg Speaker: Optimizing Persuasive Communication in Social Deduction Games
Authors: Zhang Zheng, Deheng Ye, Peilin Zhao, Hao Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-10-10T07:33:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T04:05:00+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have shown remarkable progress in social deduction games (SDGs). However, existing approaches primarily focus on information processing and strategy selection, overlooking the significance of persuasive communication in influencing other players' beliefs and responses. In SDGs, success depends not only on making correct deductions but on convincing others to response in alignment with one's intent. To address this limitation, we formalize turn-based dialogue in SDGs as a Stackelberg competition, where the current player acts as the leader who strategically influences the follower's response. Building on this theoretical foundation, we propose a reinforcement learning framework that trains agents to optimize utterances for persuasive impact. Through comprehensive experiments across three diverse SDGs, we demonstrate that our agents significantly outperform baselines. This work represents a significant step toward developing AI agents capable of strategic social influence, with implications extending to scenarios requiring persuasive communication. Our code and data are available at https://3dagentworld.github.io/leader_follower.
中文标题/摘要
标题：斯塔克尔伯格发言者：社交推理游戏中优化说服性沟通的策略
大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在社交推理游戏（SDGs）中已展现出显著进展。然而，现有方法主要关注信息处理和策略选择，忽视了说服性沟通在影响其他玩家信念与反应方面的重要性。在SDGs中，成功不仅取决于做出正确推理，更在于说服他人按照自身意图行动。为弥补这一局限，我们将SDGs中的回合制对话形式化为斯塔克尔伯格竞争模型，当前玩家作为领导者策略性地影响跟随者的反应。基于此理论基础，我们提出了一个强化学习框架，训练智能体优化话语以实现说服效果。通过在三种不同类型的SDGs中进行全面实验，我们证明所提出的智能体显著优于基线模型。这项工作标志着向开发具备战略性社会影响力的人工智能智能体迈出了重要一步，其应用可延伸至需要说服性沟通的多种场景。代码与数据公开于https://3dagentworld.github.io/leader_follower。

The authors formalize turn-based dialogue as a Stackelberg competition, where the current player strategically influences followers, and propose a reinforcement learning framework to train agents in optimizing persuasive utterances. Experimental results across three diverse games show that these agents significantly outperform baseline methods, advancing AI capabilities in strategic social influence for scenarios requiring persuasion.
本文针对现有大型语言模型代理在社交推理游戏中侧重于信息处理而忽视说服性沟通的局限性，提出将回合制对话形式化为斯塔克尔伯格竞争，其中当前玩家作为领导者战略性地影响跟随者。基于此理论，作者设计了一个强化学习框架来训练代理优化说服性话语。在三个不同游戏中的综合实验表明，该代理显著优于基线方法，推动了AI在需要说服性沟通场景中战略社会影响能力的发展。
EvoNash-MARL: A Closed-Loop Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Framework for Medium-Horizon Equity Allocation
Authors: Chongliu Jia, Yi Luo, Sipeng Han, Pengwei Li, Jie Ding, Youshuang Hu, Yimiao Qian, Qiya Wang
First: 2026-04-13T02:24:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T03:47:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Medium- to long-horizon equity allocation is challenging due to weak predictive structure, non-stationary market regimes, and the degradation of signals under realistic trading constraints. Conventional approaches often rely on single predictors or loosely coupled pipelines, which limit robustness under distributional shift. This paper proposes EvoNash-MARL, a closed-loop framework that integrates reinforcement learning with population-based policy optimization and execution-aware selection to improve robustness in medium- to long-horizon allocation. The framework combines multi-agent policy populations, game-theoretic aggregation, and constraint-aware validation within a unified walk-forward design. Under a 120-window walk-forward protocol, the final configuration achieves the highest robust score among internal baselines. On out-of-sample data from 2014 to 2024, it delivers a 19.6% annualized return, compared to 11.7% for SPY, and remains stable under extended evaluation through 2026. While the framework demonstrates consistent performance under realistic constraints and across market settings, strong global statistical significance is not established under White's Reality Check (WRC) and SPA-lite tests. The results therefore provide evidence of improved robustness rather than definitive proof of superior market timing performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EvoNash-MARL：面向中周期股权配置的闭环多智能体强化学习框架
中长周期股权配置因预测结构薄弱、市场机制非平稳及实际交易约束下信号衰减而面临挑战。传统方法常依赖单一预测器或松散耦合的流程，限制了分布偏移下的鲁棒性。本文提出EvoNash-MARL闭环框架，通过集成强化学习与基于群体的策略优化及执行感知选择，提升中长周期配置的鲁棒性。该框架在统一的前向滚动设计中融合多智能体策略群体、博弈论聚合与约束感知验证机制。在120期前向滚动协议下，最终配置在内部基线中取得最高鲁棒性评分。在2014-2024年样本外数据上实现19.6%年化收益（同期SPY为11.7%），且截至2026年的扩展评估中保持稳定。虽然框架在实际约束与多市场环境下表现一致，但怀特现实检验与SPA-lite测试未确立全局统计显著性。因此，结果证明了鲁棒性提升，而非市场择时能力优越的确定性证据。

The paper addresses the challenges of medium- to long-horizon equity allocation, such as weak predictive structure and non-stationary markets, by proposing EvoNash-MARL, a closed-loop multi-agent reinforcement learning framework. This method integrates population-based policy optimization with game-theoretic aggregation and execution-aware selection within a walk-forward design to enhance robustness under distributional shifts. Experimental results under a 120-window walk-forward protocol show the framework achieves the highest robust score among baselines, delivering a 19.6% annualized return on out-of-sample data from 2014 to 2024 compared to SPY's 11.7%, with stable performance through 2026, though statistical significance tests like White's Reality Check do not confirm superior market timing.
本文针对中长周期股权配置中预测结构弱、市场机制非平稳等挑战，提出了EvoNash-MARL，一种闭环多智能体强化学习框架。该方法在滚动前向设计中整合了基于群体的策略优化、博弈论聚合和执行感知选择，以提高分布变化下的鲁棒性。在120窗口滚动前向协议下的实验结果表明，该框架在内部基线中获得了最高的鲁棒分数，在2014年至2024年的样本外数据上实现了19.6%的年化收益，优于SPY的11.7%，且性能稳定至2026年，但怀特现实检验等统计测试未证实其市场择时能力的显著优越性。
MolMem: Memory-Augmented Agentic Reinforcement Learning for Sample-Efficient Molecular Optimization
Authors: Ziqing Wang, Yibo Wen, Abhishek Pandy, Han Liu, Kaize Ding
First: 2026-04-14T03:24:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T03:24:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In drug discovery, molecular optimization aims to iteratively refine a lead compound to improve molecular properties while preserving structural similarity to the original molecule. However, each oracle evaluation is expensive, making sample efficiency a key challenge for existing methods under a limited oracle budget. Trial-and-error approaches require many oracle calls, while methods that leverage external knowledge tend to reuse familiar templates and struggle on challenging objectives. A key missing piece is long-term memory that can ground decisions and provide reusable insights for future optimizations. To address this, we present MolMem (\textbf{Mol}ecular optimization with \textbf{Mem}ory), a multi-turn agentic reinforcement learning (RL) framework with a dual-memory system. Specifically, MolMem uses Static Exemplar Memory to retrieve relevant exemplars for cold-start grounding, and Evolving Skill Memory to distill successful trajectories into reusable strategies. Built on this memory-augmented formulation, we train the policy with dense step-wise rewards, turning costly rollouts into long-term knowledge that improves future optimization. Extensive experiments show that MolMem achieves 90\% success on single-property tasks (1.5$\times$ over the best baseline) and 52\% on multi-property tasks using only 500 oracle calls. Our code is available at https://github.com/REAL-Lab-NU/MolMem.

标题：MolMem：基于记忆增强的智能体强化学习实现样本高效分子优化
在药物发现中，分子优化旨在迭代改进先导化合物以提升分子性质，同时保持与原始分子的结构相似性。然而，每次评估成本高昂，使得样本效率成为现有方法在有限评估预算下的关键挑战。试错法需要大量评估调用，而利用外部知识的方法倾向于重复使用常见模板，在复杂目标上表现不佳。现有方法缺乏能够支撑决策并为未来优化提供可复用见解的长期记忆机制。为此，我们提出MolMem（基于记忆的分子优化框架），这是一种配备双记忆系统的多轮智能体强化学习框架。具体而言，MolMem利用静态范例记忆检索相关范例实现冷启动支撑，并通过演化技能记忆将成功轨迹提炼为可复用策略。基于此记忆增强架构，我们采用密集步进奖励训练策略，将高成本模拟转化为可提升未来优化效果的长期知识。大量实验表明，MolMem在单属性任务上达到90%成功率（较最佳基线提升1.5倍），在多属性任务上仅用500次评估调用即实现52%成功率。代码已开源：https://github.com/REAL-Lab-NU/MolMem。

Automated co-design of high-performance thermodynamic cycles via graph-based hierarchical reinforcement learning
Authors: Wenqing Li, Xu Feng, Peixue Jiang, Yinhai Zhu
First: 2026-04-14T02:22:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T02:22:37+00:00
Comments: 21 pages,8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Thermodynamic cycles are pivotal in determining the efficacy of energy conversion systems. Traditional design methodologies, which rely on expert knowledge or exhaustive enumeration, are inefficient and lack scalability, thereby constraining the discovery of high-performance cycles. In this study, we introduce a graph-based hierarchical reinforcement learning approach for the co-design of structure parameters in thermodynamic cycles. These cycles are encoded as graphs, with components and connections depicted as nodes and edges, adhering to grammatical constraints. A deep learning-based thermophysical surrogate facilitates stable graph decoding and the simultaneous resolution of global parameters. Building on this foundation, we develop a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework wherein a high-level manager explores structural evolution and proposes candidate configurations, whereas a low-level worker optimizes parameters and provides performance rewards to steer the search towards high-performance regions. By integrating graph representation, thermophysical surrogate, and manager-worker learning, this method establishes a fully automated pipeline for encoding, decoding, and co-optimization. Using heat pump and heat engine cycles as case studies, the results demonstrate that the proposed method not only replicates classical cycle configurations but also identifies 18 and 21 novel heat pump and heat engine cycles, respectively. Relative to classical cycles, the novel configurations exhibit performance improvements of 4.6% and 133.3%, respectively, surpassing the traditional designs. This method effectively balances efficiency with broad applicability, providing a practical and scalable intelligent alternative to expert-driven thermodynamic cycle design.

热力学循环对能量转换系统的效能至关重要。传统设计方法依赖专家知识或穷举枚举，效率低下且缺乏可扩展性，限制了高性能循环的发现。本研究提出一种基于图结构的分层强化学习方法，用于热力学循环的结构参数协同设计。循环被编码为图，组件与连接分别表示为节点和边，并遵循语法约束。基于深度学习的热物理代理模型支持稳定的图解码与全局参数同步求解。在此基础上，构建分层强化学习框架：高层管理器探索结构演化并提出候选配置，低层工作器优化参数并提供性能奖励，引导搜索朝向高性能区域。通过整合图表示、热物理代理模型及管理器-工作器学习机制，该方法建立了编码、解码与协同优化的全自动流程。以热泵和热引擎循环为例，结果表明该方法不仅能复现经典循环构型，还分别发现了18种新型热泵循环和21种新型热引擎循环。相较于经典循环，新构型的性能分别提升4.6%和133.3%，超越传统设计。该方法在效率与普适性间取得平衡，为专家驱动的热力学循环设计提供了实用、可扩展的智能替代方案。

RLGT: A reinforcement learning framework for extremal graph theory
Authors: Ivan Damnjanović, Uroš Milivojević, Irena Đorđević, Dragan Stevanović
First: 2026-02-19T11:25:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T00:51:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a subfield of machine learning that focuses on developing models that can autonomously learn optimal decision-making strategies over time. In a recent pioneering paper, Wagner demonstrated how the Deep Cross-Entropy RL method can be applied to tackle various problems from extremal graph theory by reformulating them as combinatorial optimization problems. Subsequently, many researchers became interested in refining and extending the framework introduced by Wagner, thereby creating various RL environments specialized for graph theory. Moreover, a number of problems from extremal graph theory were solved through the use of RL. In particular, several inequalities concerning the Laplacian spectral radius of graphs were refuted, new lower bounds were obtained for certain Ramsey numbers, and contributions were made to the Turán-type extremal problem in which the forbidden structures are cycles of length three and four. Here, we present Reinforcement Learning for Graph Theory (RLGT), a novel RL framework that systematizes the previous work and provides support for both undirected and directed graphs, with or without loops, and with an arbitrary number of edge colors. The framework efficiently represents graphs and aims to facilitate future RL-based research in extremal graph theory through optimized computational performance and a clean and modular design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLGT：极值图论中的强化学习框架
强化学习是机器学习的一个子领域，专注于开发能够随时间自主习得最优决策策略的模型。在近期一篇开创性论文中，Wagner展示了如何通过将极值图论中的各类问题重构为组合优化问题，应用深度交叉熵强化学习方法加以解决。随后，众多研究者致力于改进和扩展Wagner提出的框架，由此创建了多种专用于图论的强化学习环境。此外，已有若干极值图论问题借助强化学习得以解决：具体包括证伪了若干关于图谱拉普拉斯半径的不等式、获得了某些拉姆齐数的新下界，并对禁止结构为三阶与四阶环的图兰型极值问题作出了贡献。本文提出“图论强化学习”框架，该系统化整合了先前工作，支持含或不含自环的无向图与有向图，并可处理任意边着色数量。该框架通过高效图表示、优化计算性能及清晰模块化设计，旨在为极值图论领域基于强化学习的未来研究提供支持。

本研究的动机在于系统化和扩展先前将强化学习应用于极值图论问题（通常涉及组合优化）的研究。方法上提出了RLGT这一新颖的强化学习框架，支持无向图、有向图、自环和多边色，采用高效的图表示和模块化设计以优化计算性能。主要实验结果基于早期应用，包括反驳了若干关于拉普拉斯谱半径的不等式，为特定拉姆齐数建立了新的下界，并对涉及禁止三阶和四阶循环的Turán型极值问题做出了贡献。
PubSwap: Public-Data Off-Policy Coordination for Federated RLVR
Authors: Anupam Nayak, Baris Askin, Muhammed Ustaomeroglu, Carlee Joe-Wong, Gauri Joshi
First: 2026-04-14T00:35:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T00:35:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reasoning post-training with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) is typically studied in centralized settings, yet many realistic applications involve decentralized private data distributed across organizations. Federated training is a natural solution, but scaling RLVR in this regime is challenging: full-model synchronization is expensive, and performing many local steps can cause severe client drift under heterogeneous data. We propose a federated RLVR framework that combines LoRA-based local adaptation with public-data-based off-policy steps to improve both communication efficiency and cross-client coordination. In particular, a small shared public dataset is used to periodically exchange and reuse response-level training signals across organizations, providing a lightweight anchor toward a more globally aligned objective without exposing private data. Our method selectively replaces locally incorrect responses with globally correct ones during public-data steps, thereby keeping training closer to the local policy while still benefiting from cross-client coordination. Across mathematical and medical reasoning benchmarks and models, our method consistently improves over standard baselines. Our results highlight a simple and effective recipe for federated reasoning post-training: combining low-rank communication with limited public-data coordination.

标题：PubSwap：面向联邦RLVR的公共数据离策略协调方法
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）的后训练推理通常集中于集中式场景，然而实际应用常涉及跨机构分布的分散式私有数据。联邦训练是自然解决方案，但在此场景下扩展RLVR面临挑战：全模型同步成本高昂，且异构数据下的多步本地训练易引发严重的客户端漂移。本文提出一种联邦RLVR框架，结合基于LoRA的本地适配与基于公共数据的离策略训练，以提升通信效率与跨客户端协调能力。该框架利用小型共享公共数据集，周期性地在机构间交换和复用响应级训练信号，通过轻量级锚定机制实现全局目标对齐，同时保护私有数据。在公共数据训练阶段，本方法选择性地用全局正确响应替换本地错误响应，使训练既贴近本地策略又受益于跨客户端协调。在数学与医学推理基准测试及多种模型上的实验表明，本方法持续优于基线模型。研究结果为联邦后训练推理提供了一种简洁有效的方案：将低秩通信与有限公共数据协调相结合。

Mixed-Density Diffuser: Efficient Planning with Non-Uniform Temporal Resolution
Authors: Crimson Stambaugh, Rajesh P. N. Rao
First: 2025-10-27T05:45:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T00:17:25+00:00
Comments: European Symposium on Artificial Neural Networks, Computational Intelligence and Machine Learning (ESANN, 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies demonstrate that diffusion planners benefit from sparse-step planning over single-step planning. Training models to skip steps in their trajectories helps capture long-term dependencies without additional memory or computational cost. However, predicting excessively sparse plans degrades performance. We hypothesize this temporal density threshold is non-uniform across a planning horizon and that certain parts of a predicted trajectory should be more densely generated. We propose Mixed-Density Diffuser (MDD), a diffusion planner where the densities throughout the horizon are tunable hyperparameters. We show that MDD surpasses the SOTA Diffusion Veteran (DV) framework across the Maze2D, Franka Kitchen, and Antmaze Datasets for Deep Data-Driven Reinforcement Learning (D4RL) task domains, achieving a new SOTA on the D4RL benchmark.
中文标题/摘要

近期研究表明，扩散规划器通过稀疏步长规划优于单步规划。训练模型跳过轨迹中的步骤有助于捕捉长期依赖关系，且无需额外内存或计算成本。然而，预测过度稀疏的规划会降低性能。我们假设时间密度阈值在规划时域内是非均匀的，且预测轨迹的某些部分应更密集生成。本文提出混合密度扩散器（MDD），一种扩散规划器，其整个时域的密度可作为可调超参数。实验表明，在Maze2D、Franka Kitchen和Antmaze数据集上，MDD在深度数据驱动强化学习（D4RL）任务领域均超越当前最优的扩散规划框架（DV），并在D4RL基准测试中创造了新的最优性能。

本文的动机源于观察到稀疏步扩散规划虽能通过捕捉长期依赖提高效率，但均匀稀疏的预测会降低性能，这表明在规划时域内需要非均匀的时间分辨率。方法上提出了混合密度扩散器（MDD），这是一种基于扩散的规划器，通过可调超参数控制轨迹不同点的生成步密度，从而在需要时实现更精细的规划。实验结果表明，MDD在D4RL基准的Maze2D、Franka Kitchen和Antmaze数据集上超越了最先进的Diffusion Veteran框架，在这些任务领域建立了新的SOTA性能。
Robust Optimization for Mitigating Reward Hacking with Correlated Proxies
Authors: Zixuan Liu, Xiaolin Sun, Zizhan Zheng
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-13T21:47:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T21:47:49+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Designing robust reinforcement learning (RL) agents in the presence of imperfect reward signals remains a core challenge. In practice, agents are often trained with proxy rewards that only approximate the true objective, leaving them vulnerable to reward hacking, where high proxy returns arise from unintended or exploitative behaviors. Recent work formalizes this issue using r-correlation between proxy and true rewards, but existing methods like occupancy-regularized policy optimization (ORPO) optimize against a fixed proxy and do not provide strong guarantees against broader classes of correlated proxies. In this work, we formulate reward hacking as a robust policy optimization problem over the space of all r-correlated proxy rewards. We derive a tractable max-min formulation, where the agent maximizes performance under the worst-case proxy consistent with the correlation constraint. We further show that when the reward is a linear function of known features, our approach can be adapted to incorporate this prior knowledge, yielding both improved policies and interpretable worst-case rewards. Experiments across several environments show that our algorithms consistently outperform ORPO in worst-case returns, and offer improved robustness and stability across different levels of proxy-true reward correlation. These results show that our approach provides both robustness and transparency in settings where reward design is inherently uncertain. The code is available at https://github.com/ZixuanLiu4869/reward_hacking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于相关代理的鲁棒优化缓解奖励黑客攻击
在奖励信号不完美的环境下设计鲁棒的强化学习（RL）智能体仍是一个核心挑战。实践中，智能体常使用仅近似真实目标的代理奖励进行训练，使其易受奖励黑客攻击，即高代理回报源于非预期或利用性行为。近期研究通过代理奖励与真实奖励间的r-相关性形式化该问题，但现有方法（如占用正则化策略优化ORPO）仅针对固定代理进行优化，无法对更广泛的相关代理类别提供强保证。本文提出将奖励黑客问题形式化为在所有r-相关代理奖励空间上的鲁棒策略优化问题，推导出可处理的极大极小化公式，使智能体在相关性约束下针对最坏情况代理最大化性能。进一步证明当奖励为已知特征的线性函数时，该方法可结合先验知识，同时提升策略性能并生成可解释的最坏情况奖励。多环境实验表明，所提算法在最坏情况回报上持续优于ORPO，并在不同代理-真实奖励相关性水平下展现出更强的鲁棒性与稳定性。这些结果证明，在奖励设计存在固有不确定性的场景中，本方法兼具鲁棒性与可解释性。代码发布于https://github.com/ZixuanLiu4869/reward_hacking。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reward hacking in reinforcement learning, where agents exploit imperfect proxy rewards that only approximate the true objective. The authors formulate reward hacking as a robust policy optimization problem over all r-correlated proxy rewards, proposing a tractable max-min approach where the agent maximizes performance under the worst-case proxy consistent with the correlation constraint. Experimental results across several environments demonstrate that their algorithms consistently outperform existing methods like occupancy-regularized policy optimization in worst-case returns, offering improved robustness and stability across different levels of proxy-true reward correlation.
本文针对强化学习中奖励黑客攻击的挑战展开研究，即智能体利用仅近似真实目标的不完美代理奖励进行不当优化。作者将奖励黑客攻击形式化为一个在所有r相关代理奖励空间上的鲁棒策略优化问题，提出了一种可处理的最大最小方法，使智能体在符合相关性约束的最坏情况代理奖励下最大化性能。在多个环境中的实验结果表明，其算法在最坏情况回报上持续优于现有方法（如占用正则化策略优化），并在不同代理与真实奖励相关性水平下提供了更好的鲁棒性和稳定性。
Iterative Compositional Data Generation for Robot Control
Authors: Anh-Quan Pham, Marcel Hussing, Shubhankar P. Patankar, Dani S. Bassett, Jorge Mendez-Mendez, Eric Eaton
First: 2025-12-11T18:20:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T21:38:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Collecting robotic manipulation data is expensive, making it impractical to acquire demonstrations for the combinatorially large space of tasks that arise in multi-object, multi-robot, and multi-environment settings. While recent generative models can synthesize useful data for individual tasks, they do not exploit the compositional structure of robotic domains and struggle to generalize to unseen task combinations. We propose a semantic compositional diffusion transformer that factorizes transitions into robot-, object-, obstacle-, and objective-specific components and learns their interactions through attention. Once trained on a limited subset of tasks, we show that our model can zero-shot generate high-quality transitions from which we can learn control policies for unseen task combinations. Then, we introduce an iterative self-improvement procedure in which synthetic data is validated via offline reinforcement learning and incorporated into subsequent training rounds. Our approach substantially improves zero-shot performance over monolithic and hard-coded compositional baselines, ultimately solving nearly all held-out tasks and demonstrating the emergence of meaningful compositional structure in the learned representations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器人控制的迭代组合数据生成方法
机器人操作数据采集成本高昂，难以覆盖多物体、多机器人、多环境场景中组合爆炸的任务空间。现有生成模型虽能为单一任务合成数据，却未利用机器人领域的组合结构，难以泛化至未见任务组合。我们提出一种语义组合扩散变换器，将状态转移分解为机器人、物体、障碍物和目标等组件，并通过注意力机制学习其交互关系。在有限任务子集上训练后，该模型能零样本生成高质量状态转移数据，进而学习未见任务组合的控制策略。我们还引入迭代自改进流程：通过离线强化学习验证合成数据，并将其纳入后续训练轮次。相比整体式和硬编码组合基线，本方法显著提升零样本性能，最终解决几乎所有预留任务，并在学习表征中呈现出有意义的组合结构。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high cost of collecting robotic manipulation data for the vast space of multi-object, multi-robot tasks by proposing a semantic compositional diffusion transformer that factorizes transitions into components like robots and objects, learning their interactions via attention. This model, trained on a limited task subset, can zero-shot generate high-quality transitions for unseen task combinations, enabling control policy learning, and an iterative self-improvement procedure validates synthetic data via offline reinforcement learning to enhance training. Experimental results show substantial zero-shot performance gains over baselines, solving nearly all held-out tasks and revealing meaningful compositional structure in learned representations.
该论文针对多物体、多机器人任务空间中收集机器人操作数据成本高昂的问题，提出了一种语义组合扩散变换器，将状态转移分解为机器人、物体等组件，并通过注意力机制学习其交互。该模型在有限任务子集上训练后，能零样本生成高质量的状态转移以学习未见任务组合的控制策略，并引入迭代自改进过程，通过离线强化学习验证合成数据以增强训练。实验结果表明，其零样本性能大幅超越基线方法，解决了几乎所有保留任务，并在学习表征中展现出有意义的组合结构。
